§ 1

p.1, l.1

(p.1, l.1)|| śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ ||

|| śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ ||

p.1, l.2

  • (p.1, l.2)praṇamya śāradāṃ devīṃ divyavijñānaśālinīm | (p.1, l.3)vacmi cetovinodārthamuddhāraṃ kīrasaṃmateḥ || 1.1 (= 1) ||
praṇamya śāradāṃ devīṃ divyavijñānaśālinīm | vacmi cetovinodārthamuddhāraṃ kīrasaṃmateḥ || 1.1 (= 1) ||

p.1, l.4

(p.1, l.4)asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vikramaseno nāma rājā babhūva |
(p.1, l.5)tasminnagare haridatto nāma śreṣṭhī | tasya bhāryā śṛṅgārasundarīnāmnī |
(p.1, l.6)tatputro madanavinodanāmā babhūva | tasya patnī prabhāvatī | sā somadattaśreṣṭhinaḥ
(p.1, l.7)kanyā | madanavinodastu atīva viṣayāsaktaḥ kuputraḥ
(p.1, l.8)pituḥ śikṣāṃ na śṛṇoti | tasya dyūtamṛgayāveśyāmadyādiṣu atīva āsaktiḥ |
(p.1, l.9)kumārgacāriṇaṃ taṃ kuputraṃ dṛṣṭvā tatpitā haridattaḥ sapatnīkaḥ
(p.1, l.10)atīva duḥkhitaḥ saṃjātaḥ | taṃ haridattaṃ kuputraduḥkhena pīḍitaṃ dṛṣṭvā
(p.1, l.11)tasya sakhā trivikramanāmā dvijaḥ svagṛhato nītinipuṇaṃ śukaṃ sārikāṃ
(p.1, l.12)ca gṛhītvā tadgṛhe gatvā prāha | sakhe haridatta enaṃ śukaṃ sapatnīkaṃ
(p.1, l.13)putravattvaṃ paripālaya | etatsaṃrakṣaṇena tava duḥkhaṃ dūrībhaviṣyati | haridattas
(p.1, l.14)tu taṃ śukaṃ gṛhītvā putrāya samarpayāmāsa | madanavinodena śayanamandire
(p.2, l.1)svarṇapañjarasthaḥ sthāpitaḥ paripoṣitaśca | athaikadā rahasi
(p.2, l.2)śuko madanaṃ prāha | he sakhe

asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vikramaseno nāma rājā babhūva | tasminnagare haridatto nāma śreṣṭhī | tasya bhāryā śṛṅgārasundarīnāmnī | tatputro madanavinodanāmā babhūva | tasya patnī prabhāvatī | sā somadattaśreṣṭhinaḥ kanyā | madanavinodastu atīva viṣayāsaktaḥ kuputraḥ pituḥ śikṣāṃ na śṛṇoti | tasya dyūtamṛgayāveśyāmadyādiṣu atīva āsaktiḥ | kumārgacāriṇaṃ taṃ kuputraṃ dṛṣṭvā tatpitā haridattaḥ sapatnīkaḥ atīva duḥkhitaḥ saṃjātaḥ | taṃ haridattaṃ kuputraduḥkhena pīḍitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasya sakhā trivikramanāmā dvijaḥ svagṛhato nītinipuṇaṃ śukaṃ sārikāṃ ca gṛhītvā tadgṛhe gatvā prāha | sakhe haridatta enaṃ śukaṃ sapatnīkaṃ putravattvaṃ paripālaya | etatsaṃrakṣaṇena tava duḥkhaṃ dūrībhaviṣyati | haridattas tu taṃ śukaṃ gṛhītvā putrāya samarpayāmāsa | madanavinodena śayanamandire svarṇapañjarasthaḥ sthāpitaḥ paripoṣitaśca | athaikadā rahasi śuko madanaṃ prāha | he sakhe

p.2, l.3

  • (p.2, l.3)pitroste duḥkhinorduḥkhātpatatyaśrucayo bhuvi | (p.2, l.4)tena pāpena te vatsa patanaṃ devaśarmavat || 1.2 (= 2) ||
pitroste duḥkhinorduḥkhātpatatyaśrucayo bhuvi | tena pāpena te vatsa patanaṃ devaśarmavat || 1.2 (= 2) ||

p.2, l.5

(p.2, l.5)sa prāha | kathametat | śuka āha | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram |
(p.2, l.6)tatra satyaśarmā brāhmaṇaḥ | tadbhāryā dharmaśīlānāmnī putrastu devaśarmā |
(p.2, l.7)sa ca adhītavidyaḥ pitṛpracchannavṛttyā deśāntaraṃ gatvā bhāgīrathītīre
(p.2, l.8)tapaḥ kṛtavān | ekadā sa tapasvī gaṅgātīre japārthamupaviṣṭaḥ | tasmin
(p.2, l.9)kāle kayācit balākayā uḍḍīyamānayā tadaṅgopari purīṣotsargaḥ
(p.2, l.10)kṛtaḥ | sa ca tapasvī krodhākulitanetraḥ yāvadūrdhvaṃ paśyati tāvattatkrodhāgninā
(p.2, l.11)bhasmībhūtāṃ balākāṃ bhūmau patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā (balākāṃ dagdhvā)
(p.2, l.12)nārāyaṇadvijagṛhe bhikṣārthaṃ yayau | svabhartṛśuśrūṣāparayā tatpatnyā kopābhiviṣṭo
(p.2, l.13)nirbhartsitaḥ satpakṣihāyamuktaśca | nāhaṃ balākeva tvatkopasthānam |
(p.2, l.14)sa ca pracchannapātakajñānādbhīto vismitaśca preṣitaśca tayā
(p.3, l.1)dharmavyādhapārśve vārāṇasīṃ nagarīṃ yayau | tatra raktāktahastaṃ yamapratibhaṃ
(p.3, l.2)māṃsavikrayaṃ vidadhānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛśāmante sthitaḥ | vyādhena svāgatapraśnapūrvakaṃ
(p.3, l.3)svagṛhaṃ nītvā nijapitarau sabhaktikaṃ bhojayitvā paścāttasya bhojanaṃ
(p.3, l.4)dattam | tadanantaraṃ sa ca vyādhaṃ jñānakāraṇaṃ papraccha | kathaṃ satī
(p.3, l.5)jñānavatī kathaṃ ca tvaṃ jñānavān | tena vyādhenoktam |

sa prāha | kathametat | śuka āha | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra satyaśarmā brāhmaṇaḥ | tadbhāryā dharmaśīlānāmnī putrastu devaśarmā | sa ca adhītavidyaḥ pitṛpracchannavṛttyā deśāntaraṃ gatvā bhāgīrathītīre tapaḥ kṛtavān | ekadā sa tapasvī gaṅgātīre japārthamupaviṣṭaḥ | tasmin kāle kayācit balākayā uḍḍīyamānayā tadaṅgopari purīṣotsargaḥ kṛtaḥ | sa ca tapasvī krodhākulitanetraḥ yāvadūrdhvaṃ paśyati tāvattatkrodhāgninā bhasmībhūtāṃ balākāṃ bhūmau patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā (balākāṃ dagdhvā) nārāyaṇadvijagṛhe bhikṣārthaṃ yayau | svabhartṛśuśrūṣāparayā tatpatnyā kopābhiviṣṭo nirbhartsitaḥ satpakṣihāyamuktaśca | nāhaṃ balākeva tvatkopasthānam | sa ca pracchannapātakajñānādbhīto vismitaśca preṣitaśca tayā dharmavyādhapārśve vārāṇasīṃ nagarīṃ yayau | tatra raktāktahastaṃ yamapratibhaṃ māṃsavikrayaṃ vidadhānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛśāmante sthitaḥ | vyādhena svāgatapraśnapūrvakaṃ svagṛhaṃ nītvā nijapitarau sabhaktikaṃ bhojayitvā paścāttasya bhojanaṃ dattam | tadanantaraṃ sa ca vyādhaṃ jñānakāraṇaṃ papraccha | kathaṃ satī jñānavatī kathaṃ ca tvaṃ jñānavān | tena vyādhenoktam |

p.3, l.6

  • (p.3, l.6)nijānvayapraṇītaṃ yaḥ samyagdharmaṃ niṣevate | (p.3, l.7)uttamādhamamadhyeṣu vikāreṣu parāṅmukhaḥ || 1.3 (= 3) ||
  • (p.3, l.8)sa gṛhī sa muniḥ sādhuḥ sa ca yogī sa dhārmikaḥ | (p.3, l.9)pitṛśuśrūṣako nityaṃ jantuḥ sādhāraṇaśca yaḥ || 1.4 (= 4) ||
nijānvayapraṇītaṃ yaḥ samyagdharmaṃ niṣevate | uttamādhamamadhyeṣu vikāreṣu parāṅmukhaḥ || 1.3 (= 3) ||
sa gṛhī sa muniḥ sādhuḥ sa ca yogī sa dhārmikaḥ | pitṛśuśrūṣako nityaṃ jantuḥ sādhāraṇaśca yaḥ || 1.4 (= 4) ||

p.3, l.10

(p.3, l.10)ahaṃ sāpi ca evaṃ jñāninau tvaṃ ca nijapitarau parityajya bhramanmādṛśāṃ
(p.3, l.11)na sambhāṣaṇārhaḥ | paramatithiṃ matvā jalpitaḥ | evamuktaḥ sa brāhmaṇo
(p.3, l.12)vinayaparaṃ vyādhaṃ papraccha | tenoktam |

ahaṃ sāpi ca evaṃ jñāninau tvaṃ ca nijapitarau parityajya bhramanmādṛśāṃ na sambhāṣaṇārhaḥ | paramatithiṃ matvā jalpitaḥ | evamuktaḥ sa brāhmaṇo vinayaparaṃ vyādhaṃ papraccha | tenoktam |

p.3, l.13

  • (p.3, l.13)na pūjayanti ye pūjyānmānyānno mānayanti ye | (p.4, l.1)jīvanti nindyamānāste mṛtāḥ svargaṃ na yānti ca || 1.5 (= 5) ||
  • (p.4, l.2)vyādhena bodhitastena sa yayau gṛhamātmanaḥ | (p.4, l.3)abhavatkīrtimānloke parataḥ kīrtibhājanam || 1.6 (= 6) ||
na pūjayanti ye pūjyānmānyānno mānayanti ye | jīvanti nindyamānāste mṛtāḥ svargaṃ na yānti ca || 1.5 (= 5) ||
vyādhena bodhitastena sa yayau gṛhamātmanaḥ | abhavatkīrtimānloke parataḥ kīrtibhājanam || 1.6 (= 6) ||

p.4, l.4

(p.4, l.4)tasmādvaṇigdharmaṃ svakulodbhavaṃ smara pitrośca vinayaparo bhava | evamuktaḥ
(p.4, l.5)sa madanaḥ pitarau namaskṛtya tadanujñāto bhāryāṃ cāpṛcchya pravahaṇamadhirūḍhavān
(p.4, l.6)gato deśāntaram | paścāttatpatnī katiciddināni śokayuktā
(p.4, l.7)nirvāhya svairiṇībhiḥ sakhībhiḥ pratibodhitā puruṣāntarābhilāṣukābhavat |
(p.4, l.8)yatastābhirevamuktam |

tasmādvaṇigdharmaṃ svakulodbhavaṃ smara pitrośca vinayaparo bhava | evamuktaḥ sa madanaḥ pitarau namaskṛtya tadanujñāto bhāryāṃ cāpṛcchya pravahaṇamadhirūḍhavān gato deśāntaram | paścāttatpatnī katiciddināni śokayuktā nirvāhya svairiṇībhiḥ sakhībhiḥ pratibodhitā puruṣāntarābhilāṣukābhavat | yatastābhirevamuktam |

p.4, l.9

  • (p.4, l.9)tāvatpitā tathā bandhuryāvajjīvati mānavaḥ | (p.4, l.10)mṛto mṛta iti jñātvā kṣaṇātsneho nivartate || 1.7 (= 7) ||
tāvatpitā tathā bandhuryāvajjīvati mānavaḥ | mṛto mṛta iti jñātvā kṣaṇātsneho nivartate || 1.7 (= 7) ||

p.5, l.1

(p.5, l.1)atastvaṃ svapatimaprāpyamānā nijaśarīrasya katiciddinasthāyiyauvanasya
(p.5, l.2)puruṣāntararamaṇādgṛhāṇa phalam | tatastāsāṃ vacanena puruṣāntarasya guṇacandrasaṃjñasya
(p.5, l.3)ramaṇāya śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya yāvatpracalitā tāvatsārikayā
(p.5, l.4)mā gacchetyādivacanairnirbhartsitā | tato yāvatsā tāṃ sārikāṃ galamoṭanapūrvaṃ
(p.5, l.5)vināśayati tāvaduḍḍīya yayau | tataḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā sveṣṭadevatāṃ
(p.5, l.6)hṛdi smṛtvā tāmbūlaṃ pragṛhya yāvaccalitā tāvat śukaḥ prāha |
(p.5, l.7)siddhirastu | kva gantavyamityādivākyaiḥ pṛṣṭā | sā ca śukavacanaṃ śakunam
(p.5, l.8)iti kṛtvā prahasya tamāha | he śukarāja narāntarāsvādaṃ vijñātuṃ
(p.5, l.9)pracalitāsmi | śuka uvāca | yuktamidaṃ kartavyameva paraṃ duṣkaraṃ ninditaṃ
(p.5, l.10)ca kulastrīṇām | kiṃ ca | tadā gamyatāṃ yadi viparīte samāyāte
(p.5, l.11)sati tava buddhirasti | yadi nāsti tadā parābhavapadaṃ bhaviṣyasi |

atastvaṃ svapatimaprāpyamānā nijaśarīrasya katiciddinasthāyiyauvanasya puruṣāntararamaṇādgṛhāṇa phalam | tatastāsāṃ vacanena puruṣāntarasya guṇacandrasaṃjñasya ramaṇāya śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya yāvatpracalitā tāvatsārikayā mā gacchetyādivacanairnirbhartsitā | tato yāvatsā tāṃ sārikāṃ galamoṭanapūrvaṃ vināśayati tāvaduḍḍīya yayau | tataḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā sveṣṭadevatāṃ hṛdi smṛtvā tāmbūlaṃ pragṛhya yāvaccalitā tāvat śukaḥ prāha | siddhirastu | kva gantavyamityādivākyaiḥ pṛṣṭā | sā ca śukavacanaṃ śakunam iti kṛtvā prahasya tamāha | he śukarāja narāntarāsvādaṃ vijñātuṃ pracalitāsmi | śuka uvāca | yuktamidaṃ kartavyameva paraṃ duṣkaraṃ ninditaṃ ca kulastrīṇām | kiṃ ca | tadā gamyatāṃ yadi viparīte samāyāte sati tava buddhirasti | yadi nāsti tadā parābhavapadaṃ bhaviṣyasi |

p.6, l.1

  • (p.6, l.1)yataḥ |
  • kautukānveṣiṇo nityaṃ durjanā vyasanāgame | (p.6, l.2)māsopavāsinī yadvadvaṇikputrakacagrahe || 1.8 (= 8) ||
  • (p.6, l.3)papraccha sā tadā sārdhaṃ puṃścalībhiḥ kṛtādarā | (p.6, l.4)sasaṃbhramā jagādedaṃ kimidaṃ bhāṣitaṃ śuka || 1.9 (= 9) ||
  • (p.6, l.5)yadi te kautukaṃ subhru parārthaṃ gaccha sundari | (p.6, l.6)sthirībhūya tvayā paścāt śrāvyeyaṃ mahatī kathā || 1.10 (= 10) ||

yataḥ |

kautukānveṣiṇo nityaṃ durjanā vyasanāgame | māsopavāsinī yadvadvaṇikputrakacagrahe || 1.8 (= 8) ||
papraccha sā tadā sārdhaṃ puṃścalībhiḥ kṛtādarā | sasaṃbhramā jagādedaṃ kimidaṃ bhāṣitaṃ śuka || 1.9 (= 9) ||
yadi te kautukaṃ subhru parārthaṃ gaccha sundari | sthirībhūya tvayā paścāt śrāvyeyaṃ mahatī kathā || 1.10 (= 10) ||

p.6, l.7

(p.6, l.7)evaṃ śukoktaṃ śrutvā yadā sā kautukākulacetasā nijagṛha āsīnāsti
(p.6, l.8)tadā śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti candrāvatī purī | tasyāṃ bhīmanāmā
(p.6, l.9)nṛpaḥ | tatra sudhano nāma mohanaśreṣṭhisutaḥ tannagaravāsino haridattasya
(p.6, l.10)kalatraṃ lakṣmīṃ rantumīhate | tadvatsā na manyate | tato māsopavāsinīṃ
(p.6, l.11)pūrṇābhidhānāṃ gatvā pūrṇadhanāvarjitāṃ kṛtvā haridatte nagarādbahirgate
(p.6, l.12)tadgṛhe dūtītvena preṣayāmāsa | sāpi cāṭūktibhirlakṣmīṃ prasādayāmāsa |
(p.6, l.13)prasannayā ca tayetyuktam | yattvaṃ yācase tatkaromi | pūrṇayoktam |
(p.7, l.1)tarhi manmataṃ naraṃ bhaja | tayoktam | kulastrīṇāṃ naitadyujyate paraṃ yattavāgre
(p.7, l.2)pratipannaṃ tatkaromi |

evaṃ śukoktaṃ śrutvā yadā sā kautukākulacetasā nijagṛha āsīnāsti tadā śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti candrāvatī purī | tasyāṃ bhīmanāmā nṛpaḥ | tatra sudhano nāma mohanaśreṣṭhisutaḥ tannagaravāsino haridattasya kalatraṃ lakṣmīṃ rantumīhate | tadvatsā na manyate | tato māsopavāsinīṃ pūrṇābhidhānāṃ gatvā pūrṇadhanāvarjitāṃ kṛtvā haridatte nagarādbahirgate tadgṛhe dūtītvena preṣayāmāsa | sāpi cāṭūktibhirlakṣmīṃ prasādayāmāsa | prasannayā ca tayetyuktam | yattvaṃ yācase tatkaromi | pūrṇayoktam | tarhi manmataṃ naraṃ bhaja | tayoktam | kulastrīṇāṃ naitadyujyate paraṃ yattavāgre pratipannaṃ tatkaromi |

p.7, l.3

  • (p.7, l.3)uktaṃ ca |
  • chijjau sīsaṃ aha hou bandhaṇaṃ caau savvahā lacchī | (p.7, l.4)paḍivaṇṇapālaṇe supurisāṇa jaṃ hou taṃ hou || 1.11 (= 11) || (•)
  • (p.7, l.5)tathā ca |
  • diḍhalohasiṅkhalāṇaṃ assāṇa vi vihapāsabandhāṇaṃ | (p.7, l.6)tāṇaṃ cia ahiaraaro vāābandho supurisassa || 1.12 (= 12) || (•)
  • (p.7, l.7)adyāpi nojjhati haraḥ kila kālakūṭaṃ (p.7, l.8)kūrmo bibharti dharaṇīṃ khalu cātmapṛṣṭhe | (p.7, l.9)ambhonidhirvahati duḥsahavāḍavāgnim (p.7, l.10)aṅgīkṛtaṃ sukṛtinaḥ paripālayanti || 1.13 (= 13) ||

uktaṃ ca |

chijjau sīsaṃ aha hou bandhaṇaṃ caau savvahā lacchī | paḍivaṇṇapālaṇe supurisāṇa jaṃ hou taṃ hou || 1.11 (= 11) || (•)

tathā ca |

diḍhalohasiṅkhalāṇaṃ assāṇa vi vihapāsabandhāṇaṃ | tāṇaṃ cia ahiaraaro vāābandho supurisassa || 1.12 (= 12) || (•)
adyāpi nojjhati haraḥ kila kālakūṭaṃ kūrmo bibharti dharaṇīṃ khalu cātmapṛṣṭhe | ambhonidhirvahati duḥsahavāḍavāgnim aṅgīkṛtaṃ sukṛtinaḥ paripālayanti || 1.13 (= 13) ||

p.7, l.11

(p.7, l.11)tac chrutvā hṛṣṭā pūrṇā | evamevaitat | tatastāṃ lakṣmīṃ pratividhāya guṇamohanārthe
(p.7, l.12)pradoṣe svagṛhe nināya | tataḥ sa mohanaḥ kathitavelopari
(p.7, l.13)nāgataḥ kiṃcitkāryādivaiyagryeṇa | tato lakṣmyā sakāmayoktam |
(p.8, l.1)yatkamapi naraṃ samānaya | tataḥ pūrṇayā mūḍhayā tatpatireva samānītaḥ |
(p.8, l.2)svabhartari samāyāte sā kathaṃ bhavatviti kathaṃ gṛhaṃ yātviti tvaṃ sakhyas
(p.8, l.3)tava vā kathayantu | tā āhuḥ | na jānīmaḥ | tvameva kathaya | śuka
(p.8, l.4)āha | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayoktam | na yāsyāmi |
(p.8, l.5)śukaḥ | sā āgacchanneva svapatiriti jñātvā taṃ kacagrahaṃ pragṛhyaivamuvāca |
(p.8, l.6)he śaṭha sarvadā tvamiti mamāgre jalpasi yanme tvāṃ vinā nānyā
(p.8, l.7)vallabhā asti | adhunā tu mayā parīkṣito jñātaśceti kopaṃ cakre |
(p.8, l.8)sa ca tāṃ kaṣṭena sukomalavacanairanunīya svagṛhaṃ ninye |

tac chrutvā hṛṣṭā pūrṇā | evamevaitat | tatastāṃ lakṣmīṃ pratividhāya guṇamohanārthe pradoṣe svagṛhe nināya | tataḥ sa mohanaḥ kathitavelopari nāgataḥ kiṃcitkāryādivaiyagryeṇa | tato lakṣmyā sakāmayoktam | yatkamapi naraṃ samānaya | tataḥ pūrṇayā mūḍhayā tatpatireva samānītaḥ | svabhartari samāyāte sā kathaṃ bhavatviti kathaṃ gṛhaṃ yātviti tvaṃ sakhyas tava vā kathayantu | tā āhuḥ | na jānīmaḥ | tvameva kathaya | śuka āha | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayoktam | na yāsyāmi | śukaḥ | sā āgacchanneva svapatiriti jñātvā taṃ kacagrahaṃ pragṛhyaivamuvāca | he śaṭha sarvadā tvamiti mamāgre jalpasi yanme tvāṃ vinā nānyā vallabhā asti | adhunā tu mayā parīkṣito jñātaśceti kopaṃ cakre | sa ca tāṃ kaṣṭena sukomalavacanairanunīya svagṛhaṃ ninye |

p.9, l.5

(p.9, l.5)tataḥ prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kā yaśodevī | kadā kasmin saṃkaṭe tayā
(p.9, l.6)ka upāyaḥ kṛta iti | śukaḥ | yadā kathayāmi tadā mayi suratavighātena
(p.9, l.7)tava kopaḥ prāṇanisūdanaḥ syāt | sā āha | suhṛdāṃ sādhv
(p.9, l.8)asādhvapi śrotavyameva | ityanujñātaḥ śuka āha | asti nandanaṃ nāma
(p.9, l.9)nagaram | tatra nandano nāma rājā | tatputro rājaśekharaḥ | tadvadhūḥ
(p.9, l.10)śaśiprabhā | tāṃ dhanasenasuto vīranāmā dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ sanjvarapīḍito
(p.9, l.11)'bhūt | bhojanādi na vidhatte | sa ca mātrā yaśodevyā pṛṣṭaḥ
(p.9, l.12)san sagadgadaṃ kāraṇamāha | sā ca rājakanyā durlabhā | sa kathaṃ jīvatu |
(p.9, l.13)iti praśnaḥ | tayoktam | tvameva kathaya | śukaḥ | yadi prabhāvati adya
(p.9, l.14)na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | ityukte sā āha | kathayeti | atha śukaḥ |
(p.10, l.1)sā yaśodevī ekāṃ śunīṃ bhojanādyairāvarjayitvā ābharaṇāni paridhāyātmanā
(p.10, l.2)sārdhaṃ gṛhītvā śaśiprabhāpārśve gatvā tāṃ vijane sagadgadā
(p.10, l.3)jagāda | ahaṃ ca tvaṃ ca iyaṃ ca pūrvabhave bhaginyo 'bhūvan | mayā
(p.10, l.4)niḥśaṅkayā tvayā tu saśaṅkayā paranarābhilāṣaḥ pūritaḥ | anayā tu
(p.10, l.5)naiva | ato 'syāḥ śīlaprabhāvātkevalaṃ jātismaraṇameva na bhogāḥ śunikā
(p.10, l.6)ca saṃjātā | saṃbhogavighnājjātismaraṇaṃ ca na te vartate | mama
(p.10, l.7)punarbhogānnirvighnānnirvighnajātismaraṇaṃ ca | ato 'hamanukampayā imāṃ
(p.10, l.8)śunakīṃ tvāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kathayitumāgatā | atastvayārthināṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ dātavyam
(p.10, l.9)eva | yo dānaṃ kuryātsa bhavetsarvasaṃpadāṃ sthānam |

tataḥ prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kā yaśodevī | kadā kasmin saṃkaṭe tayā ka upāyaḥ kṛta iti | śukaḥ | yadā kathayāmi tadā mayi suratavighātena tava kopaḥ prāṇanisūdanaḥ syāt | sā āha | suhṛdāṃ sādhv asādhvapi śrotavyameva | ityanujñātaḥ śuka āha | asti nandanaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra nandano nāma rājā | tatputro rājaśekharaḥ | tadvadhūḥ śaśiprabhā | tāṃ dhanasenasuto vīranāmā dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ sanjvarapīḍito 'bhūt | bhojanādi na vidhatte | sa ca mātrā yaśodevyā pṛṣṭaḥ san sagadgadaṃ kāraṇamāha | sā ca rājakanyā durlabhā | sa kathaṃ jīvatu | iti praśnaḥ | tayoktam | tvameva kathaya | śukaḥ | yadi prabhāvati adya na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | ityukte sā āha | kathayeti | atha śukaḥ | sā yaśodevī ekāṃ śunīṃ bhojanādyairāvarjayitvā ābharaṇāni paridhāyātmanā sārdhaṃ gṛhītvā śaśiprabhāpārśve gatvā tāṃ vijane sagadgadā jagāda | ahaṃ ca tvaṃ ca iyaṃ ca pūrvabhave bhaginyo 'bhūvan | mayā niḥśaṅkayā tvayā tu saśaṅkayā paranarābhilāṣaḥ pūritaḥ | anayā tu naiva | ato 'syāḥ śīlaprabhāvātkevalaṃ jātismaraṇameva na bhogāḥ śunikā ca saṃjātā | saṃbhogavighnājjātismaraṇaṃ ca na te vartate | mama punarbhogānnirvighnānnirvighnajātismaraṇaṃ ca | ato 'hamanukampayā imāṃ śunakīṃ tvāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kathayitumāgatā | atastvayārthināṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ dātavyam eva | yo dānaṃ kuryātsa bhavetsarvasaṃpadāṃ sthānam |

p.10, l.10

  • (p.10, l.10)uktaṃ ca |

uktaṃ ca |

kathayanti na yācante bhikṣāhārā gṛhe gṛhe | arthibhyo dīyatāṃ nityamadātuḥ phalamīdṛśam || 2.3 (= 17) ||

p.10, l.12

(p.10, l.12)tataḥ śaśiprabhā sakaṇṭhagrāhaṃ ruditvā prāha | māmapi kalyāṇi puruṣāntareṇa
(p.10, l.13)yojaya | tato yaśodevī tāṃ svasthīkṛtya bhartṛviditāṃ svagṛhaṃ
(p.10, l.14)nītvā svaputreṇa yojayāmāsa | sa ca rājaśekharo dravyādidānatoṣitaḥ
(p.10, l.15)sakhīyamiti kṛtvā na nivārayāmāsa |

p.11, l.10

(p.11, l.10)prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kathametat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā
(p.11, l.11)nagarī | tatra sudarśano rājā | tatra ca vimalo nāma vaṇik |
(p.11, l.12)tasya ca patnīdvayaṃ subhagaṃ rūpasaṃpannaṃ dṛṣṭvā kuṭilanāmā dhūrtastadbhāryādvayagrahaṇecchayā
(p.11, l.13)ambikāṃ devīmārādhya vimalarūpaṃ yayāce | labdhvā
(p.11, l.14)ca tatprakṛtiṃ vimale bahirgate tadgṛhaṃ gatvā prabhutvaṃ cakāra | prasādadhanadānair
(p.11, l.15)vaśīkṛto 'khilo 'pi parijanavargaḥ | tadbhāryādvayaṃ bahumānadānādinā
(p.12, l.1)saṃtoṣya svecchayā bhuṅkte | vimalo 'yaṃ dhanādyanityatāṃ śrutvā
(p.12, l.2)dātā babhūveti parijano anavarataṃ cintayati | atha satyavimalo 'pi
(p.12, l.3)dvāramāgataḥ kuṭilājñayā dvārapālena niṣiddhaḥ | tato bahiḥsthaḥ phūtkaroti |
(p.12, l.4)vañcito 'haṃ dhūrtarājena | tasya caivaṃ krandato gotrajā janāḥ
(p.12, l.5)kautukācca militāḥ | tatkṣaṇāt haṭṭāni muktvā vaṇiksārtho militvā
(p.12, l.6)ārakṣikamantrimukhyānāṃ purataḥ phūccakre | rājanvañcito 'smi dhūrtarājena |
(p.12, l.7)tato rājñā tadavalokanāya prahitāḥ puruṣāḥ | tenāpi te dravyādidānena
(p.12, l.8)sānukūlāḥ kṛtāḥ | taṃ dhanadāyakaṃ gṛhe dṛṣṭvā jano vadati |
(p.12, l.9)svāminvimalo gṛhe vidyate | ayaṃ ca dhūrtarāṭ dvārasthaḥ | tato nṛpeṇa
(p.12, l.10)dvāvapyekatra kṛtau | tato dvayormadhyānna ko 'pi dhūrtetarayorvyaktiṃ jānāti |
(p.12, l.11)jātaḥ kolāhalo 'khilalokavyavahāranāśakaraḥ rājñaścāpavādaḥ |
(p.12, l.12)yato rājñāṃ duṣṭanigrahaḥ śiṣṭapālanaṃ ca svargāya |

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kathametat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā nagarī | tatra sudarśano rājā | tatra ca vimalo nāma vaṇik | tasya ca patnīdvayaṃ subhagaṃ rūpasaṃpannaṃ dṛṣṭvā kuṭilanāmā dhūrtastadbhāryādvayagrahaṇecchayā ambikāṃ devīmārādhya vimalarūpaṃ yayāce | labdhvā ca tatprakṛtiṃ vimale bahirgate tadgṛhaṃ gatvā prabhutvaṃ cakāra | prasādadhanadānair vaśīkṛto 'khilo 'pi parijanavargaḥ | tadbhāryādvayaṃ bahumānadānādinā saṃtoṣya svecchayā bhuṅkte | vimalo 'yaṃ dhanādyanityatāṃ śrutvā dātā babhūveti parijano anavarataṃ cintayati | atha satyavimalo 'pi dvāramāgataḥ kuṭilājñayā dvārapālena niṣiddhaḥ | tato bahiḥsthaḥ phūtkaroti | vañcito 'haṃ dhūrtarājena | tasya caivaṃ krandato gotrajā janāḥ kautukācca militāḥ | tatkṣaṇāt haṭṭāni muktvā vaṇiksārtho militvā ārakṣikamantrimukhyānāṃ purataḥ phūccakre | rājanvañcito 'smi dhūrtarājena | tato rājñā tadavalokanāya prahitāḥ puruṣāḥ | tenāpi te dravyādidānena sānukūlāḥ kṛtāḥ | taṃ dhanadāyakaṃ gṛhe dṛṣṭvā jano vadati | svāminvimalo gṛhe vidyate | ayaṃ ca dhūrtarāṭ dvārasthaḥ | tato nṛpeṇa dvāvapyekatra kṛtau | tato dvayormadhyānna ko 'pi dhūrtetarayorvyaktiṃ jānāti | jātaḥ kolāhalo 'khilalokavyavahāranāśakaraḥ rājñaścāpavādaḥ | yato rājñāṃ duṣṭanigrahaḥ śiṣṭapālanaṃ ca svargāya |

p.12, l.13

  • (p.12, l.13)uktaṃ ca |

p.13, l.2

(p.13, l.2)tato rājā ekānte tayornirṇayamacintayat | tatkathaya kathaṃ niścayaḥ
(p.13, l.3)syāditi praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | sa rājā labdhopāyastadvimalabhāryādvayaṃ pṛthak
(p.13, l.4)pṛthaksaṃsthāpya pṛṣṭavān | kiṃ yuvayoḥ pāṇigrahaṇe bhartrā vibhūṣaṇaṃ pradattaṃ
(p.13, l.5)dhanaṃ ca | paścātkiṃ jalpitaṃ prathamasaṅge ca kā vārttā bhartrā sahābhūt |
(p.13, l.6)kā mātā kaśca pitā | kiṃ kulam | kā jātiḥ | ityevaṃ pṛṣṭābhyāṃ
(p.13, l.7)yathālabdhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāproktaṃ yathāsuptaṃ sarvaṃ tābhyāṃ kathitam | paścāttu
(p.13, l.8)tau puruṣau pṛṣṭau parasparaṃ visaṃvadantau | tato bhāryādvayasya rukmiṇīsundarīnāmadheyasya
(p.13, l.9)yaḥ saṃvādaṃ vadati sa satyaḥ | itarastu dhūrto rājñā
(p.13, l.10)nirvāsitaḥ | satyastu rājñā sabhāryaḥ satkṛtaḥ svagṛhaṃ gataḥ | iti mahārājabuddhiḥ |
(p.13, l.11)iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā ||
(p.13, l.12)iti śukasaptatau tṛtīyā kathā ||

tato rājā ekānte tayornirṇayamacintayat | tatkathaya kathaṃ niścayaḥ syāditi praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | sa rājā labdhopāyastadvimalabhāryādvayaṃ pṛthak pṛthaksaṃsthāpya pṛṣṭavān | kiṃ yuvayoḥ pāṇigrahaṇe bhartrā vibhūṣaṇaṃ pradattaṃ dhanaṃ ca | paścātkiṃ jalpitaṃ prathamasaṅge ca kā vārttā bhartrā sahābhūt | kā mātā kaśca pitā | kiṃ kulam | kā jātiḥ | ityevaṃ pṛṣṭābhyāṃ yathālabdhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāproktaṃ yathāsuptaṃ sarvaṃ tābhyāṃ kathitam | paścāttu tau puruṣau pṛṣṭau parasparaṃ visaṃvadantau | tato bhāryādvayasya rukmiṇīsundarīnāmadheyasya yaḥ saṃvādaṃ vadati sa satyaḥ | itarastu dhūrto rājñā nirvāsitaḥ | satyastu rājñā sabhāryaḥ satkṛtaḥ svagṛhaṃ gataḥ | iti mahārājabuddhiḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau tṛtīyā kathā ||

p.14, l.1

p.14, l.5

(p.14, l.5)prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti somaprabhaṃ nāma dvijasthānam |
(p.14, l.6)tatra vidvāndhārmikaḥ somaśarmā nāma vipraḥ | tatputrī rūpaudāryaguṇopetā
(p.14, l.7)viṣakanyeti vijñātābhūt | tena tāṃ bhayena ko 'pi na
(p.14, l.8)vivāhayati | tataḥ somaśarmā varārthaṃ bhuvaṃ paryaṭan saṃprāpto dvijasthānaṃ
(p.14, l.9)janasthānaṃ nāma | tatra govindanāmā brāhmaṇo jaḍo nirdhanaśca | tasmai
(p.14, l.10)kanyā pradattā | tena suhṛdāṃ nivārayatāmapi kṛtāvajñenoḍhā sarvarūpalāvaṇyaguṇopetā
(p.14, l.11)mohinī viṣakanyā | sā vidagdhā govindastu mūrkhaḥ
(p.14, l.12)laghuvayāśca | tataśca sā ātmano rūpalāvaṇyayauvanaṃ śuśoca |

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti somaprabhaṃ nāma dvijasthānam | tatra vidvāndhārmikaḥ somaśarmā nāma vipraḥ | tatputrī rūpaudāryaguṇopetā viṣakanyeti vijñātābhūt | tena tāṃ bhayena ko 'pi na vivāhayati | tataḥ somaśarmā varārthaṃ bhuvaṃ paryaṭan saṃprāpto dvijasthānaṃ janasthānaṃ nāma | tatra govindanāmā brāhmaṇo jaḍo nirdhanaśca | tasmai kanyā pradattā | tena suhṛdāṃ nivārayatāmapi kṛtāvajñenoḍhā sarvarūpalāvaṇyaguṇopetā mohinī viṣakanyā | sā vidagdhā govindastu mūrkhaḥ laghuvayāśca | tataśca sā ātmano rūpalāvaṇyayauvanaṃ śuśoca |

  • (p.15, l.1)pāusasamaapavāso jovvaṇadiahe tahā a dāliddaṃ | (p.15, l.2)paḍhamasiṇehavioo tiṇṇi vi garuāi dukkhāiṃ || 4.3 (= 24) || (•)
  • (p.15, l.3)appatthāve paḍhiaṃ kaṇṭhavihūṇaṃ ca gāiaṃ gīaṃ | (p.15, l.4)mā mā bhaṇantisuraaṃ tiṇṇi vi garuāi dukkhāiṃ || 4.4 (= 25) || (•)
avidagdhaḥ patiḥ strīṇāṃ prauḍhāṇāṃ nāyako 'guṇī | guṇināṃ tyāgināṃ stoko vibhavaśceti duḥkhakṛt || 4.2 (= 23) ||
pāusasamaapavāso jovvaṇadiahe tahā a dāliddaṃ | paḍhamasiṇehavioo tiṇṇi vi garuāi dukkhāiṃ || 4.3 (= 24) || (•)
appatthāve paḍhiaṃ kaṇṭhavihūṇaṃ ca gāiaṃ gīaṃ | mā mā bhaṇantisuraaṃ tiṇṇi vi garuāi dukkhāiṃ || 4.4 (= 25) || (•)

p.15, l.5

(p.15, l.5)sānyadā govindaṃ patimityabravīt | mama piturgehātsamāgatāyā bahūni
(p.15, l.6)dināni saṃjātāni | tato 'haṃ tvayaiva saha gamiṣye nānyathā | tataḥ
(p.15, l.7)śakaṭaṃ mārgayitvā sabhāryakaḥ sa calitaḥ | yāvatprayāti tāvatpathi
(p.16, l.1)eko yuvā vāgmī surūpaḥ śūraśca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo militaḥ |
(p.16, l.2)tasya brāhmaṇasya tasyāścānyonyamanurāgaḥ saṃjātaḥ |

sānyadā govindaṃ patimityabravīt | mama piturgehātsamāgatāyā bahūni dināni saṃjātāni | tato 'haṃ tvayaiva saha gamiṣye nānyathā | tataḥ śakaṭaṃ mārgayitvā sabhāryakaḥ sa calitaḥ | yāvatprayāti tāvatpathi eko yuvā vāgmī surūpaḥ śūraśca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo militaḥ | tasya brāhmaṇasya tasyāścānyonyamanurāgaḥ saṃjātaḥ |

p.16, l.3

  • (p.16, l.3)uktaṃ ca |
  • prītiḥ syāddarśanādyaiḥ prathamamatha manaḥsaṅgasaṃkalpabhāvo (p.16, l.4)nidrācchedastanutvaṃ vapuṣi kaluṣatā cendriyāṇāṃ nivṛttiḥ | (p.16, l.5)hrīnāśonmādamūrcchāmaraṇamiti jagadyātyavasthā daśaitāḥ (p.16, l.6)lagnairyatpuṣpabāṇaiḥ sa jayati madanaḥ saṃnirastānyadhanvī || 4.5 (= 26) ||

uktaṃ ca |

prītiḥ syāddarśanādyaiḥ prathamamatha manaḥsaṅgasaṃkalpabhāvo nidrācchedastanutvaṃ vapuṣi kaluṣatā cendriyāṇāṃ nivṛttiḥ | hrīnāśonmādamūrcchāmaraṇamiti jagadyātyavasthā daśaitāḥ lagnairyatpuṣpabāṇaiḥ sa jayati madanaḥ saṃnirastānyadhanvī || 4.5 (= 26) ||

p.16, l.7

(p.16, l.7)sa pathiko dampatyoḥ pūgapattroccayaṃ dadāti | ityevaṃ grāmyabrāhmaṇo viṣṇor
(p.16, l.8)viśvastaḥ ātmano nirodhasaṅgabhayāduttīrya (?) taṃ gantrīvāhamārohayati |
(p.16, l.9)viṣṇunā ca patyau vṛkṣāntaragate sā mohinī bhuktā ātmavaśīkṛtā |
(p.16, l.10)tayā cātmīyaṃ nāma gotraṃ kulakramaṃ cājñāpitaḥ | patyuśca samāgatasya
(p.16, l.11)tvaṃ cauro 'sīti gantryārohaṇaṃ kurvato niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ | viṣṇurapi tāṃ
(p.16, l.12)gṛhītvā govindaṃ dharṣitavān | tatastayoḥ keśākeśi saṃvṛttam |
(p.17, l.1)govindastu viṣṇunā viṣakanyāprabhāveṇa nirjitaḥ | tatastāṃ gṛhītvā
(p.17, l.2)viṣṇuḥ svagṛhaṃ praticalitaḥ | govindaḥ pṛṣṭhastho mārgāsanne grāme gatvā
(p.17, l.3)phūtkṛtavān | yadanena caureṇa mama bhāryā gṛhītā | trāyatāṃ tām | mama
(p.17, l.4)śaraṇaṃ bho janāḥ | atha grāmādhipena viṣṇurmohinīyuto dhṛtaḥ | pṛṣṭenottaraṃ
(p.17, l.5)dattaṃ viṣṇunā yatheyaṃ mayā pariṇītā | madīyāṃ ca bhāryāmeṣa
(p.17, l.6)pathiko mārge dṛṣṭvā grahilo babhūva | govindenāpi pṛṣṭena idamevottaritam |
(p.17, l.7)tato mantrī tayorekamevottaraṃ śrutvā jātyādikaṃ pṛṣṭavān |
(p.17, l.8)trayamapi tu saṃvadati tataḥ kathaṃ niścayaḥ |
(p.17, l.9)iti śukapraśnaḥ | tatastayā
(p.17, l.10)pṛṣṭaḥ śuka āha | mantriṇoktam | kiyanti dināni saṃgamasya yuṣmākaṃ
(p.17, l.11)prayāṇe | tairuktam | kalye bhojanāntaraṃ saṃvṛttaḥ samāgamaḥ | tato
(p.17, l.12)mantriṇā brāhmaṇau pṛthakpṛthakpṛṣṭau | kimanayā kalye bhojanavelāyāṃ
(p.17, l.13)bhuktam | yacca tayā bhuktaṃ tadgovindo jānāti itarastu na | tataḥ sa
(p.17, l.14)viḍambitaḥ sacivena | govindaḥ śikṣitaḥ | dhigimāṃ brāhmaṇīṃ paratreha
(p.17, l.15)ca duḥkhadāṃ muñca śīghram |

sa pathiko dampatyoḥ pūgapattroccayaṃ dadāti | ityevaṃ grāmyabrāhmaṇo viṣṇor viśvastaḥ ātmano nirodhasaṅgabhayāduttīrya (?) taṃ gantrīvāhamārohayati | viṣṇunā ca patyau vṛkṣāntaragate sā mohinī bhuktā ātmavaśīkṛtā | tayā cātmīyaṃ nāma gotraṃ kulakramaṃ cājñāpitaḥ | patyuśca samāgatasya tvaṃ cauro 'sīti gantryārohaṇaṃ kurvato niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ | viṣṇurapi tāṃ gṛhītvā govindaṃ dharṣitavān | tatastayoḥ keśākeśi saṃvṛttam | govindastu viṣṇunā viṣakanyāprabhāveṇa nirjitaḥ | tatastāṃ gṛhītvā viṣṇuḥ svagṛhaṃ praticalitaḥ | govindaḥ pṛṣṭhastho mārgāsanne grāme gatvā phūtkṛtavān | yadanena caureṇa mama bhāryā gṛhītā | trāyatāṃ tām | mama śaraṇaṃ bho janāḥ | atha grāmādhipena viṣṇurmohinīyuto dhṛtaḥ | pṛṣṭenottaraṃ dattaṃ viṣṇunā yatheyaṃ mayā pariṇītā | madīyāṃ ca bhāryāmeṣa pathiko mārge dṛṣṭvā grahilo babhūva | govindenāpi pṛṣṭena idamevottaritam | tato mantrī tayorekamevottaraṃ śrutvā jātyādikaṃ pṛṣṭavān | trayamapi tu saṃvadati tataḥ kathaṃ niścayaḥ | iti śukapraśnaḥ | tatastayā pṛṣṭaḥ śuka āha | mantriṇoktam | kiyanti dināni saṃgamasya yuṣmākaṃ prayāṇe | tairuktam | kalye bhojanāntaraṃ saṃvṛttaḥ samāgamaḥ | tato mantriṇā brāhmaṇau pṛthakpṛthakpṛṣṭau | kimanayā kalye bhojanavelāyāṃ bhuktam | yacca tayā bhuktaṃ tadgovindo jānāti itarastu na | tataḥ sa viḍambitaḥ sacivena | govindaḥ śikṣitaḥ | dhigimāṃ brāhmaṇīṃ paratreha ca duḥkhadāṃ muñca śīghram |

p.18, l.1

  • (p.18, l.1)uktaṃ ca |
  • vaidyaṃ pānarataṃ naṭaṃ kupaṭhitaṃ mūrkhaṃ parivrājakaṃ (p.18, l.2)yodhaṃ kāpuruṣaṃ viṭaṃ vivayasaṃ svādhyāyahīnaṃ dvijam | (p.18, l.3)rājyaṃ bālanarendramantrirahitaṃ mitraṃ chalānveṣi ca (p.18, l.4)bhāryāṃ yauvanagarvitāṃ pararatāṃ muñcanti ye paṇḍitāḥ || 4.6 (= 27) ||
  • (p.18, l.5)tathāpi kāminīlubdho dhikkṛtaḥ sādhubhistadā | (p.18, l.6)tāmevādāya calitastatkṛte nihataḥ pathi || 4.7 (= 28) ||
  • (p.18, l.7)taddevi yaḥ karotyevamavajñāṃ vṛddhaśikṣitaḥ | (p.18, l.8)sa parābhavamāpnoti govindo brāhmaṇo yathā || 4.8 (= 29) ||

uktaṃ ca |

vaidyaṃ pānarataṃ naṭaṃ kupaṭhitaṃ mūrkhaṃ parivrājakaṃ yodhaṃ kāpuruṣaṃ viṭaṃ vivayasaṃ svādhyāyahīnaṃ dvijam | rājyaṃ bālanarendramantrirahitaṃ mitraṃ chalānveṣi ca bhāryāṃ yauvanagarvitāṃ pararatāṃ muñcanti ye paṇḍitāḥ || 4.6 (= 27) ||
tathāpi kāminīlubdho dhikkṛtaḥ sādhubhistadā | tāmevādāya calitastatkṛte nihataḥ pathi || 4.7 (= 28) ||
taddevi yaḥ karotyevamavajñāṃ vṛddhaśikṣitaḥ | sa parābhavamāpnoti govindo brāhmaṇo yathā || 4.8 (= 29) ||

p.18, l.12

  • (p.18, l.12)gaccha devi vijānāsi yadi kartuṃ tvamuttaram | (p.18, l.13)sabhāyāṃ nṛpateryadvadviṣame bālapaṇḍitā || 5.1 (= 30) ||

p.19, l.1

(p.19, l.1)prabhāvatīpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti ujjayinī nāma nagarī |
(p.19, l.2)tatra vikramādityo rājā | tasya rājñī kāmalīlā nāma uttamakulajātā |
(p.19, l.3)sā ca rājño 'tīva vallabhā | ekadā nṛpastayā sārdhaṃ bhojanaṃ
(p.19, l.4)kurvanbhṛṣṭamatsyāṃstasyai dāpayāmāsa | sā āha | svāminnāhametān puruṣān
(p.19, l.5)avalokayitumapi samarthā kiṃ punaḥ sparśanam | iti śrutvā tena
(p.19, l.6)matsyā aṭṭāṭṭahāsena tathā jahasuryathā nāgarikalokena śrutam | rājā
(p.19, l.7)ca tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ mantrijyotirvicchākunikakovidān pṛcchati | yadā
(p.19, l.8)na ko 'pi jānāti tadā sarvadvijāgresaraṃ purohitaṃ prāha yathā tvayaiva
(p.19, l.9)matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ kathanīyamanyathā tvaṃ deśānnirvāsaṃ prāpnoṣi | purodhāpyetad
(p.19, l.10)vacaḥ śrutvā dinapañcakaṃ vyavadhāne yācayitvā saviṣādo gṛhamāgamat |
(p.19, l.11)sa purohitaḥ taduttaramajānan purastādrājñā nirvāsyate | sa kathaṃ bhavatv
(p.19, l.12)iti praśnaḥ | uttaramapyāha śukaḥ | sa brāhmaṇo viṣādāpannaḥ putryā
(p.19, l.13)bālapaṇḍitayā babhāṣe | tāta kathamudvignacitta iva lakṣyase | kathaya
(p.19, l.14)viṣādasya kāraṇam | vidvadbhirvipadyapyuccaiḥ sthātavyam |

prabhāvatīpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti ujjayinī nāma nagarī | tatra vikramādityo rājā | tasya rājñī kāmalīlā nāma uttamakulajātā | sā ca rājño 'tīva vallabhā | ekadā nṛpastayā sārdhaṃ bhojanaṃ kurvanbhṛṣṭamatsyāṃstasyai dāpayāmāsa | sā āha | svāminnāhametān puruṣān avalokayitumapi samarthā kiṃ punaḥ sparśanam | iti śrutvā tena matsyā aṭṭāṭṭahāsena tathā jahasuryathā nāgarikalokena śrutam | rājā ca tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ mantrijyotirvicchākunikakovidān pṛcchati | yadā na ko 'pi jānāti tadā sarvadvijāgresaraṃ purohitaṃ prāha yathā tvayaiva matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ kathanīyamanyathā tvaṃ deśānnirvāsaṃ prāpnoṣi | purodhāpyetad vacaḥ śrutvā dinapañcakaṃ vyavadhāne yācayitvā saviṣādo gṛhamāgamat | sa purohitaḥ taduttaramajānan purastādrājñā nirvāsyate | sa kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | uttaramapyāha śukaḥ | sa brāhmaṇo viṣādāpannaḥ putryā bālapaṇḍitayā babhāṣe | tāta kathamudvignacitta iva lakṣyase | kathaya viṣādasya kāraṇam | vidvadbhirvipadyapyuccaiḥ sthātavyam |

  • (p.20, l.5)yataḥ |
  • na sauhṛdaṃ na viśvāso na sneho na ca bandhutā | (p.20, l.6)kenāpi saha saṃsāre kuto rājñā chalārthinā || 5.3 (= 32) ||
  • (p.20, l.7)uktaṃ ca |
  • kāke śaucaṃ dyūtakāre ca satyaṃ sarpe kṣāntiḥ strīṣu kāmopaśāntiḥ | (p.20, l.8)klībe dhairyaṃ madyape tattvacintā rājā mitraṃ kena dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā || 5.4 (= 33) ||
  • (p.20, l.9)kiṃ ca |
  • nadīnāṃ nakhināṃ caiva śṛṅgiṇāṃ śastrapāṇinām | (p.20, l.10)viśvāso naiva kartavyaḥ strīṣu rājakuleṣu ca || 5.5 (= 34) ||
  • (p.20, l.11)bhoginaḥ kañcukāsaktāḥ krūrāḥ kuṭilagaminaḥ | (p.20, l.12)duḥkhopasarpaṇīyāśca rājāno bhujagā iva || 5.6 (= 35) ||
  • (p.20, l.13)hasannapi nṛpo hanti mānayannapi durjanaḥ | (p.21, l.1)spṛśannapi gajo hanti jighrannapi bhujaṅgamaḥ || 5.7 (= 36) ||

yataḥ |

na sauhṛdaṃ na viśvāso na sneho na ca bandhutā | kenāpi saha saṃsāre kuto rājñā chalārthinā || 5.3 (= 32) ||

  • (p.22, l.11)dhavalānyātapatrāṇi vājinaśca manoramāḥ | (p.22, l.12)sadā mattāśca mātaṅgāḥ prasanne sati bhūpatau || 5.17 (= 46) ||

tathā ca |

vidyāvatāṃ mahecchānāṃ śilpavikramaśālinām | sevāvṛttividāṃ caiva nāśrayaḥ pārthivaṃ vinā || 5.12 (= 41) ||
ye jātyādimahotsāhā nopagacchanti pārthivam | teṣāmāmaraṇaṃ bhikṣā prāyaścittaṃ vinirmitam || 5.13 (= 42) ||
rogairgrahairnṛpairgrasto yo na vetti jaḍakriyaḥ | madhyamantramupāyaṃ ca so 'vaśyaṃ tāta na sthiraḥ || 5.14 (= 43) ||

uktaṃ ca |

sarpānvyāghrāngajān siṃhāndṛṣṭvopāyairvaśīkṛtān | rājeti kiyatī mātrā dhīmatāmapramādinām || 5.15 (= 44) ||

tathā ca |

rājānameva saṃśritya vidvānyāti paronnatim | vinā malayamanyatra candanaṃ na vivardhate || 5.16 (= 45) ||
dhavalānyātapatrāṇi vājinaśca manoramāḥ | sadā mattāśca mātaṅgāḥ prasanne sati bhūpatau || 5.17 (= 46) ||

(p.22, l.14)viṣādībhava |

p.23, l.2

(p.23, l.2)tato he tāta sthirībhava | matsyahasanottaraṃ rājñaḥ purato mayābhidheyam
(p.23, l.3)iti | snāhi bhuṅkṣva | tataḥ sa evaṃ kṛtvā rājño 'grato gatvā sarvaṃ
(p.23, l.4)nivedayāmāsa | nṛpo 'pi tuṣṭastāmājuhāva | sā āśīrvādaṃ dattvā
(p.23, l.5)rājānamabravīt | rājanmā mudhā viprānviḍambaya | kiṃ tvayā evaṃvidhaṃ
(p.23, l.6)matsyānāṃ hāsyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā | kathaṃ māmabalājanaṃ pṛcchanna vilajjase |

tato he tāta sthirībhava | matsyahasanottaraṃ rājñaḥ purato mayābhidheyam iti | snāhi bhuṅkṣva | tataḥ sa evaṃ kṛtvā rājño 'grato gatvā sarvaṃ nivedayāmāsa | nṛpo 'pi tuṣṭastāmājuhāva | sā āśīrvādaṃ dattvā rājānamabravīt | rājanmā mudhā viprānviḍambaya | kiṃ tvayā evaṃvidhaṃ matsyānāṃ hāsyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā | kathaṃ māmabalājanaṃ pṛcchanna vilajjase |

  • (p.23, l.9)uktaṃ ca |

(p.24, l.11)athāparasmindivase prabhāvatī śukaṃ prāha | śuka sa matsyahāsyavyatikaro

(p.24, l.13)nidrāṃ lebhe |

p.27, l.1

(p.27, l.1)yāvatsa tasya vināyakasya pāṭanāyottiṣṭhati tāvattuṣṭaḥ sanjagāda |
(p.27, l.2)ahaṃ tava pratidinaṃ pañca pañca maṇḍakāndāsye khaṇḍaghṛtayutān | mamālaye
(p.27, l.3)prātaryāyāḥ | paraṃ kasyāpi idaṃ rahasyaṃ na kathanīyam | kathite tu
(p.27, l.4)madvaco vitathaṃ bhaviṣyati | so 'pi ca tatheti pratipadya nityaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ
(p.27, l.5)bhāryāyā arpayati | taddaivaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ ghṛtakhaṇḍayuktamādāya
(p.27, l.6)tadbhāryā nijakuṭumbaṃ tṛptīkaroti | nityaṃ ca tānmaṇḍakāngotriṇāṃ
(p.27, l.7)gṛhe vāhayāmāsa | nijasakhyā mandodaryāstṛptyarthaṃ nityaṃ prāhiṇot |
(p.27, l.8)anyadā sā sakhī tāṃ papraccha | padminyapi maṇḍakāgamanamidaṃ na jānāti |
(p.28, l.1)tatastasyāḥ purā sā sakhī kapaṭādbrūte | sakhi yadi tvaṃ mama purato
(p.28, l.2)guhyaṃ na kathayasi tatkaḥ snehaḥ |

yāvatsa tasya vināyakasya pāṭanāyottiṣṭhati tāvattuṣṭaḥ sanjagāda | ahaṃ tava pratidinaṃ pañca pañca maṇḍakāndāsye khaṇḍaghṛtayutān | mamālaye prātaryāyāḥ | paraṃ kasyāpi idaṃ rahasyaṃ na kathanīyam | kathite tu madvaco vitathaṃ bhaviṣyati | so 'pi ca tatheti pratipadya nityaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ bhāryāyā arpayati | taddaivaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ ghṛtakhaṇḍayuktamādāya tadbhāryā nijakuṭumbaṃ tṛptīkaroti | nityaṃ ca tānmaṇḍakāngotriṇāṃ gṛhe vāhayāmāsa | nijasakhyā mandodaryāstṛptyarthaṃ nityaṃ prāhiṇot | anyadā sā sakhī tāṃ papraccha | padminyapi maṇḍakāgamanamidaṃ na jānāti | tatastasyāḥ purā sā sakhī kapaṭādbrūte | sakhi yadi tvaṃ mama purato guhyaṃ na kathayasi tatkaḥ snehaḥ |

p.29, l.13

(p.29, l.13)sā ca patimukhāt śrutvā sakhīpuro jagāda | tayā cātmapatiḥ kuṭhārahastaḥ
(p.30, l.1)preṣito vināyakapārśve | so 'pi padminīpatiśca prātastatra
(p.30, l.2)jagāma | vināyako 'pi tau dvāvapi mayūrabandhairbandhayāmāsa | so 'pi
(p.30, l.3)ca padminīpatiruktaḥ | re tvadīya evāyamanarthaḥ | tatastvayyeva daṇḍo
(p.30, l.4)yujyate | tataḥ sakhīpatiryayāce | tān pañca maṇḍakān tasmai sa pradadau |
(p.30, l.5)tau dvāvapi svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tataḥ patyā padminī jalpitā |
(p.30, l.6)tvayā te pañcāpi maṇḍakā asmākaṃ spheṭitāḥ etasya dāpitāḥ | paścāttāpaṃ
(p.30, l.7)ca kurute | tatastvamapi rājendra māṃ mā pṛccha | tava paścāttāpo
(p.30, l.8)bhaviṣyati | idaṃ ślokaṃ svayameva vicintaya | iti kathayitvā bālapaṇḍitā
(p.30, l.9)utthāya svagṛhaṃ gatā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.30, l.10)iti śukasaptatau ṣaṣṭhī kathā ||

sā ca patimukhāt śrutvā sakhīpuro jagāda | tayā cātmapatiḥ kuṭhārahastaḥ preṣito vināyakapārśve | so 'pi padminīpatiśca prātastatra jagāma | vināyako 'pi tau dvāvapi mayūrabandhairbandhayāmāsa | so 'pi ca padminīpatiruktaḥ | re tvadīya evāyamanarthaḥ | tatastvayyeva daṇḍo yujyate | tataḥ sakhīpatiryayāce | tān pañca maṇḍakān tasmai sa pradadau | tau dvāvapi svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tataḥ patyā padminī jalpitā | tvayā te pañcāpi maṇḍakā asmākaṃ spheṭitāḥ etasya dāpitāḥ | paścāttāpaṃ ca kurute | tatastvamapi rājendra māṃ mā pṛccha | tava paścāttāpo bhaviṣyati | idaṃ ślokaṃ svayameva vicintaya | iti kathayitvā bālapaṇḍitā utthāya svagṛhaṃ gatā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṣṭhī kathā ||

§ 7

p.31, l.1

(p.31, l.1)anyasmindine prabhāvatī śukaṃ papraccha | kīra punastanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ
(p.31, l.2)rājñā śrutaṃ na vā | śukaḥ prāha | prātaḥ punarbālapaṇḍitāmākārayitvā
(p.31, l.3)rājā prāha | kiṃ tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇam brūhi śīghraṃ bālike |
(p.31, l.4)sā cāha |

anyasmindine prabhāvatī śukaṃ papraccha | kīra punastanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ rājñā śrutaṃ na vā | śukaḥ prāha | prātaḥ punarbālapaṇḍitāmākārayitvā rājā prāha | kiṃ tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇam brūhi śīghraṃ bālike | sā cāha |

p.31, l.5

  • (p.31, l.5)devāgraho na kartavyaḥ paścāttāpo bhaviṣyati | (p.31, l.6)sthagikāsaktacittasya viprasyābhūtpurā yathā || 7.1 (= 65) ||
devāgraho na kartavyaḥ paścāttāpo bhaviṣyati | sthagikāsaktacittasya viprasyābhūtpurā yathā || 7.1 (= 65) ||

p.31, l.7

(p.31, l.7)asti dharaṇītale vatsonanāma paṭṭanam | tatra vīrākhyo rājā | tatra
(p.31, l.8)ca keśavo nāma brāhmaṇaḥ | tena kadāciditi cintitam | yadahaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ
(p.31, l.9)na bhokṣye |

asti dharaṇītale vatsonanāma paṭṭanam | tatra vīrākhyo rājā | tatra ca keśavo nāma brāhmaṇaḥ | tena kadāciditi cintitam | yadahaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ na bhokṣye |

p.32, l.1

  • (p.32, l.1)uktaṃ ca |
  • uttamāḥ svaguṇaiḥ khyātā madhyamāśca piturguṇaiḥ | (p.32, l.2)adhamā mātulaiḥ khyātā śvaśuraiścādhamādhamāḥ || 7.2 (= 66) ||
  • (p.32, l.3)kiṃ ca |
  • piara viḍhattai davvaḍai caḍḍiri ko ṇa karei | (p.32, l.4)saiṃ viḍhavai saiṃ bhojaai viralā jaṇaṇi jaṇei || 7.3 (= 67) || (•)

uktaṃ ca |

uttamāḥ svaguṇaiḥ khyātā madhyamāśca piturguṇaiḥ | adhamā mātulaiḥ khyātā śvaśuraiścādhamādhamāḥ || 7.2 (= 66) ||

kiṃ ca |

piara viḍhattai davvaḍai caḍḍiri ko ṇa karei | saiṃ viḍhavai saiṃ bhojaai viralā jaṇaṇi jaṇei || 7.3 (= 67) || (•)

p.32, l.5

(p.32, l.5)ityavadhārya sa medinyāṃ babhrāma devatīrthaśmaśānanagareṣu dhanārtham |
(p.32, l.6)anyadā sa nirjane pradeśe prasiddhe śivacatvare karālāyāḥ śmaśāne ca
(p.32, l.7)paribhramya pariśrāntaḥ kapilakamaṭhamapaśyat | tatra ca paryaṅkāsanasthaṃ tāpasaṃ
(p.32, l.8)dadarśa | sa ca viprastasyāgre kṛtāñjalipuṭastasthau | tāpaso dhyānaṃ
(p.32, l.9)śanairmuktvā evamuktavān |

ityavadhārya sa medinyāṃ babhrāma devatīrthaśmaśānanagareṣu dhanārtham | anyadā sa nirjane pradeśe prasiddhe śivacatvare karālāyāḥ śmaśāne ca paribhramya pariśrāntaḥ kapilakamaṭhamapaśyat | tatra ca paryaṅkāsanasthaṃ tāpasaṃ dadarśa | sa ca viprastasyāgre kṛtāñjalipuṭastasthau | tāpaso dhyānaṃ śanairmuktvā evamuktavān |

p.33, l.1

  • (p.33, l.1)kiṃ kasmai dīyate loke trāyate ko bhavārṇavāt | (p.33, l.2)asādhyaṃ sādhyate kasya kāle 'sminnatitheraho || 7.4 (= 68) ||
kiṃ kasmai dīyate loke trāyate ko bhavārṇavāt | asādhyaṃ sādhyate kasya kāle 'sminnatitheraho || 7.4 (= 68) ||

p.33, l.3

(p.33, l.3)tataḥ sa brāhmaṇa ūrdhvabāhurjagāda | tavāhamatithirdhanārthī | tāpaso
(p.33, l.4)'pi taṃ vipramalpayācakaṃ dṛṣṭvā manasi duḥkhībabhūva |

tataḥ sa brāhmaṇa ūrdhvabāhurjagāda | tavāhamatithirdhanārthī | tāpaso 'pi taṃ vipramalpayācakaṃ dṛṣṭvā manasi duḥkhībabhūva |

p.33, l.5

  • (p.33, l.5)uktaṃ ca |
  • stokārthaprārthanāndīnāndṛṣṭvodārānhi yācakān | (p.33, l.6)khidyante 'tīva manasi api prāṇapradāyinaḥ || 7.5 (= 69) ||
  • (p.33, l.7)kiṃ ca |
  • ahihūo vi a vivaā karei suaṇo parassa uvaāraṃ | (p.33, l.8)oṇei aṇṇadāvaṃ candaṇataruo sakhaṇḍo vi || 7.6 (= 70) || (•)

uktaṃ ca |

stokārthaprārthanāndīnāndṛṣṭvodārānhi yācakān | khidyante 'tīva manasi api prāṇapradāyinaḥ || 7.5 (= 69) ||

kiṃ ca |

ahihūo vi a vivaā karei suaṇo parassa uvaāraṃ | oṇei aṇṇadāvaṃ candaṇataruo sakhaṇḍo vi || 7.6 (= 70) || (•)

p.34, l.1

(p.34, l.1)tato yogīndra yadā tvametatsparśanaṃ kariṣyasi tadā hemnaḥ pañcaśatāni
(p.34, l.2)nityaṃ dāsyatītyuktvā viprāya paryaṅkīkṛtaṃ sindūramarpayāmāsa | uktaśca |
(p.34, l.3)etattvayānyasmai na dātavyaṃ na kathanīyaṃ ca | anyathā mama samīpe vyāvṛtya
(p.34, l.4)sameṣyati | tadarpitaṃ yadā sa dvijaḥ prātaḥ spṛśati tadā suvarṇaśatapañcakaṃ
(p.34, l.5)dadāti | sa ca ratnāvatīṃ purīṃ gataḥ | tatra sthagikāṃ nāma
(p.34, l.6)veśyāṃ nityaṃ kāmayate | sā ca taddravyāgamanaṃ na jānāti | kuṭṭinī
(p.34, l.7)pṛcchati | hale eṣa vipraḥ kimapi vyavasāyādikaṃ na vidhatte | paraṃ
(p.34, l.8)dravyaṃ kuto 'smākaṃ vitarati kasmādvilasatīti | tato veśyā taṃ pṛcchati |
(p.34, l.9)sa vipraḥ sarvathā na kathayati | tato veśyayā svakalayā bhaktyā
(p.35, l.1)cārādhitaḥ | tataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ san kathayāmāsa yatsindūrāddravyāgamaḥ | tayā
(p.35, l.2)ca suptasya sindūraṃ gṛhītam | tato dravyābhāve kuṭṭinyā gṛhānniḥkāsitaḥ |

tato yogīndra yadā tvametatsparśanaṃ kariṣyasi tadā hemnaḥ pañcaśatāni nityaṃ dāsyatītyuktvā viprāya paryaṅkīkṛtaṃ sindūramarpayāmāsa | uktaśca | etattvayānyasmai na dātavyaṃ na kathanīyaṃ ca | anyathā mama samīpe vyāvṛtya sameṣyati | tadarpitaṃ yadā sa dvijaḥ prātaḥ spṛśati tadā suvarṇaśatapañcakaṃ dadāti | sa ca ratnāvatīṃ purīṃ gataḥ | tatra sthagikāṃ nāma veśyāṃ nityaṃ kāmayate | sā ca taddravyāgamanaṃ na jānāti | kuṭṭinī pṛcchati | hale eṣa vipraḥ kimapi vyavasāyādikaṃ na vidhatte | paraṃ dravyaṃ kuto 'smākaṃ vitarati kasmādvilasatīti | tato veśyā taṃ pṛcchati | sa vipraḥ sarvathā na kathayati | tato veśyayā svakalayā bhaktyā cārādhitaḥ | tataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ san kathayāmāsa yatsindūrāddravyāgamaḥ | tayā ca suptasya sindūraṃ gṛhītam | tato dravyābhāve kuṭṭinyā gṛhānniḥkāsitaḥ |

p.35, l.4

  • (p.35, l.4)uktaṃ ca |
  • viśvāsapratipannānāṃ vañcane kā vidagdhatā | (p.35, l.5)aṅkamāruhya suptaṃ hi hantuṃ kiṃ nāma pauruṣam || 7.7 (= 71) ||

uktaṃ ca |

viśvāsapratipannānāṃ vañcane kā vidagdhatā | aṅkamāruhya suptaṃ hi hantuṃ kiṃ nāma pauruṣam || 7.7 (= 71) ||

p.35, l.5

(p.35, l.5)sa viprastatsindūramapaśyan phūtkurvanrājadvāraṃ yayau muṣito 'hamiti vadan |
(p.35, l.6)tato vivādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | kuṭṭinyāha |

sa viprastatsindūramapaśyan phūtkurvanrājadvāraṃ yayau muṣito 'hamiti vadan | tato vivādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | kuṭṭinyāha |

p.35, l.7

  • (p.35, l.7)dhūrto 'sau matsutālubdho dhanahīno bhavatyasau | (p.35, l.8)manobhavagrahagrasto asamaṃjasamīdṛśam || 7.8 (= 72) ||
  • (p.35, l.9)janairguṇairasaṃbhāvyaṃ rājñā kathaṃ saṃbhāvyate | (p.35, l.10)paraṃ satyamidaṃ jātaṃ sindūraṃ dhanadaṃ yataḥ || 7.9 (= 73) ||
dhūrto 'sau matsutālubdho dhanahīno bhavatyasau | manobhavagrahagrasto asamaṃjasamīdṛśam || 7.8 (= 72) ||
janairguṇairasaṃbhāvyaṃ rājñā kathaṃ saṃbhāvyate | paraṃ satyamidaṃ jātaṃ sindūraṃ dhanadaṃ yataḥ || 7.9 (= 73) ||

p.35, l.11

(p.35, l.11)sa ca janairvaideśiko 'yamiti jñātvā nirvāsitaḥ | tacca sindūraṃ
(p.36, l.1)yogīndrameva yayau | tato rājanvikramāditya sthagikāprītinibandhanāt
(p.36, l.2)tenākhyāte ca sindūre sthagikā naiva viprasya babhūva na ca sindūram |
(p.36, l.3)evaṃ tavāpi rājanratiḥ prītiśca na bhaviṣyati | evamuktvā bālapaṇḍitā
(p.36, l.4)gṛhaṃ jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.36, l.5)iti śukasaptatau saptamī kathā ||

sa ca janairvaideśiko 'yamiti jñātvā nirvāsitaḥ | tacca sindūraṃ yogīndrameva yayau | tato rājanvikramāditya sthagikāprītinibandhanāt tenākhyāte ca sindūre sthagikā naiva viprasya babhūva na ca sindūram | evaṃ tavāpi rājanratiḥ prītiśca na bhaviṣyati | evamuktvā bālapaṇḍitā gṛhaṃ jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptamī kathā ||

§ 8

p.36, l.6

(p.36, l.6)athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka uttaraṃ dadau | devi bālapaṇḍitā
(p.36, l.7)dvitīye 'hni saṃyāte rājānaṃ prāha | deva nāgrahaḥ kartuṃ yujyate |

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka uttaraṃ dadau | devi bālapaṇḍitā dvitīye 'hni saṃyāte rājānaṃ prāha | deva nāgrahaḥ kartuṃ yujyate |

p.36, l.8

  • (p.36, l.8)yataḥ |
  • rājñā naivāgrahaḥ kāryaḥ śubhe vāśubhakarmaṇi | (p.36, l.9)tadaṅgāni hi bhūtāni rājñāṃ hi mahatī tanuḥ || 8.1 (= 74) ||
  • (p.36, l.10)ākhyāte ca tava mayā vaṇikputryā yathābhavat | (p.36, l.11)na bahirna gṛhaṃ rājan tathā te 'pi bhaviṣyati || 8.2 (= 75) ||

yataḥ |

rājñā naivāgrahaḥ kāryaḥ śubhe vāśubhakarmaṇi | tadaṅgāni hi bhūtāni rājñāṃ hi mahatī tanuḥ || 8.1 (= 74) ||
ākhyāte ca tava mayā vaṇikputryā yathābhavat | na bahirna gṛhaṃ rājan tathā te 'pi bhaviṣyati || 8.2 (= 75) ||

p.37, l.1

(p.37, l.1)rājā pṛcchati | kathametat | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | asti pṛthvītale
(p.37, l.2)tripuraṃ nāma sthānam | tasmin trivikramo nāma rājā | tatra sundarābhidhāno
(p.37, l.3)vaṇik | tadbhāryā subhagā nāma atīva kulaṭā | sā ca
(p.37, l.4)bhartrā gṛhānniryāntī prayatnena niyantritā | tāṃ ca niyantraṇātpūrvameko
(p.37, l.5)vaṇigyakṣagṛhe sthitaḥ sakāmāmabhajat | yadā ca bahirnirgacchantī patinā
(p.37, l.6)nivāritā tadā sakhīṃ prāha | sakhi adya tvayā sa mānavo yakṣāyatane
(p.37, l.7)ākāraṇīyaḥ yathāhaṃ tatra gatvā taṃ rame | tvayā ca mayi gatāyāṃ
(p.37, l.8)paścādasmadgṛhaṃ jvālanīyaṃ yathā gṛhakāryāsakto jano māṃ gatāṃ na
(p.37, l.9)jānāti | atrāntare 'haṃ taṃ svecchayā bhuktā samupāgacchāmi | tataḥ
(p.37, l.10)sakhīvacanātsa pumān tatrāyātaḥ | sāpyāgatā | tadā ca gatāyāṃ tasyāṃ
(p.38, l.1)sā sakhī tadgṛhaṃ prajvālitavatī | sa pumān prajvalane kutūhalī yakṣāyatanaṃ
(p.38, l.2)muktvā tatrāvalokanāya gataḥ | sā ca tatra sthitāsamāptātmaprayojanā
(p.38, l.3)yāvatā gṛhamāgatā tāvatā gṛhaṃ dagdham |

rājā pṛcchati | kathametat | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | asti pṛthvītale tripuraṃ nāma sthānam | tasmin trivikramo nāma rājā | tatra sundarābhidhāno vaṇik | tadbhāryā subhagā nāma atīva kulaṭā | sā ca bhartrā gṛhānniryāntī prayatnena niyantritā | tāṃ ca niyantraṇātpūrvameko vaṇigyakṣagṛhe sthitaḥ sakāmāmabhajat | yadā ca bahirnirgacchantī patinā nivāritā tadā sakhīṃ prāha | sakhi adya tvayā sa mānavo yakṣāyatane ākāraṇīyaḥ yathāhaṃ tatra gatvā taṃ rame | tvayā ca mayi gatāyāṃ paścādasmadgṛhaṃ jvālanīyaṃ yathā gṛhakāryāsakto jano māṃ gatāṃ na jānāti | atrāntare 'haṃ taṃ svecchayā bhuktā samupāgacchāmi | tataḥ sakhīvacanātsa pumān tatrāyātaḥ | sāpyāgatā | tadā ca gatāyāṃ tasyāṃ sā sakhī tadgṛhaṃ prajvālitavatī | sa pumān prajvalane kutūhalī yakṣāyatanaṃ muktvā tatrāvalokanāya gataḥ | sā ca tatra sthitāsamāptātmaprayojanā yāvatā gṛhamāgatā tāvatā gṛhaṃ dagdham |

p.38, l.4

  • (p.38, l.4)na gṛhaṃ na bahirbhūpa vaṇigvadhvā yathābhavat | (p.38, l.5)tathā tava mahārāja bhaviṣyati suniścayam || 8.3 (= 76) ||
na gṛhaṃ na bahirbhūpa vaṇigvadhvā yathābhavat | tathā tava mahārāja bhaviṣyati suniścayam || 8.3 (= 76) ||

p.38, l.6

(p.38, l.6)atha cet jñātena ślokārthena prayojanaṃ tadā kalye svayameva jñāpayiṣyāmi |
(p.38, l.7)ityuktvā sā gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā ||
(p.38, l.8)iti śukasaptatau aṣṭamī kathā ||

atha cet jñātena ślokārthena prayojanaṃ tadā kalye svayameva jñāpayiṣyāmi | ityuktvā sā gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau aṣṭamī kathā ||

§ 9

p.38, l.9

(p.38, l.9)athāparedyuḥ savismayā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati sma | śuka kiṃ vijñātaṃ
(p.39, l.1)vikramārkeṇa matsyahasanakāraṇam | śukaḥ prāha | devi na kimapi rājñā
(p.39, l.2)svayaṃ jñātam | tato rājā prātardvijasutāmāhūya bālapaṇḍitāṃ prāha |
(p.39, l.3)tvayā ityuktaṃ yattvaṃ svayameva jñāsyasi | mayā tu kimapi na jñātam |
(p.39, l.4)bālapaṇḍitā prāha | yadi rājannevamapi mayā kathyamānaṃ na vetsi
(p.39, l.5)tataḥ śṛṇu | puṣpahāso nāma mantrī sarvamantriṇāmagraṇīrnirdoṣo guptaḥ |
(p.39, l.6)kimiti niyantrito 'sti | rājā prāha | anvartho 'yaṃ puṣpahāsaḥ |
(p.39, l.7)yataḥ | yadāsau madīyāyāṃ saṃsadi hasati tadāsyāsyātpuṣpaprakaro
(p.39, l.8)nipatati | iyaṃ ca kathāpararājyamaṇḍaleṣu khyātābhūt | tatastaiḥ preṣitāḥ
(p.39, l.9)svīyapumāṃsaḥ kutūhalānveṣaṇāya | teṣu samāyāteṣu tena na hasitaṃ puṣpaprakaro
(p.39, l.10)'pi nābhūt | iti kāraṇāt guptibandhaḥ | bālapaṇḍitā prāha |
(p.40, l.1)kenāpi kāraṇena mantriṇā na hasitam | rājan tatkāraṇaṃ tvayā jñātaṃ
(p.40, l.2)na vā | rājā prāha | mayā kimapi na jñātam | bālapaṇḍitā
(p.40, l.3)prāha | tarhi kathamidaṃ daṇḍaṃ kurvan pāpabhāk na bhavasi |

athāparedyuḥ savismayā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati sma | śuka kiṃ vijñātaṃ vikramārkeṇa matsyahasanakāraṇam | śukaḥ prāha | devi na kimapi rājñā svayaṃ jñātam | tato rājā prātardvijasutāmāhūya bālapaṇḍitāṃ prāha | tvayā ityuktaṃ yattvaṃ svayameva jñāsyasi | mayā tu kimapi na jñātam | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | yadi rājannevamapi mayā kathyamānaṃ na vetsi tataḥ śṛṇu | puṣpahāso nāma mantrī sarvamantriṇāmagraṇīrnirdoṣo guptaḥ | kimiti niyantrito 'sti | rājā prāha | anvartho 'yaṃ puṣpahāsaḥ | yataḥ | yadāsau madīyāyāṃ saṃsadi hasati tadāsyāsyātpuṣpaprakaro nipatati | iyaṃ ca kathāpararājyamaṇḍaleṣu khyātābhūt | tatastaiḥ preṣitāḥ svīyapumāṃsaḥ kutūhalānveṣaṇāya | teṣu samāyāteṣu tena na hasitaṃ puṣpaprakaro 'pi nābhūt | iti kāraṇāt guptibandhaḥ | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | kenāpi kāraṇena mantriṇā na hasitam | rājan tatkāraṇaṃ tvayā jñātaṃ na vā | rājā prāha | mayā kimapi na jñātam | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | tarhi kathamidaṃ daṇḍaṃ kurvan pāpabhāk na bhavasi |

p.40, l.4

  • (p.40, l.4)uktaṃ ca |
  • dharmeṇa rāṣṭraṃ vindeta dharmeṇaivānupālayet | (p.40, l.5)dharmāc charaṇyatāṃ yāti rājā sarvabhayāpahaḥ || 9.1 (= 77) ||

uktaṃ ca |

dharmeṇa rāṣṭraṃ vindeta dharmeṇaivānupālayet | dharmāc charaṇyatāṃ yāti rājā sarvabhayāpahaḥ || 9.1 (= 77) ||

p.40, l.6

(p.40, l.6)yathā āgrahānmāṃ matsyahāsakāraṇaṃ pṛcchasi tathā tamapi pṛccha hāsyakāraṇam |
(p.40, l.7)sa evātmīyahāsyasya matsyahāsyasya ca kāraṇaṃ vaktā | rājāpi
(p.40, l.8)tadvacanātpuṣpahāsaṃ mantriṇaṃ vastradānapūrvaṃ mantripade pratiṣṭhāpya
(p.40, l.9)matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ papraccha | mantryāha | yadyapi gṛhaduścaritamakathyam |

yathā āgrahānmāṃ matsyahāsakāraṇaṃ pṛcchasi tathā tamapi pṛccha hāsyakāraṇam | sa evātmīyahāsyasya matsyahāsyasya ca kāraṇaṃ vaktā | rājāpi tadvacanātpuṣpahāsaṃ mantriṇaṃ vastradānapūrvaṃ mantripade pratiṣṭhāpya matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ papraccha | mantryāha | yadyapi gṛhaduścaritamakathyam |

p.41, l.6

(p.41, l.6)tato rājanme kalatraṃ narāntararataṃ jātaṃ tacca mayā jñātam | tena ca
(p.41, l.7)duḥkhena na hasitaḥ | rājāpīdamākarṇya puṣpahastakai rājñīmāhatya saṃmukham
(p.41, l.8)avalokayāmāsa | sā ca tena prahāreṇa kapaṭamūrcchāṃ nāṭayati sma |
(p.41, l.9)puṣpahāso 'pi tāmavalokya sahāso babhūva puṣpotkaraśca samajani |
(p.41, l.10)rājāpi tāmāśvāsya kṛtakopo dvijātmajāsyaṃ vilokya mantriṇamavādīt |
(p.41, l.11)kathamasmadduḥkhe sahāso 'si | mantryapi sabhayamañjaliṃ baddhvābhāṣata |
(p.42, l.1)rājan poṭakajanaistvadīyā rājñī rātrau nāḍikābhirāhatāpi na
(p.42, l.2)mūrcchitā adhunā mūrcchiteti hāsyam | rājāpi sakopo mantrinnidaṃ
(p.42, l.3)tvayā dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ veti papraccha | mantryāha | svāmindṛṣṭamevedam | yadi
(p.42, l.4)svāmī na pratyeti tadā kañcukamuttāryāvalokayatu | evaṃ kṛte rājā
(p.42, l.5)sarvamajñāsīt | mantriṇo dvijasutāyāśca mukhamavalokya kimidamityavādīt |
(p.42, l.6)mantryāha | svāminyadidaṃ dvijaputryā gūḍhārthaṃ matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ
(p.42, l.7)niveditaṃ tanmayā prakaṭīkṛtam | ityevamukto rājā āsthānaṃ vyasarjayat |
(p.42, l.8)atha dvijasutāpuṣpahāsāvapi bhītahṛṣṭau svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ |
(p.42, l.9)tena ca rājñā tasyā mañjūṣāsthito naro dṛṣṭo vināśitaḥ | sā ca
(p.42, l.10)nijavāsādvisarjitā | śukaḥ prabhāvatīmāha |

tato rājanme kalatraṃ narāntararataṃ jātaṃ tacca mayā jñātam | tena ca duḥkhena na hasitaḥ | rājāpīdamākarṇya puṣpahastakai rājñīmāhatya saṃmukham avalokayāmāsa | sā ca tena prahāreṇa kapaṭamūrcchāṃ nāṭayati sma | puṣpahāso 'pi tāmavalokya sahāso babhūva puṣpotkaraśca samajani | rājāpi tāmāśvāsya kṛtakopo dvijātmajāsyaṃ vilokya mantriṇamavādīt | kathamasmadduḥkhe sahāso 'si | mantryapi sabhayamañjaliṃ baddhvābhāṣata | rājan poṭakajanaistvadīyā rājñī rātrau nāḍikābhirāhatāpi na mūrcchitā adhunā mūrcchiteti hāsyam | rājāpi sakopo mantrinnidaṃ tvayā dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ veti papraccha | mantryāha | svāmindṛṣṭamevedam | yadi svāmī na pratyeti tadā kañcukamuttāryāvalokayatu | evaṃ kṛte rājā sarvamajñāsīt | mantriṇo dvijasutāyāśca mukhamavalokya kimidamityavādīt | mantryāha | svāminyadidaṃ dvijaputryā gūḍhārthaṃ matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ niveditaṃ tanmayā prakaṭīkṛtam | ityevamukto rājā āsthānaṃ vyasarjayat | atha dvijasutāpuṣpahāsāvapi bhītahṛṣṭau svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tena ca rājñā tasyā mañjūṣāsthito naro dṛṣṭo vināśitaḥ | sā ca nijavāsādvisarjitā | śukaḥ prabhāvatīmāha |

p.44, l.1

(p.44, l.7)iti śukasaptatau daśamī kathā ||

(p.46, l.5)tataḥ sa tadantikamāgatya jagāda | bhadre kiṃ vidheyam | sāha | tvayā
(p.46, l.6)mama pṛṣṭhalagnena asmadgṛhaṃ samāgantavyaṃ mama patyuśca namaskāro vidheyaḥ |
(p.46, l.7)sarvamanyadahaṃ kariṣye | tvayā tathaiveti vācyam | evamuktvā sā gṛhaṃ
(p.46, l.8)praviṣṭā | so 'pi gṛhaṃ praviṣṭastatpatyuragre tasthau | patirapi vismitaḥ |
(p.47, l.1)tataḥ sā kumbhaṃ muktvā patyuḥ sakāśamāgatyābravīt | nātha upalakṣasvainam |
(p.47, l.2)sa āha | na vedmīti | tataḥ sā prāha | ayaṃ mātṛsvasuḥ suto yo
(p.47, l.3)mayā śiśutve muktaḥ | sa dhavalo nāma mama milanārthaṃ samāgamat |
(p.47, l.4)tato mayā āliṅgya sarvāpi svajanavārttā pṛṣṭā | sa ca brāhmaṇa evam
(p.47, l.5)iti jalpati | tataḥ patinā sānujñātā taṃ mahānasaṃ nītvā bhojanacchādanasaṃskārais
(p.47, l.6)toṣayāmāsa | patirapi tuṣṭaḥ prāha | bhadre tvayā
(p.47, l.7)nijabāndhavasya mahatī bhaktiḥ kāryetyuktvā suptaḥ | tadā ca rambhikā
(p.47, l.8)brāhmaṇakhaṭvāmupāviśat | tatastenoktam | tvayā patyuragre ityuktaṃ yanmadīyo
(p.47, l.9)bhrātā samāgataḥ | tattvaṃ me pratipannā bhaginī pratipannaṃ ca
(p.47, l.10)nirvāhyate |

tataḥ sa tadantikamāgatya jagāda | bhadre kiṃ vidheyam | sāha | tvayā mama pṛṣṭhalagnena asmadgṛhaṃ samāgantavyaṃ mama patyuśca namaskāro vidheyaḥ | sarvamanyadahaṃ kariṣye | tvayā tathaiveti vācyam | evamuktvā sā gṛhaṃ praviṣṭā | so 'pi gṛhaṃ praviṣṭastatpatyuragre tasthau | patirapi vismitaḥ | tataḥ sā kumbhaṃ muktvā patyuḥ sakāśamāgatyābravīt | nātha upalakṣasvainam | sa āha | na vedmīti | tataḥ sā prāha | ayaṃ mātṛsvasuḥ suto yo mayā śiśutve muktaḥ | sa dhavalo nāma mama milanārthaṃ samāgamat | tato mayā āliṅgya sarvāpi svajanavārttā pṛṣṭā | sa ca brāhmaṇa evam iti jalpati | tataḥ patinā sānujñātā taṃ mahānasaṃ nītvā bhojanacchādanasaṃskārais toṣayāmāsa | patirapi tuṣṭaḥ prāha | bhadre tvayā nijabāndhavasya mahatī bhaktiḥ kāryetyuktvā suptaḥ | tadā ca rambhikā brāhmaṇakhaṭvāmupāviśat | tatastenoktam | tvayā patyuragre ityuktaṃ yanmadīyo bhrātā samāgataḥ | tattvaṃ me pratipannā bhaginī pratipannaṃ ca nirvāhyate |

  • (p.49, l.5)śrūyate rukmiṇī pūrvaṃ kṛṣṇena madanāturā | (p.49, l.6)gṛhītā bhrātṛjāyāpi kaḥ kāmamatilaṅghayet || 11.13 (= 95) ||
  • (p.49, l.7)virañcirapi kāmārtaḥ svasutāmabhilāṣukaḥ | (p.49, l.8)dṛśyate 'dyāpi viyati hāriṇīṃ tanumāśritaḥ || 11.14 (= 96) ||

  • (p.49, l.11)tayaivaṃ bodhito mūrkhaḥ sa yāvadramate na tām | (p.49, l.12)phūtkṛtaṃ muṣitāsmīti trāyatāṃ trāyatāmaho || 11.16 (= 98) ||

uktaṃ ca |

kāmārtāṃ svayamāyātāṃ yo na bhuṅkte nitambinīm | so 'vaśyaṃ narakaṃ yāti tanniḥśvāsahato naraḥ || 11.10 (= 92) ||
so kiṃva māṇai para mahila jo ṇavi jaṃpi emva | ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● || 11.11 (= 93) || (•)
jo ṇavi māṇai ● ● ● ● so kiṃva māṇai thī avarā i | ● ● ● ● ● ● mā kari ṇeha amhahaṃ bhaṅgu || 11.12 (= 94) || (•)
śrūyate rukmiṇī pūrvaṃ kṛṣṇena madanāturā | gṛhītā bhrātṛjāyāpi kaḥ kāmamatilaṅghayet || 11.13 (= 95) ||
virañcirapi kāmārtaḥ svasutāmabhilāṣukaḥ | dṛśyate 'dyāpi viyati hāriṇīṃ tanumāśritaḥ || 11.14 (= 96) ||
vivāhe pārvatīṃ dṛṣṭvā harasya haravallabhām | caskanda retastasyāpi bālakhilyāstadudbhavāḥ || 11.15 (= 97) ||
tayaivaṃ bodhito mūrkhaḥ sa yāvadramate na tām | phūtkṛtaṃ muṣitāsmīti trāyatāṃ trāyatāmaho || 11.16 (= 98) ||

p.50, l.1

(p.50, l.1)tayā ca phūtkṛte kimidamiti kurvāṇo bāndhavaiḥ saha dhāvito bhartā |
(p.50, l.2)sa ca kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | evaṃ ca sa brāhmaṇaḥ
(p.50, l.3)sabhayaḥ san tatpādayoḥ patito jagāda | svāmini prāṇānrakṣa | tavehitaṃ
(p.50, l.4)kariṣyāmi | evaṃ sthite sā dugdhasahitaṃ bhaktamaḍhaṃḍholayat antike
(p.50, l.5)jvalinamajvālayat āgataṃ ca patiṃ jagāda | asya viṣūcikā utpannā |
(p.50, l.6)tato mayā phūtkṛtam | evamuktvā dugdhabhaktaṃ pradarśitam | patirapi
(p.50, l.7)mūrkho dṛṣṭvā yayau | tataḥ sā patyau supte yadṛcchayā surataṃ cakāra |
(p.50, l.8)so 'pi ca māndyavyājānmāsamekaṃ sthitaḥ paścājjagāma | iti śrutvā
(p.50, l.9)prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.50, l.10)iti śukasaptatau ekādaśī kathā ||

tayā ca phūtkṛte kimidamiti kurvāṇo bāndhavaiḥ saha dhāvito bhartā | sa ca kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | evaṃ ca sa brāhmaṇaḥ sabhayaḥ san tatpādayoḥ patito jagāda | svāmini prāṇānrakṣa | tavehitaṃ kariṣyāmi | evaṃ sthite sā dugdhasahitaṃ bhaktamaḍhaṃḍholayat antike jvalinamajvālayat āgataṃ ca patiṃ jagāda | asya viṣūcikā utpannā | tato mayā phūtkṛtam | evamuktvā dugdhabhaktaṃ pradarśitam | patirapi mūrkho dṛṣṭvā yayau | tataḥ sā patyau supte yadṛcchayā surataṃ cakāra | so 'pi ca māndyavyājānmāsamekaṃ sthitaḥ paścājjagāma | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekādaśī kathā ||

p.51, l.4

(p.51, l.4)astyatra nalauḍāgrāme kulālo mahādhanaḥ | tasya bhāryā śobhikā
(p.51, l.5)nāma paraṃ kulaṭā naralampaṭā ca | sā patyau bahirgate upapatisahitā
(p.51, l.6)gṛhāntaḥ krīḍati | tasyāścaivaṃ sthitāyā bhartā gṛhaṃ samāgamat |
(p.51, l.7)tadanantaraṃ sā kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ |
(p.51, l.8)śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā sa
(p.51, l.9)āgacchanjñātastadā upapatiruktaḥ | caṭa tvaṃ vavvūlavṛkṣam | evaṃ ca sa
(p.51, l.10)tayā proktastathā cakāra | tasya ca vṛkṣe caṭataḥ paridhānavastraṃ vilagnaṃ
(p.51, l.11)nagno 'pi vṛkṣamārūḍhaḥ | tasmiṃśca vṛkṣamārūḍhe patiḥ prāha | kimidamiti |
(p.52, l.1)sā āha | ayaṃ śatrubhirabhibhūto 'dho vastramapi tyaktvā vavvūlamadhirūḍhaḥ |
(p.52, l.2)tataḥ samāgatya tasyāḥ patinā vṛkṣānmandaṃ mandamuttārya sa svagṛhaṃ
(p.52, l.3)preṣitaḥ | tayā dhūrtayā ca saha hastatālaṃ hasitam | iti kathāṃ śrutvā
(p.52, l.4)prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.52, l.5)iti śukasaptatau dvādaśī kathā ||

astyatra nalauḍāgrāme kulālo mahādhanaḥ | tasya bhāryā śobhikā nāma paraṃ kulaṭā naralampaṭā ca | sā patyau bahirgate upapatisahitā gṛhāntaḥ krīḍati | tasyāścaivaṃ sthitāyā bhartā gṛhaṃ samāgamat | tadanantaraṃ sā kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā sa āgacchanjñātastadā upapatiruktaḥ | caṭa tvaṃ vavvūlavṛkṣam | evaṃ ca sa tayā proktastathā cakāra | tasya ca vṛkṣe caṭataḥ paridhānavastraṃ vilagnaṃ nagno 'pi vṛkṣamārūḍhaḥ | tasmiṃśca vṛkṣamārūḍhe patiḥ prāha | kimidamiti | sā āha | ayaṃ śatrubhirabhibhūto 'dho vastramapi tyaktvā vavvūlamadhirūḍhaḥ | tataḥ samāgatya tasyāḥ patinā vṛkṣānmandaṃ mandamuttārya sa svagṛhaṃ preṣitaḥ | tayā dhūrtayā ca saha hastatālaṃ hasitam | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvādaśī kathā ||

p.52, l.9

(p.52, l.9)asti nāgapuraṃ nāma sthānam | yatraiko vaṇik | tatpatnī rājikānāmnī
(p.52, l.10)surūpā paraṃ duścāriṇī | vaṇiksutaśca tāṃ narāntarāsaktāṃ na
(p.52, l.11)jānāti | tataśca ekadā sa bhojanāya yadopaviṣṭastadā upapatiḥ kṛtasaṃketo
(p.52, l.12)mārge gacchan tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā gṛhe 'dya ghṛtaṃ nāsti ityuktvā
(p.53, l.1)dravyaṃ tatsakāśādādāya ghṛtānayanadambhena veśmato nirgatya ca sā bahir
(p.53, l.2)jāreṇa saha ciraṃ sthitā | patistu gṛhe kṣudhārtaḥ kruddhaśca | tataḥ sā
(p.53, l.3)kathaṃ gṛhaṃ gantumarhati | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | tataḥ sā hastau pādau
(p.53, l.4)mukhaṃ ca dhūlidhūsaraṃ vidhāya sadrammā dhūliṃ gṛhītvā gṛhamāgatā |
(p.53, l.5)patiḥ kruddho raktekṣaṇaḥ kimidamityāha | sā ca saniḥśvāsaṃ rudatī
(p.53, l.6)dhūlipuñjaṃ darśayitvā idamuvāca | yatkṛte tvaṃ kruddhaḥ sa te dravyo 'tra
(p.53, l.7)dhūlyāṃ patitaḥ | enāmutkṣipya gṛhāṇa tvam | evamuktaḥ sa vilakṣaḥ
(p.53, l.8)tadaṅgāni vastrāñcalena saṃmārjya sāntvayāmāsa vividhalālanaiḥ | iti
(p.53, l.9)kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.53, l.10)iti śukasaptatau trayodaśī kathā ||

asti nāgapuraṃ nāma sthānam | yatraiko vaṇik | tatpatnī rājikānāmnī surūpā paraṃ duścāriṇī | vaṇiksutaśca tāṃ narāntarāsaktāṃ na jānāti | tataśca ekadā sa bhojanāya yadopaviṣṭastadā upapatiḥ kṛtasaṃketo mārge gacchan tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā gṛhe 'dya ghṛtaṃ nāsti ityuktvā dravyaṃ tatsakāśādādāya ghṛtānayanadambhena veśmato nirgatya ca sā bahir jāreṇa saha ciraṃ sthitā | patistu gṛhe kṣudhārtaḥ kruddhaśca | tataḥ sā kathaṃ gṛhaṃ gantumarhati | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | tataḥ sā hastau pādau mukhaṃ ca dhūlidhūsaraṃ vidhāya sadrammā dhūliṃ gṛhītvā gṛhamāgatā | patiḥ kruddho raktekṣaṇaḥ kimidamityāha | sā ca saniḥśvāsaṃ rudatī dhūlipuñjaṃ darśayitvā idamuvāca | yatkṛte tvaṃ kruddhaḥ sa te dravyo 'tra dhūlyāṃ patitaḥ | enāmutkṣipya gṛhāṇa tvam | evamuktaḥ sa vilakṣaḥ tadaṅgāni vastrāñcalena saṃmārjya sāntvayāmāsa vividhalālanaiḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau trayodaśī kathā ||

(p.56, l.1)tayottaraṃ vicintyoktam | nātha tvayā tāvadgṛhadvāri sthīyatāṃ yāvatsarvaṃ
(p.56, l.2)sajjaṃ vidhīyate | tena caivaṃ pratipanne sā madhye gatvā bhaṭṭārikāṃ pūjayitvā

(p.56, l.9)suptā |
(p.56, l.10)iti śukasaptatau caturdaśī kathā ||

tatastvamapi kuru vayaḥsāphalyamityukte dhanaśrīrjagāda | nāhaṃ vilambituṃ sahāmi | yattvayā bhavati tat śīghraṃ vidhehi | tatastayā sā narāntareṇa yojitā | yadā ca sā tenātmāsaktā jñātā tadā tadīyaśiroveṇī chinnā | tatkāle ca patirdeśāntarādājagāma | tadā sā kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca patirgṛhadvāramāyayau tadā tayottaraṃ vicintyoktam | nātha tvayā tāvadgṛhadvāri sthīyatāṃ yāvatsarvaṃ sajjaṃ vidhīyate | tena caivaṃ pratipanne sā madhye gatvā bhaṭṭārikāṃ pūjayitvā purato veṇīṃ sthāpayāmāsa | evaṃ kṛtvā bahirnirgatya caraṇamaṇḍakaiḥ patiṃ gṛhāntardevīpurato nītvā jagāda | nātha pūjaya gṛhādhidevatām | tena pūjayatā veṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā uktam | kimidamiti | tayoktam | mayopayācitamāsīt | yadā me patiḥ sameṣyati tadā svāminyahaṃ tavāgre veṇīṃ chetsyāmi | tadadhunā mayā kṛtam | sa ca mugdho devīṃ namaskṛtya tāṃ bahumānayāmāsa | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau caturdaśī kathā ||

  • mahilārattā purisā cheā vi ṇa saṃbharanti appāṇaṃ | (p.57, l.8)iare uṇa taruṇīṇaṃ purisā salilaṃ va hatthagaaṃ || 15.3 (= 109) || (•)

uktaṃ ca |

rattā picchanti guṇā dosā picchanti je viratta tti | majjhatthā uṇa purisā dosā vi guṇā vi picchanti || 15.2 (= 108) || (•)

kiṃ ca |

mahilārattā purisā cheā vi ṇa saṃbharanti appāṇaṃ | iare uṇa taruṇīṇaṃ purisā salilaṃ va hatthagaaṃ || 15.3 (= 109) || (•)

p.58, l.1

(p.58, l.1)anyadā sā śvaśureṇa narāntarasahitā suptā dṛṣṭā | tataścaraṇānnūpuraṃ
(p.58, l.2)śvaśureṇa cottāritaṃ tayā ca jñātam | tataḥ sā taṃ jāraṃ prasthāpya
(p.58, l.3)bhartāraṃ tatrānīya tena saha suptā | nidrāntare ca patirutthāpitaḥ kathitaṃ
(p.58, l.4)ca | tvadīyena pitrā nūpuramasmatpadādavatārya gṛhītam | evaṃvidhaṃ
(p.58, l.5)ca pātakaṃ kvāpi na dṛṣṭaṃ yadvadhūpādāt śvaśuro nūpuraṃ gṛhṇāti | tenoktam |
(p.58, l.6)prātaḥ pituḥ sakāśātsvayamarpayiṣyāmi | tena ca guṇākareṇa
(p.58, l.7)pitaraṃ nirbhartsya tatsakāśānnūpuraṃ yācitam | pitrā coktam | yadiyaṃ
(p.58, l.8)parapuruṣeṇa saha suptā dṛṣṭā ato mayā nūpuraṃ gṛhītam | tayoktam |
(p.58, l.9)tvatputreṇa saha suptāhamāsam | ityarthe divyaṃ karomi | atraiva grāme
(p.58, l.10)uttarasyāṃ diśi yakṣo 'sti | tasya jaṅghāntarānnirgamiṣyāmi | yaḥ
(p.58, l.11)kaścitsatyo bhavati sa jaṅghayorantarānniṣkrāmyatīti prasiddham | evaṃ
(p.59, l.1)śvaśureṇa cāṅgīkṛte sā kulaṭāsati dine jārasya gṛhe gatvā tamuvāca |
(p.59, l.2)bhoḥ kānta prātarahaṃ divyārthaṃ yakṣasya jaṅghāntarānnirgamiṣyāmi | tvayā
(p.59, l.3)tatra samāgatya vātūlatvamāśritya mama kaṇṭhagraho vidheyaḥ | tena ca
(p.59, l.4)tathokte sā svagṛhamājagāma | atha prātaḥ samastamahājanaṃ melayitvā
(p.59, l.5)puṣpākṣatādikamādāya yakṣāyatane gatvā samīpasarasi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣapūjārthaṃ
(p.59, l.6)samāgacchantyāstasyāḥ pūrvasaṃketito jāro grahilībhūtastatkaṇṭhe
(p.59, l.7)nijabāhudvayaṃ yojayāmāsa | tata āḥ kimetadityabhidhāya sā punaḥ
(p.59, l.8)snānārthaṃ yayau | so 'pi grahilo lokaiḥ kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā tasmātpradeśād
(p.59, l.9)dūrīkṛtaḥ | sāpi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣasamīpamāgatya puṣpagandhādyairabhyarcya
(p.59, l.10)sarvalokānāṃ śṛṇvatāmuvāca | bho bhagavanyakṣa nijabhartāramenaṃ ca grahilaṃ
(p.59, l.11)vinā yadyanyapuruṣaḥ spṛśati kadācana māṃ tadā tava jaṅghābhyāṃ sakāśān
(p.59, l.12)mama niṣkramaṇaṃ mā bhavatvityabhidhāya sarvalokasamakṣameva jaṅghayormadhye
(p.59, l.13)praviśya niṣkrāntā | yakṣo 'pi tadbuddhiṃ manasi ślāghamāna eva sthitaḥ |
(p.59, l.14)sāpi satīti samastalokaiḥ pūjitā svabhavanaṃ jagāma | evaṃ cet śriyādevīvat
(p.59, l.15)kartuṃ jānāsi tadā vraja | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.59, l.16)iti śukasaptatau pañcadaśī kathā ||

anyadā sā śvaśureṇa narāntarasahitā suptā dṛṣṭā | tataścaraṇānnūpuraṃ śvaśureṇa cottāritaṃ tayā ca jñātam | tataḥ sā taṃ jāraṃ prasthāpya bhartāraṃ tatrānīya tena saha suptā | nidrāntare ca patirutthāpitaḥ kathitaṃ ca | tvadīyena pitrā nūpuramasmatpadādavatārya gṛhītam | evaṃvidhaṃ ca pātakaṃ kvāpi na dṛṣṭaṃ yadvadhūpādāt śvaśuro nūpuraṃ gṛhṇāti | tenoktam | prātaḥ pituḥ sakāśātsvayamarpayiṣyāmi | tena ca guṇākareṇa pitaraṃ nirbhartsya tatsakāśānnūpuraṃ yācitam | pitrā coktam | yadiyaṃ parapuruṣeṇa saha suptā dṛṣṭā ato mayā nūpuraṃ gṛhītam | tayoktam | tvatputreṇa saha suptāhamāsam | ityarthe divyaṃ karomi | atraiva grāme uttarasyāṃ diśi yakṣo 'sti | tasya jaṅghāntarānnirgamiṣyāmi | yaḥ kaścitsatyo bhavati sa jaṅghayorantarānniṣkrāmyatīti prasiddham | evaṃ śvaśureṇa cāṅgīkṛte sā kulaṭāsati dine jārasya gṛhe gatvā tamuvāca | bhoḥ kānta prātarahaṃ divyārthaṃ yakṣasya jaṅghāntarānnirgamiṣyāmi | tvayā tatra samāgatya vātūlatvamāśritya mama kaṇṭhagraho vidheyaḥ | tena ca tathokte sā svagṛhamājagāma | atha prātaḥ samastamahājanaṃ melayitvā puṣpākṣatādikamādāya yakṣāyatane gatvā samīpasarasi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣapūjārthaṃ samāgacchantyāstasyāḥ pūrvasaṃketito jāro grahilībhūtastatkaṇṭhe nijabāhudvayaṃ yojayāmāsa | tata āḥ kimetadityabhidhāya sā punaḥ snānārthaṃ yayau | so 'pi grahilo lokaiḥ kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā tasmātpradeśād dūrīkṛtaḥ | sāpi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣasamīpamāgatya puṣpagandhādyairabhyarcya sarvalokānāṃ śṛṇvatāmuvāca | bho bhagavanyakṣa nijabhartāramenaṃ ca grahilaṃ vinā yadyanyapuruṣaḥ spṛśati kadācana māṃ tadā tava jaṅghābhyāṃ sakāśān mama niṣkramaṇaṃ mā bhavatvityabhidhāya sarvalokasamakṣameva jaṅghayormadhye praviśya niṣkrāntā | yakṣo 'pi tadbuddhiṃ manasi ślāghamāna eva sthitaḥ | sāpi satīti samastalokaiḥ pūjitā svabhavanaṃ jagāma | evaṃ cet śriyādevīvat kartuṃ jānāsi tadā vraja | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcadaśī kathā ||

p.60, l.5

(p.60, l.5)tac chrutvā prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | so 'bravīt | asti vidiśā nāma
(p.60, l.6)purī | tasyāṃ janavallabho nāma vaṇik | tasya bhāryā mugdhikā nāma
(p.60, l.7)capalā svairiṇī | yadā ca tayātiśayena vidūṣito 'yaṃ tadā bandhūnāṃ
(p.60, l.8)kathayāmāsa yadiyaṃ bahiḥ śāyinī | yadā ca tairevamuktā tadā tayāpy
(p.60, l.9)uktam | ayameva bahiḥśāyī sadaiva | māṃ mudhāpavādayati | tatas
(p.60, l.10)tairmilitvā nirbandhaḥ kṛtaḥ | yaḥ ko 'pi adyaprabhṛti bahiḥ śāyī so
(p.60, l.11)'parādhī | evaṃ nirbandhe kṛte 'pi sā suptaṃ patiṃ vihāya bahirgatā |
(p.61, l.1)tasyāṃ ca bahirgatāyāṃ sa patirdvāraṃ dattvā suptaḥ | yadā ca bahiḥ krīḍāṃ
(p.61, l.2)kṛtvā samāgatāyāḥ sa patirdvāraṃ nodghāṭayati tadā sā kūpe dṛṣadaṃ kṣiptvā
(p.61, l.3)dvāradeśa eva sthitā | patirapi kūpe patitā bhaviṣyatīti jñātvā
(p.61, l.4)dvāramudghāṭya bahirnirgataḥ | tadā sā dvāraṃ pidhāya madhye sthitā | so
(p.61, l.5)'pi ca bahiḥ sthito hā priye evaṃ vadanmahatā śabdena roditumārabdhaḥ |
(p.61, l.6)sāpi vigopakabhayādbahirnirgatya patiṃ madhye nināya | tatastanmithunaṃ
(p.61, l.7)parasparaṃ nirbandhaṃ cakāra | yadadyaprabhṛti mayā tvayā ca visaṃvādo na
(p.61, l.8)vidheyaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.61, l.9)iti śukasaptatau ṣoḍaśī kathā ||

tac chrutvā prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | so 'bravīt | asti vidiśā nāma purī | tasyāṃ janavallabho nāma vaṇik | tasya bhāryā mugdhikā nāma capalā svairiṇī | yadā ca tayātiśayena vidūṣito 'yaṃ tadā bandhūnāṃ kathayāmāsa yadiyaṃ bahiḥ śāyinī | yadā ca tairevamuktā tadā tayāpy uktam | ayameva bahiḥśāyī sadaiva | māṃ mudhāpavādayati | tatas tairmilitvā nirbandhaḥ kṛtaḥ | yaḥ ko 'pi adyaprabhṛti bahiḥ śāyī so 'parādhī | evaṃ nirbandhe kṛte 'pi sā suptaṃ patiṃ vihāya bahirgatā | tasyāṃ ca bahirgatāyāṃ sa patirdvāraṃ dattvā suptaḥ | yadā ca bahiḥ krīḍāṃ kṛtvā samāgatāyāḥ sa patirdvāraṃ nodghāṭayati tadā sā kūpe dṛṣadaṃ kṣiptvā dvāradeśa eva sthitā | patirapi kūpe patitā bhaviṣyatīti jñātvā dvāramudghāṭya bahirnirgataḥ | tadā sā dvāraṃ pidhāya madhye sthitā | so 'pi ca bahiḥ sthito hā priye evaṃ vadanmahatā śabdena roditumārabdhaḥ | sāpi vigopakabhayādbahirnirgatya patiṃ madhye nināya | tatastanmithunaṃ parasparaṃ nirbandhaṃ cakāra | yadadyaprabhṛti mayā tvayā ca visaṃvādo na vidheyaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣoḍaśī kathā ||

(p.62, l.7)ca nagaryāṃ buddhijīvanaṃ vyacintayat | tataḥ ṣaṇḍaṃ yavakāśādibhiḥ pupoṣa |

(p.62, l.9)vaṇijārakaveṣadhārī madanāyā veśyāyāḥ kuṭṭinīṃ jagāda | asmadīyā
(p.62, l.10)balīvardāḥ savastukāḥ prātareṣyanti | adyāhaṃ tṛṇānayanārthamāgataḥ |
(p.62, l.11)tadyatra asmadīyasya balīvardasya sthānaṃ bhavati tatrāhaṃ svapimi |
(p.63, l.1)ityukte sā kuṭṭinī balīvardadhanaiṣiṇī taṃ sthāpayāmāsa | so 'pi taṃ
(p.63, l.2)ṣaṇḍaṃ baddhvā vilāsinīpārśve yayau | tayā ca snāpito bhojitaśca
(p.63, l.3)guṇāḍhyo rajanyāṃ śṛṅgāritaḥ tatsakāśe sthitaḥ | so 'pi ca prabhātāyāṃ
(p.63, l.4)niśi prathamamevotthāya svarṇaśṛṅkhalaṃ gṛhītvā jagāma | gate ca
(p.63, l.5)tasminnekā ceṭī utthitā ṣaṇḍamadṛṣṭvā kuṭṭinīṃ pratyāha | āue kim
(p.63, l.6)idam | tatastaṃ vilāsinīpārśvādgataṃ jñātvā maunaṃ vidhāya sthitā |

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kathametat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā purī | tatra yāyajūko brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya patnī pāhinī nāma surūpā ativallabhā | tatputraḥ pitrā sarvāmapi kramādvidyāṃ grāhitaḥ | anyadā sa pitarau muktvā deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | guṇāḍhya iti viśruto babhūva | jayantyāṃ ca nagaryāṃ buddhijīvanaṃ vyacintayat | tataḥ ṣaṇḍaṃ yavakāśādibhiḥ pupoṣa | so 'pi ṣaṇḍastamanu paribhramati | anyadā sabandhanaṃ ṣaṇḍaṃ vidhāya vaṇijārakaveṣadhārī madanāyā veśyāyāḥ kuṭṭinīṃ jagāda | asmadīyā balīvardāḥ savastukāḥ prātareṣyanti | adyāhaṃ tṛṇānayanārthamāgataḥ | tadyatra asmadīyasya balīvardasya sthānaṃ bhavati tatrāhaṃ svapimi | ityukte sā kuṭṭinī balīvardadhanaiṣiṇī taṃ sthāpayāmāsa | so 'pi taṃ ṣaṇḍaṃ baddhvā vilāsinīpārśve yayau | tayā ca snāpito bhojitaśca guṇāḍhyo rajanyāṃ śṛṅgāritaḥ tatsakāśe sthitaḥ | so 'pi ca prabhātāyāṃ niśi prathamamevotthāya svarṇaśṛṅkhalaṃ gṛhītvā jagāma | gate ca tasminnekā ceṭī utthitā ṣaṇḍamadṛṣṭvā kuṭṭinīṃ pratyāha | āue kim idam | tatastaṃ vilāsinīpārśvādgataṃ jñātvā maunaṃ vidhāya sthitā |

asti śubhasthānaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra daridro nāma vaṇik | tasya gṛhe cauraḥ praviṣṭaḥ | so 'pi ca tatrānyatkimapyalabhamānaḥ sarṣapān gṛhītvā nirgato rājapuruṣaiḥ prāptaḥ | sarṣapāngale baddhvā bhrāmito rājakulātsa kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | yo yaḥ pṛcchati tasya tasyāgre vadati | aho sarṣapāṇāṃ madhye na kiṃcit | tato rājñā sabhāyām ākārya pṛṣṭaḥ | tava vaco 'bhiprāyaṃ na jāne | sa prāha |

(p.65, l.3)yato 'hametāvadbhirapi gale baddhairbaddhaḥ | rājāpi tadākarṇya hasaṃstaṃ mumoca |

(p.65, l.5)iti śukasaptatau aṣṭādaśī kathā ||

p.65, l.9

(p.65, l.9)asti karahaḍābhidhaṃ puram | tatra rājā guṇapriyo nāma yathārthaḥ |
(p.65, l.10)tatra ca soḍhāko nāma śreṣṭhiḥ | tadbhāryā santikā nāma pativratā |
(p.65, l.11)tatraiva cānyo vaṇik | tadbhāryā svacchandā nāma puṃścalī |
(p.66, l.1)sā ca soḍhākaṃ nityamicchati paraṃ so 'bhivāñchāṃ na vidhatte | anyadā
(p.66, l.2)ca manorathābhidhaṃ yakṣaṃ namaskartuṃ jagāma saḥ | tataḥ svacchandā pṛṣṭhalagnā
(p.66, l.3)tatra praviṣṭā | sa ca hāvabhāvādyairanukūlito bhuktaḥ |

asti karahaḍābhidhaṃ puram | tatra rājā guṇapriyo nāma yathārthaḥ | tatra ca soḍhāko nāma śreṣṭhiḥ | tadbhāryā santikā nāma pativratā | tatraiva cānyo vaṇik | tadbhāryā svacchandā nāma puṃścalī | sā ca soḍhākaṃ nityamicchati paraṃ so 'bhivāñchāṃ na vidhatte | anyadā ca manorathābhidhaṃ yakṣaṃ namaskartuṃ jagāma saḥ | tataḥ svacchandā pṛṣṭhalagnā tatra praviṣṭā | sa ca hāvabhāvādyairanukūlito bhuktaḥ |

p.66, l.8

(p.66, l.8)tacca mithunaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā rājapuruṣaiḥ tadbandhanāya yakṣagṛhaṃ veṣṭitam |
(p.66, l.9)santikā ca śuddhiṃ jñātvā rātrau mahatā tūryaśabdena yakṣagṛhaṃ gatā |
(p.66, l.10)teṣāmārakṣakāṇāṃ purata uktam | ahamadyadinavratā yakṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhojanaṃ
(p.66, l.11)vijane vidhāsye | māṃ ca kiṃciddhanaṃ gṛhītvā madhye praveśayata | tairapi
(p.66, l.12)tathaiva kṛtam | tatastayā svacchandā svaveṣāṃ kārayitvā bahirniṣkāsitā |

(p.67, l.2)vilakṣībabhūvuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.67, l.3)iti śukasaptatau ekonaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

tacca mithunaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā rājapuruṣaiḥ tadbandhanāya yakṣagṛhaṃ veṣṭitam | santikā ca śuddhiṃ jñātvā rātrau mahatā tūryaśabdena yakṣagṛhaṃ gatā | teṣāmārakṣakāṇāṃ purata uktam | ahamadyadinavratā yakṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhojanaṃ vijane vidhāsye | māṃ ca kiṃciddhanaṃ gṛhītvā madhye praveśayata | tairapi tathaiva kṛtam | tatastayā svacchandā svaveṣāṃ kārayitvā bahirniṣkāsitā | svayaṃ te madhye sthitā | taṃ ca prātarnijakāntāsahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā ārakṣakā vilakṣībabhūvuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekonaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

p.67, l.7

(p.67, l.7)asti sābhramatyā nadyāstaṭe śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma sthānam | tatra ca karṣukaḥ
(p.67, l.8)sūrākhyo dhanī | tasya kelikā bhāryā paraṃ kuṭilā kulaṭā ca |
(p.67, l.9)sānyasminnadītīre siddheśvarapurasthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kāmayate | tadāsaktā ca
(p.68, l.1)rātrau prātiveśikādūtikāsāhāyyānnadīṃ tīrtvā tadantikaṃ prāpnoti |
(p.68, l.2)anyadā bhartrā jñātam | sa ca tatra gatastaccaritragaveṣaṇāya | yāvatsā
(p.68, l.3)nadītīre tatra samāgatā tayā sa tāvaddṛṣṭaḥ | tatastaraṇaghaṭaṃ pānīyabhṛtaṃ
(p.68, l.4)vidhāya prātiveśmikāgṛhamadhye bhaṭṭārikāṃ maṇḍayitvā tena payasā
(p.68, l.5)snāpayitvā pratyuvāca prathamasaṃketitāṃ dūtikāmuddiśya | svāmini purā
(p.68, l.6)tvayā uktam | yadi tvaṃ siddheśvarīṃ na snāpayasi tataḥ pañcānāṃ dinānāṃ
(p.68, l.7)madhye tvadbhartṛmaraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | tato yadi tvadvacanapramāṇaṃ tadā
(p.68, l.8)mama patiściraṃ jīvatu | prātiveśmikayoktam | evamastviti śrutvā
(p.68, l.9)sa patistuṣṭo bhūtvālakṣita eva jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī
(p.68, l.10)suptā |
(p.68, l.11)iti śukasaptatau viṃśatitamī kathā ||

asti sābhramatyā nadyāstaṭe śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma sthānam | tatra ca karṣukaḥ sūrākhyo dhanī | tasya kelikā bhāryā paraṃ kuṭilā kulaṭā ca | sānyasminnadītīre siddheśvarapurasthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kāmayate | tadāsaktā ca rātrau prātiveśikādūtikāsāhāyyānnadīṃ tīrtvā tadantikaṃ prāpnoti | anyadā bhartrā jñātam | sa ca tatra gatastaccaritragaveṣaṇāya | yāvatsā nadītīre tatra samāgatā tayā sa tāvaddṛṣṭaḥ | tatastaraṇaghaṭaṃ pānīyabhṛtaṃ vidhāya prātiveśmikāgṛhamadhye bhaṭṭārikāṃ maṇḍayitvā tena payasā snāpayitvā pratyuvāca prathamasaṃketitāṃ dūtikāmuddiśya | svāmini purā tvayā uktam | yadi tvaṃ siddheśvarīṃ na snāpayasi tataḥ pañcānāṃ dinānāṃ madhye tvadbhartṛmaraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | tato yadi tvadvacanapramāṇaṃ tadā mama patiściraṃ jīvatu | prātiveśmikayoktam | evamastviti śrutvā sa patistuṣṭo bhūtvālakṣita eva jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau viṃśatitamī kathā ||

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti pratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra hemaprabho nāma rājā | śrutaśīlo mantrī | śreṣṭhī yaśodharaḥ | mohinī bhāryā | tayostanayā mandodarī | sa śrīvatsāya vaṇije kāntipurīsamāgatāya dattā | tanmithunamatīva snehalampaṭam | sā ca prātiveśmikayā pitṛbhāryayā kuṭṭinyā daṃṣṭrākarālayā yojitamanyaṃ rājaputram upabhuṅkte | sā cāpannasattvā bhūtā garbhasaṃbhavātsaṃjāte dohade rājavallabhaṃ mayūraṃ mārayitvā bhakṣitavatī | rājā tu tasminmayūre samāgate bhuṅkte iti sthitiḥ | tasmindivase tu bhojanavelāyāṃ na labdhaḥ | ḍiṇḍimaghoṣaṇe kṛte kuṭṭinyā paṭahaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tayā ca jñātaṃ yatkayācid āpannasattvayā mayūro dohadādbhakṣitaḥ | tataḥ sā garbhavatī pṛṣṭā | tayā kuṭṭinī gṛhamāgatā saṃmānitā |

(p.73, l.6)mātarmayā evaṃvidhaḥ svapno dṛṣṭaḥ | yaḥ kaścidarthapramāṇo me bhavati sa
(p.73, l.7)kathyatām | evaṃ śrutvā mantrī dvāramāhatya bahirnirgataḥ | tataḥ sanmānitā

mātarmayā evaṃvidhaḥ svapno dṛṣṭaḥ | yaḥ kaścidarthapramāṇo me bhavati sa kathyatām | evaṃ śrutvā mantrī dvāramāhatya bahirnirgataḥ | tataḥ sanmānitā vaṇigvadhūḥ | sā tu kuṭṭinīti nirvāsitā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau ekaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

§ 22

(p.74, l.4)tac chrutvā prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ prāha | dāmbhilāgrāme soḍhāko
(p.74, l.5)karṣukaḥ | tadbhāryā māḍhukā nāma | tāṃ ca bhaktahāriṇīṃ pathi

(p.74, l.7)muktvā tena saha sthitā | tato mūladevena dhūrtena tasminbhakte uṣṭrikā
(p.74, l.8)kṛtā | tayā ca evaṃjātaṃ bhaktamanutpāṭayitvā nītam | yāvacca bhartrā
(p.74, l.9)uṣṭrikā dṛṣṭā tāvatkimidamiti sā pṛṣṭā | tatastayā tatkālottaraṃ
(p.75, l.1)kṛtvoktam | nāthādya rātrau svapne uṣṭrikayā bhakṣito dṛṣṭastvam | tato
(p.75, l.2)mayā vighnāpahārāya viparītamidaṃ kṛtam | viśrabdhaṃ bhakṣaya yathā vighno
(p.75, l.3)naśyati | iti śrutvā ratātmanā tenoṣṭrikāpi bhakṣitā | iti kathāṃ
(p.75, l.4)śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.75, l.5)iti śukasaptatau dvāviṃśatitamī kathā ||

tac chrutvā prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ prāha | dāmbhilāgrāme soḍhāko karṣukaḥ | tadbhāryā māḍhukā nāma | tāṃ ca bhaktahāriṇīṃ pathi gacchantīmeko bahiḥ sūrapālākhyo naro bhuṅkte | sā kadācinmārge bhaktaṃ muktvā tena saha sthitā | tato mūladevena dhūrtena tasminbhakte uṣṭrikā kṛtā | tayā ca evaṃjātaṃ bhaktamanutpāṭayitvā nītam | yāvacca bhartrā uṣṭrikā dṛṣṭā tāvatkimidamiti sā pṛṣṭā | tatastayā tatkālottaraṃ kṛtvoktam | nāthādya rātrau svapne uṣṭrikayā bhakṣito dṛṣṭastvam | tato mayā vighnāpahārāya viparītamidaṃ kṛtam | viśrabdhaṃ bhakṣaya yathā vighno naśyati | iti śrutvā ratātmanā tenoṣṭrikāpi bhakṣitā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvāviṃśatitamī kathā ||

(p.81, l.8)preṣitaḥ | tatra ca kalāvatī veśyā | tayā saha varṣamekaṃ sthitaḥ | tāṃ

(p.82, l.1)sarvamapi māturniveditam | mātāpi prāha | niścitameṣa veśyāsutaḥ | nedṛśair
(p.82, l.2)gṛhyate | prapañcenaiva grāhyaḥ | tato yadāyaṃ svadeśaṃ gantukāmastvāmutkalāpayati
(p.82, l.3)tadā tvayā vācyam | ahamapi tatra yāsyāmi | yadi na
(p.82, l.4)nayasi tadā mariṣyāmītyuktvā kūpe jhampā deyā | tato 'sau prītastvāṃ
(p.82, l.5)prati sarvaṃ dāsyati | tayoktam | mātarmāṃ vinā taddravyeṇa kim |

ityevamādi samagraṃ veśyānugaṃ caritaṃ śikṣitam | tataḥ sa putraḥ pratijñāpūrvaṃ vaṇije samarpitaḥ | piturvākyena ca suvarṇadvīpe vāṇijyāya preṣitaḥ | tatra ca kalāvatī veśyā | tayā saha varṣamekaṃ sthitaḥ | tāṃ vaiśikāni kurvantīṃ sa prāha | viśeṣaṃ vada | eva mamānujāpi vadati | tato bahubhirapi vaiśikairna tatsarvasvaṃ gṛhītuṃ śaknoti | tatastayā sarvamapi māturniveditam | mātāpi prāha | niścitameṣa veśyāsutaḥ | nedṛśair gṛhyate | prapañcenaiva grāhyaḥ | tato yadāyaṃ svadeśaṃ gantukāmastvāmutkalāpayati tadā tvayā vācyam | ahamapi tatra yāsyāmi | yadi na nayasi tadā mariṣyāmītyuktvā kūpe jhampā deyā | tato 'sau prītastvāṃ prati sarvaṃ dāsyati | tayoktam | mātarmāṃ vinā taddravyeṇa kim |

  • (p.83, l.4)kālaḥ samaviṣamakaraḥ paribhavasanmānakārakaḥ kālaḥ | (p.83, l.5)kālaḥ karoti puruṣaṃ dātāraṃ yācitāraṃ ca || 23.27 (= 157) ||

nāsāhasaṃ samālambya naro bhadrāṇi paśyati | sāhasī sarvakāryeṣu lakṣmībhājanamuttamam || 23.25 (= 155) ||
nābhittvā paramarmāṇi nākṛtvā karma duṣkaram | nāhatvā matsyaghātīva prāpnoti mahatīṃ śriyam || 23.26 (= 156) ||
kālaḥ samaviṣamakaraḥ paribhavasanmānakārakaḥ kālaḥ | kālaḥ karoti puruṣaṃ dātāraṃ yācitāraṃ ca || 23.27 (= 157) ||
