p.87, l.3

(p.87, l.3)tataḥ śreṣṭhī taṃ putraṃ preṣayāmāsāśu tayā samaṃ suvarṇadvīpe | tatastasmin sarvo
(p.87, l.4)'pi paurajanaḥ prīto babhūva | sā ca kalāvatī sānukūlā taṃ vinayenājuhāva |
(p.87, l.5)tathā ca sa tayāvarjito yathāsau ātmāyattaḥ kṛtaḥ |
(p.87, l.6)dravyaṃ ca sarvaṃ gṛhītam | tataḥ sā dhūrtamāyā kuṭṭinī kiṃ karotu |
(p.87, l.7)iti praśnaḥ | sā prāha | śuka na jāne | tvaṃ vada | śukaḥ | yadyadya na
(p.87, l.8)yāsi tadā kathayāmi | sā āha | na yāsyāmi | śukaḥ | yadā
(p.87, l.9)tasya sarvasvaṃ gṛhītaṃ tasmin samaye kaiściddinaiścāgre 'pi cāṇḍālarūpadhāriṇī
(p.87, l.10)dhūrtamāyā nityaṃ nityaṃ gaveṣamāṇaiva kiṃcit | anyadā sa kalāvatyā
(p.87, l.11)sahitaḥ khaṭvāyāmupaviṣṭastayā dṛṣṭaḥ | tāṃ dvāri dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya nāśayitum
(p.87, l.12)udyataḥ pūrvameva saṃketitam | tamuttiṣṭhantamanu kalāvatyapi utthitā |
(p.88, l.1)uktaśca | kimidamiti | rāmastāmuvāca | bhadre iyaṃ mama jananī |
(p.88, l.2)ahaṃ ca hṛtārthako bahudinebhyo na tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | dhūrtamāyāpi taṃ saṃketasthaṃ
(p.88, l.3)dvārasthaiva saśaṅkā hastasaṃjñayā ājuhāva |

tataḥ śreṣṭhī taṃ putraṃ preṣayāmāsāśu tayā samaṃ suvarṇadvīpe | tatastasmin sarvo 'pi paurajanaḥ prīto babhūva | sā ca kalāvatī sānukūlā taṃ vinayenājuhāva | tathā ca sa tayāvarjito yathāsau ātmāyattaḥ kṛtaḥ | dravyaṃ ca sarvaṃ gṛhītam | tataḥ sā dhūrtamāyā kuṭṭinī kiṃ karotu | iti praśnaḥ | sā prāha | śuka na jāne | tvaṃ vada | śukaḥ | yadyadya na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | sā āha | na yāsyāmi | śukaḥ | yadā tasya sarvasvaṃ gṛhītaṃ tasmin samaye kaiściddinaiścāgre 'pi cāṇḍālarūpadhāriṇī dhūrtamāyā nityaṃ nityaṃ gaveṣamāṇaiva kiṃcit | anyadā sa kalāvatyā sahitaḥ khaṭvāyāmupaviṣṭastayā dṛṣṭaḥ | tāṃ dvāri dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya nāśayitum udyataḥ pūrvameva saṃketitam | tamuttiṣṭhantamanu kalāvatyapi utthitā | uktaśca | kimidamiti | rāmastāmuvāca | bhadre iyaṃ mama jananī | ahaṃ ca hṛtārthako bahudinebhyo na tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | dhūrtamāyāpi taṃ saṃketasthaṃ dvārasthaiva saśaṅkā hastasaṃjñayā ājuhāva |

p.88, l.4

p.88, l.6

(p.88, l.6)yāvadevaṃ gṛhāṅgaṇagatā śapati tāvatsa vaṇikcāṇḍālarūpīṃ samāgatya
(p.88, l.7)tatpādayoḥ patitaḥ | etacca dṛṣṭvā kalāvatī kuṭṭinīsahitā tām gṛhamadhye
(p.88, l.8)nītvā pṛcchati sma | amba ko 'yam | kiṃjātīyaḥ | tvaṃ kā | tayoktam |
(p.88, l.9)padmāvatīpurīnāthasya rājñaḥ sudarśanasya mātaṅgī gāyinī aham |
(p.88, l.10)ayaṃ ca madīyaṃ dravyaṃ hṛtvā ihāgataḥ | tacca tvayāptam | tanmayā jñātam |
(p.88, l.11)paramadhunā sa samāgacchatu | tataḥ kuṭṭinī kalāvatīsahitā
(p.88, l.12)tatpādayorlagnā uvāca | gṛhāṇedaṃ dravyam | dhūrtamāyā prāha | nāhaṃ
(p.89, l.1)gṛhakoṇe grahīṣye | rājaviditaṃ grahīṣyāmi | tato veśyāmātāpi atiśayena
(p.89, l.2)bhītā mātaṅgīṃ pratijagāda | imāṃ matsutāṃ rakṣa rakṣa |
(p.89, l.3)pāramparyāgataṃ dravyaṃ gṛhāṇa sarvasvam | paraṃ māṃ maivaṃ viḍambaya | dhūrtamāyā
(p.89, l.4)āha | grahīṣye | tataḥ sā veśyayā kuṭṭinyā saha hastapādau
(p.89, l.5)gṛhītvā sammānitā | dhūrtamāyāpi nijaṃ tadīyaṃ ca dravyaṃ sarvasvaṃ gṛhītvā
(p.89, l.6)rāmeṇa saha potamāruhya svagṛhamāgatya mahotsavamakārayat |
(p.89, l.7)iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.89, l.8)iti śukasaptatau trayoviṃśatitamī kathā ||

yāvadevaṃ gṛhāṅgaṇagatā śapati tāvatsa vaṇikcāṇḍālarūpīṃ samāgatya tatpādayoḥ patitaḥ | etacca dṛṣṭvā kalāvatī kuṭṭinīsahitā tām gṛhamadhye nītvā pṛcchati sma | amba ko 'yam | kiṃjātīyaḥ | tvaṃ kā | tayoktam | padmāvatīpurīnāthasya rājñaḥ sudarśanasya mātaṅgī gāyinī aham | ayaṃ ca madīyaṃ dravyaṃ hṛtvā ihāgataḥ | tacca tvayāptam | tanmayā jñātam | paramadhunā sa samāgacchatu | tataḥ kuṭṭinī kalāvatīsahitā tatpādayorlagnā uvāca | gṛhāṇedaṃ dravyam | dhūrtamāyā prāha | nāhaṃ gṛhakoṇe grahīṣye | rājaviditaṃ grahīṣyāmi | tato veśyāmātāpi atiśayena bhītā mātaṅgīṃ pratijagāda | imāṃ matsutāṃ rakṣa rakṣa | pāramparyāgataṃ dravyaṃ gṛhāṇa sarvasvam | paraṃ māṃ maivaṃ viḍambaya | dhūrtamāyā āha | grahīṣye | tataḥ sā veśyayā kuṭṭinyā saha hastapādau gṛhītvā sammānitā | dhūrtamāyāpi nijaṃ tadīyaṃ ca dravyaṃ sarvasvaṃ gṛhītvā rāmeṇa saha potamāruhya svagṛhamāgatya mahotsavamakārayat | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau trayoviṃśatitamī kathā ||

(p.90, l.2)prabhāvatyāha | kimetat | kīro 'bravīt | asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram |
(p.90, l.3)tatrābhūdvardhakiḥ sūrapālākhyaḥ śrīmān | tasya sajjanī nāma
(p.90, l.4)bhāryā atyantaṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tāṃ ca tadgṛhasthāṃ devako nāma ramate |

(p.90, l.9)mama patirgṛhe na vidyate | sa cāgatastava tadeva aucityaṃ vidhāsyati |
(p.91, l.1)yadyapi pūrvaṃ patyā tvadīyaṃ dravyamapahṛtaṃ tathāpi kṣantavyam | rathakṛti
(p.91, l.2)samāgate tava gṛhaṃ gamiṣyāmi yuvayoḥ saṃgatiṃ vā kariṣye | nātra
(p.91, l.3)saṃśayaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.91, l.4)iti śukasaptatau caturviṃśatitamī kathā ||

prabhāvatyāha | kimetat | kīro 'bravīt | asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatrābhūdvardhakiḥ sūrapālākhyaḥ śrīmān | tasya sajjanī nāma bhāryā atyantaṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tāṃ ca tadgṛhasthāṃ devako nāma ramate | iti lokādetadākarṇya vardhakiḥ kapaṭena gṛhānnirgatya prātaḥ saṃdhyāyāmācchannaḥ samāgatya talpasyādhobhāge sthitaḥ | sā ca jāreṇa saha tatrārūḍhā patyā keśeṣu gṛhītā kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | sā patyā dhṛtā satī dvitīyapatimukhamālokya prāha | mayā tava kathitaṃ yadrathakāro mama patirgṛhe na vidyate | sa cāgatastava tadeva aucityaṃ vidhāsyati | yadyapi pūrvaṃ patyā tvadīyaṃ dravyamapahṛtaṃ tathāpi kṣantavyam | rathakṛti samāgate tava gṛhaṃ gamiṣyāmi yuvayoḥ saṃgatiṃ vā kariṣye | nātra saṃśayaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau caturviṃśatitamī kathā ||

(p.92, l.7)sitavastraḥ | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.92, l.8)iti śukasaptatau pañcaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

asti candrapurī nāma nagarī | tatra siddhaseno nāma kṣapaṇako janapūjitaḥ | tasminneva nagare 'nyaḥ sitapaṭo guṇināṃ mukhyaḥ samāgataḥ | tena ca guṇinā sarvo 'pi jana āvarjitaḥ śrāvakā apyātmāyattāḥ kṛtāḥ | sa kṣapaṇako 'pi tasya pūjāṃ kriyamāṇāmasahamānaḥ svayaṃ tadīyopāśraye veśyāṃ preṣayitvā asau veśyālubdho na suśīla iti śvetāmbarasya lokapravādamakarot | taddarśanāya janamākārayāmāsa | brūte ca | kṣapaṇakā eva brahmacāriṇaḥ śvetāmbarāstu viplutāḥ | so 'pi śvetāmbaro dīpāgninā upādhiṃ prajvālya prabhātaprāptāyāṃ rajanyāṃ nagnībhūya veśyāyā dattahasto nirgataḥ | tato lokāpavādaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | yadasau kṣapaṇako na sitavastraḥ | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

asti kuhāḍākhyo mahāgrāmaḥ | tatra jarasākhyo kuṭumbiko mahāmūrkhaḥ | tadbhāryā devikā puṃścalī | tāṃ ca prabhākaro brāhmaṇaḥ kṣetramadhye vibhītakavṛkṣasamīpe guptasthāne mudā ramate | īdṛśaṃ vyatikaraṃ janāc chrutvā tatpatistatrāvalokanāya svayaṃ gataḥ | tena ca vṛkṣārūḍhena tattathaiva dṛṣṭam | dṛṣṭvā tatrasthenāpi jalpitam | dhūrtike bahudinebhyo 'dya saṃprāptā | ityuktā kathamiyaṃ bhartāraṃ pratyāyayatu | tayoktam | nāhaṃ jāne tvameva kathaya | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayā tatheti pratipanne śukaḥ prāha | sā ca tadvacaḥ śrutvā taṃ jāraṃ preṣayāmāsa patyā cāvatīrya samāgatena upālabdhā | sāha | he prabho | īdṛśa eva vṛkṣaḥ atrārūḍhairmithunaṃ dṛśyate | tena patinā uktam | tvamāruhya avalokaya | tayā tathā kṛtam | vṛkṣārūḍhayā ca tayā proktaṃ kapaṭena | bahudivasebhyo 'nyāṃ narīmabhigamandṛṣṭo 'si | tena mūrkheṇa jñātam | satyam idam | sa ca tāṃ śāntayitvā gṛhaṃ nināya | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭāviṃśatitamī kathā ||

(p.101, l.4)sa śaśakena dhūrtena vāṭīṃ nītvā tasyaiva pratibimbaḥ kūpe darśitaḥ |
(p.101, l.5)siṃho 'pi mūrkhastaṃ jale dṛṣṭvā kupito jhampāmadānmṛtaśca |

madhurākhye vane piṅgalanāmā siṃhaḥ | sa sattvāni bahūni hanan sarvaiḥ paśubhirvicārya pratidinamekaikasattvaparikalpanavyavasthayā nivāritaḥ | anyadā śaśakasyaikasya vārakaḥ saṃjātaḥ | sa ca na yāti śvāpadair bhaṇito 'pi | gaccha tvamanyathā pūrvavatsarvāṇi bhūtāni sa bhakṣayiṣyati | sa cādyaprabhṛti tadantike sattvāni na yāsyanti | ityuktvā bahukālakṣepaṃ cakāra | madhyāhnasamaye eva ca mandaṃ mandaṃ siṃhasyāgre gantuṃ vyavasitaḥ | tenāpi sahasākrāntaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | śaśakaḥ siṃhaṃ prāha | svāminnahaṃ śaśakacatuṣṭayena saha āgacchanmārge tava śatruṇā dhṛto 'to velātikramo babhūva | tenoktam | sa śatruḥ kvāste | tataḥ sa śaśakena dhūrtena vāṭīṃ nītvā tasyaiva pratibimbaḥ kūpe darśitaḥ | siṃho 'pi mūrkhastaṃ jale dṛṣṭvā kupito jhampāmadānmṛtaśca |

p.101, l.6

  • (p.101, l.6)buddhirbalavatī bhīrusattvānāṃ na parākramaḥ | (p.101, l.7)śaśakenālpasattvena hataḥ siṃhaḥ parākramī || 31.2 (= 178) ||
  • (p.101, l.8)uktaṃ ca |
  • ekaṃ hanyānna vā hanyādiṣurmukto dhanuṣmatā | (p.101, l.9)sarāṣṭraṃ saprajaṃ hanti rājānaṃ mantriniścayaḥ || 31.3 (= 179) ||
buddhirbalavatī bhīrusattvānāṃ na parākramaḥ | śaśakenālpasattvena hataḥ siṃhaḥ parākramī || 31.2 (= 178) ||

uktaṃ ca |

ekaṃ hanyānna vā hanyādiṣurmukto dhanuṣmatā | sarāṣṭraṃ saprajaṃ hanti rājānaṃ mantriniścayaḥ || 31.3 (= 179) ||

(p.102, l.6)rūpasaṃpannā caturā puṃścalī | sānyadā drammamarpayitvā śvaśrvājñaptā godhūmān
(p.102, l.7)haṭṭe gṛhītvāgaccha | sā ca haṭṭe gatā | krīṇatyā copapatirdṛṣṭaḥ
(p.102, l.8)saṃjñitaśca samīpamāyayau | godhūmānmoṭāyāṃ baddhvā haṭṭe muktvā tena
(p.103, l.1)sārdhaṃ sā yayau | vaṇijāpi godhūmānutsārya moṭāyāṃ dhūlirbaddhā |
(p.103, l.2)sāpi tena saha ciraṃ sthitvā āgatyākulā moṭāmanutpāṭayitvā gṛhaṃ
(p.103, l.3)yayau | tāṃ choṭayitvā yāvat śvaśrūḥ paśyati kīdṛśā godhūmā iti
(p.103, l.4)tāvaddhūliṃ paśyati | atra kimuttaram | śukaḥ | kimidamiti yadā
(p.103, l.5)śvaśrvā pṛṣṭā tadā tayoktam | mātarmama hastāddrammo haṭṭāgre bhūmau patitaḥ |
(p.103, l.6)tato mayā dhūlirāhṛtā | tataḥ sā śvaśrūrdrammamanavalokamānā
(p.103, l.7)vikalībhūtā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.103, l.8)iti śukasaptatau dvātriṃśattamī kathā ||

asti śāntipuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra mādhavaḥ śreṣṭhī | tasya mohinī bhāryā | tayostanayaḥ sohaḍābhidhaḥ | tasya bhāryā rājinīnāmnī rūpasaṃpannā caturā puṃścalī | sānyadā drammamarpayitvā śvaśrvājñaptā godhūmān haṭṭe gṛhītvāgaccha | sā ca haṭṭe gatā | krīṇatyā copapatirdṛṣṭaḥ saṃjñitaśca samīpamāyayau | godhūmānmoṭāyāṃ baddhvā haṭṭe muktvā tena sārdhaṃ sā yayau | vaṇijāpi godhūmānutsārya moṭāyāṃ dhūlirbaddhā | sāpi tena saha ciraṃ sthitvā āgatyākulā moṭāmanutpāṭayitvā gṛhaṃ yayau | tāṃ choṭayitvā yāvat śvaśrūḥ paśyati kīdṛśā godhūmā iti tāvaddhūliṃ paśyati | atra kimuttaram | śukaḥ | kimidamiti yadā śvaśrvā pṛṣṭā tadā tayoktam | mātarmama hastāddrammo haṭṭāgre bhūmau patitaḥ | tato mayā dhūlirāhṛtā | tataḥ sā śvaśrūrdrammamanavalokamānā vikalībhūtā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvātriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.104, l.2

(p.104, l.2)kathametat | śuko 'bravīt | asti śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra
(p.104, l.3)śaṅkaro nāma mālikaḥ samṛddhimān | tasya rambhikā nāma bhāryā
(p.104, l.4)bahuratipriyā subhagā surūpā bahubhartṛkā ca | anyadā śaṅkaragṛhe pitṛkāryam
(p.104, l.5)āgatam | tasmindine tayopapatayaścatvāro nimantritāḥ | puṣpāṇāṃ
(p.104, l.6)vikrīṇāya gatayā catuṣpathe grāmaṇīrvaṇiksūnustalāraśca balādhipaś
(p.104, l.7)ca pratyekaṃ te te pṛthakpṛthak ākāritāḥ parasparamajānantaḥ |
(p.104, l.8)madīyaṃ bhavanaṃ prati prāgeva samāgantavyamiti | dvitīye 'hni
(p.105, l.1)mālike vāṭikāṃ gate vaṇiksūnuḥ snātvā bhuktvā ca tayā saha rantuṃ
(p.105, l.2)samāyayau | vaṇiji ardhasnāte grāmakūṭo gṛhadvāraṃ samāpatandṛṣṭaḥ |
(p.105, l.3)tataḥ snānaṃ kurvanvaṇiktathābhūto vaṃśamaye koṣṭhe khaliyukte kṣipto bhayayuktaś
(p.105, l.4)ca | grāmakūṭe 'pyardhasnāte bahistalāraḥ samāyātaḥ | taṃ dṛṣṭvā so
(p.105, l.5)'pi tasminneva koṣṭhe kṣipta uktaśca yadadhaḥ sarpiṇī prasūtāsti | tato
(p.105, l.6)'pyantarāla eva sthātavyamiti talāro 'pyardhasnāto balādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā
(p.105, l.7)bhāṇḍasamūhe kṣiptaḥ | balādhipo 'pyardhasnāto mālikaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraiva
(p.105, l.8)kṣiptaḥ | tato māliko lokaśca tasmin pitṛkārye yadṛcchayā bhojitāḥ |
(p.105, l.9)evaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ caturṇāmapi parasparamalakṣitānāṃ pṛthakpṛthak bhojanaṃ
(p.105, l.10)paramānnāmṛtaṃ samarpitam | vaṇijā tu bhuñjānena bahu phūtkṛtam | tadoparisthitena
(p.106, l.1)ca sarpiṇīṃ śaṅkamānena mūtritam | vaṇijā tu ghṛtāmiti
(p.106, l.2)jñātvā bhājanamutkṣiptam | uparisthitasya mukhe lagnam | tataḥ sa śaṅkitaḥ |
(p.106, l.3)so 'pi ca lagnaṃ lagnamiti vadandattajhampo niryayau | anye
(p.106, l.4)'pi lagnākṣarabhayākulā yāvannirgatāḥ śaṅkareṇa janaiśca dṛṣṭāḥ savismayaṃ
(p.106, l.5)khalikharaḍitāḥ | tataḥ sā kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaram | yadā sā patyā
(p.106, l.6)pṛṣṭā kimidamiti tadā tayoktam |

kathametat | śuko 'bravīt | asti śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra śaṅkaro nāma mālikaḥ samṛddhimān | tasya rambhikā nāma bhāryā bahuratipriyā subhagā surūpā bahubhartṛkā ca | anyadā śaṅkaragṛhe pitṛkāryam āgatam | tasmindine tayopapatayaścatvāro nimantritāḥ | puṣpāṇāṃ vikrīṇāya gatayā catuṣpathe grāmaṇīrvaṇiksūnustalāraśca balādhipaś ca pratyekaṃ te te pṛthakpṛthak ākāritāḥ parasparamajānantaḥ | madīyaṃ bhavanaṃ prati prāgeva samāgantavyamiti | dvitīye 'hni mālike vāṭikāṃ gate vaṇiksūnuḥ snātvā bhuktvā ca tayā saha rantuṃ samāyayau | vaṇiji ardhasnāte grāmakūṭo gṛhadvāraṃ samāpatandṛṣṭaḥ | tataḥ snānaṃ kurvanvaṇiktathābhūto vaṃśamaye koṣṭhe khaliyukte kṣipto bhayayuktaś ca | grāmakūṭe 'pyardhasnāte bahistalāraḥ samāyātaḥ | taṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'pi tasminneva koṣṭhe kṣipta uktaśca yadadhaḥ sarpiṇī prasūtāsti | tato 'pyantarāla eva sthātavyamiti talāro 'pyardhasnāto balādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāṇḍasamūhe kṣiptaḥ | balādhipo 'pyardhasnāto mālikaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraiva kṣiptaḥ | tato māliko lokaśca tasmin pitṛkārye yadṛcchayā bhojitāḥ | evaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ caturṇāmapi parasparamalakṣitānāṃ pṛthakpṛthak bhojanaṃ paramānnāmṛtaṃ samarpitam | vaṇijā tu bhuñjānena bahu phūtkṛtam | tadoparisthitena ca sarpiṇīṃ śaṅkamānena mūtritam | vaṇijā tu ghṛtāmiti jñātvā bhājanamutkṣiptam | uparisthitasya mukhe lagnam | tataḥ sa śaṅkitaḥ | so 'pi ca lagnaṃ lagnamiti vadandattajhampo niryayau | anye 'pi lagnākṣarabhayākulā yāvannirgatāḥ śaṅkareṇa janaiśca dṛṣṭāḥ savismayaṃ khalikharaḍitāḥ | tataḥ sā kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaram | yadā sā patyā pṛṣṭā kimidamiti tadā tayoktam |

p.106, l.7

(p.110, l.4)'pyaṅgulīyakamādāya tilagrāhakasyārpayāmāsa | so 'pi yathāgataṃ tathā

p.110, l.8

(p.110, l.8)niśāmukhe 'nyedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ punarāha | he kīra gamiṣyāmi cirakāṅkṣitaṃ
(p.110, l.9)sukhaṃ bhoktum | śuka āha |

p.111, l.1

  • (p.111, l.1)kā kīra nāyinī kutra tayā kiṃ kṛtamuttaram | (p.111, l.2)kathāṃ kathaya kalyāṇīṃ kautukaṃ me kathākrame || 36.2 (= 186) ||

p.111, l.3

(p.111, l.3)śuka āha | asti saraḍākhye grāme grāmaṇīḥ śūrapālaḥ | tasya bhāryā
(p.111, l.4)nāyinī | sā ātmapatiṃ nityaṃ paṭṭasūtrakañcukaṃ yācate | sa āha |
(p.111, l.5)vayaṃ karṣukāḥ kārpāsacīvarāḥ | asmadgṛhe paṭṭasūtravārttāmapi ko 'pi
(p.111, l.6)na jānāti | anyadā sā taṃ grāmasaṃsadisthaṃ jagāda | gṛhamehi gṛhādhipa |
(p.111, l.7)rāvaḍīṃ bhuṅkṣva | sa ca tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhāryāmāha gṛhāgataḥ |
(p.111, l.8)bhadre tvayā ninditaṃ vaco lajjākārakaṃ mamāpriyaṃ saṃsadi kimittham
(p.111, l.9)uktam | tayoktam | tvayā mama priyaṃ kathaṃ na kṛtam | grāmaṇīrāha |
(p.111, l.10)dāsyāmi kañcukaṃ te 'dya | nijaṃ vākyaṃ vṛthā kuru | tayoktam |
(p.112, l.1)kañcuke datte uttārayiṣye | dattaḥ kañcukastena | tadvacaḥ kathaṃ vṛthā bhavatv
(p.112, l.2)iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | anyadā nāyinī jagāda | yadādya tvāṃ
(p.112, l.3)saṃsadisthaṃ pūrvavadākārayāmi tadā tvayā saṃsadā saha gṛhamāgantavyam |
(p.112, l.4)tena ca evameva kṛtam | tayā ca gṛhāgatāyāḥ saṃsado bhavyarītyā
(p.112, l.5)bhojanaṃ dattam | tato grāmajano vadati | śūrapālaḥ samṛddhaḥ | paraṃ
(p.112, l.6)tadbhāryā auddhatyaparihāreṇa evaṃ vadati | iti vacanamuttāritam |
(p.112, l.7)iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.112, l.8)iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭtriṃśattamī kathā || 36 ||

śuka āha | asti saraḍākhye grāme grāmaṇīḥ śūrapālaḥ | tasya bhāryā nāyinī | sā ātmapatiṃ nityaṃ paṭṭasūtrakañcukaṃ yācate | sa āha | vayaṃ karṣukāḥ kārpāsacīvarāḥ | asmadgṛhe paṭṭasūtravārttāmapi ko 'pi na jānāti | anyadā sā taṃ grāmasaṃsadisthaṃ jagāda | gṛhamehi gṛhādhipa | rāvaḍīṃ bhuṅkṣva | sa ca tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhāryāmāha gṛhāgataḥ | bhadre tvayā ninditaṃ vaco lajjākārakaṃ mamāpriyaṃ saṃsadi kimittham uktam | tayoktam | tvayā mama priyaṃ kathaṃ na kṛtam | grāmaṇīrāha | dāsyāmi kañcukaṃ te 'dya | nijaṃ vākyaṃ vṛthā kuru | tayoktam | kañcuke datte uttārayiṣye | dattaḥ kañcukastena | tadvacaḥ kathaṃ vṛthā bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | anyadā nāyinī jagāda | yadādya tvāṃ saṃsadisthaṃ pūrvavadākārayāmi tadā tvayā saṃsadā saha gṛhamāgantavyam | tena ca evameva kṛtam | tayā ca gṛhāgatāyāḥ saṃsado bhavyarītyā bhojanaṃ dattam | tato grāmajano vadati | śūrapālaḥ samṛddhaḥ | paraṃ tadbhāryā auddhatyaparihāreṇa evaṃ vadati | iti vacanamuttāritam | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭtriṃśattamī kathā || 36 ||

p.113, l.1

(p.113, l.1)prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śuko 'pyāha | saṃgamākhye grāme śūraḥ kauṭumbikaḥ |
(p.113, l.2)tasyāsti pūrṇapālastu hālikaḥ | sarvatra ca tasya śūrapater
(p.113, l.3)veśmani kṣetre khale pramāṇam | tasya ca hālikasya kṣetrasthasya śūrapatisutā
(p.113, l.4)subhagā nāma nityaṃ bhuktiṃ nayati | sa tāṃ kāmayate kṣetragahvare
(p.113, l.5)śūrapālānniḥśaṅkitaḥ | taṃ ca vṛttāntamasamañjasamiti kṛtvā prativeśmahālikās
(p.113, l.6)tasya kathayāmāsuḥ | anyadāsau śūrastayorhālikasutayoḥ saṃbandhaṃ
(p.113, l.7)pratyakṣīkartuṃ kṣetraṃ gatvā gahvarasyādūrasamante 'lakṣitastasthau | tanmithunaṃ
(p.113, l.8)ratasthaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaraṃ ca kimiti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yāvatsa
(p.113, l.9)hālikastāṃ bhuktvotthitaḥ tāvat śūrapatiṃ dadarśa | tadā sa niḥśvasannāha |
(p.114, l.1)dhiṅ me karmārjanāṃ ca yanmayā halakheṭanaṃ vidheyaṃ iyaṃ ca granthirogiṇī |
(p.114, l.2)ato dvayorapi jīvitaṃ rasātalaṃ yātu | mayā tu nityaṃ halakheṭanaṃ
(p.114, l.3)grantherākarṣaṇaṃ ca dvayamapi vidheyam | tadahaṃ kimarthamasya śūrapālasya
(p.114, l.4)hāliko bhavāmi | itthamevāhaṃ kṣayaṃ yāsyāmi | iti hālikavacanaṃ
(p.114, l.5)śrutvā nirdoṣo 'yamiti lokasya vacanaṃ vitathīkṛtya śūrapatirlajjito
(p.114, l.6)gṛhaṃ yayau | sā ca prabhāvatī śukoktāṃ kathāṃ śrutvā suptā |
(p.114, l.7)iti śukasaptatau saptatriṃśattamī kathā ||

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śuko 'pyāha | saṃgamākhye grāme śūraḥ kauṭumbikaḥ | tasyāsti pūrṇapālastu hālikaḥ | sarvatra ca tasya śūrapater veśmani kṣetre khale pramāṇam | tasya ca hālikasya kṣetrasthasya śūrapatisutā subhagā nāma nityaṃ bhuktiṃ nayati | sa tāṃ kāmayate kṣetragahvare śūrapālānniḥśaṅkitaḥ | taṃ ca vṛttāntamasamañjasamiti kṛtvā prativeśmahālikās tasya kathayāmāsuḥ | anyadāsau śūrastayorhālikasutayoḥ saṃbandhaṃ pratyakṣīkartuṃ kṣetraṃ gatvā gahvarasyādūrasamante 'lakṣitastasthau | tanmithunaṃ ratasthaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaraṃ ca kimiti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yāvatsa hālikastāṃ bhuktvotthitaḥ tāvat śūrapatiṃ dadarśa | tadā sa niḥśvasannāha | dhiṅ me karmārjanāṃ ca yanmayā halakheṭanaṃ vidheyaṃ iyaṃ ca granthirogiṇī | ato dvayorapi jīvitaṃ rasātalaṃ yātu | mayā tu nityaṃ halakheṭanaṃ grantherākarṣaṇaṃ ca dvayamapi vidheyam | tadahaṃ kimarthamasya śūrapālasya hāliko bhavāmi | itthamevāhaṃ kṣayaṃ yāsyāmi | iti hālikavacanaṃ śrutvā nirdoṣo 'yamiti lokasya vacanaṃ vitathīkṛtya śūrapatirlajjito gṛhaṃ yayau | sā ca prabhāvatī śukoktāṃ kathāṃ śrutvā suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptatriṃśattamī kathā ||

(p.115, l.1)prabhāvatī papraccha | kathametat | śukaḥ | purābhūddevi priyaṃvado nāma
(p.115, l.2)vipraḥ pathikaḥ | ekadā mārge gacchan sudarśanagrāme kasyacidvaṇijo gṛhaṃ
(p.115, l.3)yayau | tatpatnī ca puṃścalī | sa ca brāhmaṇastāṃ dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ susthānakṛtavāsakaṃ
(p.115, l.4)mene | sa ca rātrau sakāmastāṃ prārthayāmāsa | aṅgulīyakadānena
(p.115, l.5)ca haṭṭamārgaṃ vaṇiksute gate reme tayā samam | prātaḥ so
(p.115, l.6)'ṅgulīyakaṃ yācate | sā nārpayati | anena vidhinā dattamaṅgulīyakaṃ

(p.115, l.11)vaṇiktadvacanaṃ śrutvā kupito bhāryāmāha | anena pramādena asmadgṛhe
(p.116, l.1)ko 'pi pathiko na sameṣyati | ityuktvā niṣṭhuraṃ vacastatkuṇḍāduttīrya
(p.116, l.2)aṅgulīyakaṃ pathikāya samarpitam | sa ca yathāgataṃ yayau | iti
(p.116, l.3)kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.116, l.4)iti śukasaptatau aṣṭātriṃśattamī kathā ||

prabhāvatī papraccha | kathametat | śukaḥ | purābhūddevi priyaṃvado nāma vipraḥ pathikaḥ | ekadā mārge gacchan sudarśanagrāme kasyacidvaṇijo gṛhaṃ yayau | tatpatnī ca puṃścalī | sa ca brāhmaṇastāṃ dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ susthānakṛtavāsakaṃ mene | sa ca rātrau sakāmastāṃ prārthayāmāsa | aṅgulīyakadānena ca haṭṭamārgaṃ vaṇiksute gate reme tayā samam | prātaḥ so 'ṅgulīyakaṃ yācate | sā nārpayati | anena vidhinā dattamaṅgulīyakaṃ sa kathaṃ gṛhṇātu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | yadā tu yācitā na dadāti tadā sa brāhmaṇaḥ khaṭvācaraṇaṃ gṛhītvā vaṇijaḥ saṃnidhiṃ yayau | khaṭvācaraṇaṃ darśayitvā phūtkṛtam | vaṇikprāha | bho dvija kimetat | sa āha | bhagne 'smin tvadīyabhāryayā madīyamaṅgulīyakaṃ jagṛhe | sa ca vaṇiktadvacanaṃ śrutvā kupito bhāryāmāha | anena pramādena asmadgṛhe ko 'pi pathiko na sameṣyati | ityuktvā niṣṭhuraṃ vacastatkuṇḍāduttīrya aṅgulīyakaṃ pathikāya samarpitam | sa ca yathāgataṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭātriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.117, l.5

(p.117, l.5)yadā tu sa tulāmātradhano 'bhavattadānyavaṇiggṛhe tulāṃ muktvā deśāntaraṃ
(p.117, l.6)gataḥ | tatra dhanamarjayitvā nijanagaramāgatya taṃ vaṇijaṃ tulāṃ yayāce |
(p.117, l.7)vaṇikpārśvāttulā na labdhā | tulāyāṃ tu lubdho vaṇik mūrkha uttaraṃ cakre
(p.117, l.8)yattvadīyā tulā mūṣikairbhakṣiteti śrutvā bhūdharastūṣṇīṃ sthitaḥ | sa ca ekadā
(p.117, l.9)tasya veśmani bhojanāya gataḥ krīḍantaṃ bālakaṃ dṛṣṭvā pracchannaṃ gṛhītvā
(p.118, l.1)nijagṛhaṃ yayau | bālakapitā ca duḥkhapūritāṅgo ruroda sakuṭumbaḥ |
(p.118, l.2)taṃ ca rudantaṃ dṛṣṭvā prativeśmiko jagāda | re tvadīyaḥ suto bhūdhareṇa
(p.118, l.3)gṛhītaḥ | tato 'sau tadgṛhaṃ gatvā bhūdharātsutaṃ yācitavān | bhūdhareṇoktam |
(p.118, l.4)mitra tvatputro matsaṃge snānārthe nadītīre gatastatra śyenenāpahṛtaḥ |
(p.118, l.5)iti śrutvā tena vaṇijā rājakule gatvā putraharaṇavṛttānto
(p.118, l.6)niveditaḥ | bhūdharo 'pi rājakulaṃ yayau | tatkathaya | sa bālahartā
(p.118, l.7)kathaṃ mucyatāmiti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | yadā bhūdharo rājasamakṣaṃ mantriṇā
(p.118, l.8)pṛṣṭastadā evaṃ jagāda |

yadā tu sa tulāmātradhano 'bhavattadānyavaṇiggṛhe tulāṃ muktvā deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | tatra dhanamarjayitvā nijanagaramāgatya taṃ vaṇijaṃ tulāṃ yayāce | vaṇikpārśvāttulā na labdhā | tulāyāṃ tu lubdho vaṇik mūrkha uttaraṃ cakre yattvadīyā tulā mūṣikairbhakṣiteti śrutvā bhūdharastūṣṇīṃ sthitaḥ | sa ca ekadā tasya veśmani bhojanāya gataḥ krīḍantaṃ bālakaṃ dṛṣṭvā pracchannaṃ gṛhītvā nijagṛhaṃ yayau | bālakapitā ca duḥkhapūritāṅgo ruroda sakuṭumbaḥ | taṃ ca rudantaṃ dṛṣṭvā prativeśmiko jagāda | re tvadīyaḥ suto bhūdhareṇa gṛhītaḥ | tato 'sau tadgṛhaṃ gatvā bhūdharātsutaṃ yācitavān | bhūdhareṇoktam | mitra tvatputro matsaṃge snānārthe nadītīre gatastatra śyenenāpahṛtaḥ | iti śrutvā tena vaṇijā rājakule gatvā putraharaṇavṛttānto niveditaḥ | bhūdharo 'pi rājakulaṃ yayau | tatkathaya | sa bālahartā kathaṃ mucyatāmiti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | yadā bhūdharo rājasamakṣaṃ mantriṇā pṛṣṭastadā evaṃ jagāda |

p.119, l.1

(p.119, l.10)prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | nagarābhidhe pattane subuddhiḥ kubuddhiśceti
(p.120, l.1)mitradvayaṃ jane prasiddham | anyadā subuddhirdeśāntaraṃ yayau | kubuddhistu
(p.120, l.2)mitrastriyaṃ ramate | subuddhiśca dhanamarjayitvā deśāntarātsamāgataḥ | tataḥ
(p.120, l.3)kubuddhiḥ subuddheḥ kapaṭasnehaṃ darśayati | subuddhināpi saṃmānitaḥ kubuddhistaṃ
(p.120, l.4)pratyāha | bhavatā kvāpi kiṃcitkautukaṃ dṛṣṭam | tenoktam | sarasvatīnadītīre
(p.120, l.5)kūpamadhye taramāṇamakālajamāmraphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ manoramanāmni grāme |
(p.120, l.6)kubuddhirāha | mithyedam | subuddhirāha | satyametat | tenoktam | yadi
(p.120, l.7)satyaṃ bhavati tadā yadasmadgṛhe dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahītuṃ śakyate tattvayā
(p.120, l.8)grāhyam | alīke tvadīyagṛhādahaṃ gṛhṇāmi | iti paṇabandhaṃ kṛtvā
(p.120, l.9)kubuddhī rātrau kūpāttatphalaṃ jagrāha | phalābhāve tu subuddhinā hāritam |
(p.120, l.10)atha sa tadbhāryāṃ grahītukāmaḥ paṇabandhaṃ yācate | tadatra subuddhir
(p.120, l.11)nijabhāryārakṣaṇe kamupāyaṃ karotviti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ śuka āha |
(p.120, l.12)subuddhistaṃ duṣṭāśayaṃ jñātvā nijagṛhavastujātaṃ nijakalatraṃ ca prāsādopari
(p.120, l.13)kṣiptvā ārohaṇikāṃ pātayāmāsa | kubuddhiḥ samāyātaḥ | subuddhir
(p.120, l.14)āha | evaṃ yadrocate tadasmadgṛhādgṛhyatām | sa ca kalatrāharaṇāya
(p.121, l.1)niḥśreṇikāṃ dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ jagrāha | tadā subuddhinoktam | mayaivaṃ
(p.121, l.2)pūrvaṃ gaditaṃ ca | yaddvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahīṣyase tava tadeva nānyat |
(p.121, l.3)tataḥ kubuddhirvilakṣo bhūtvā bahiryayau janaiśca ninditaḥ | iti kathāṃ
(p.121, l.4)śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.121, l.5)iti śukasaptatau catvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | nagarābhidhe pattane subuddhiḥ kubuddhiśceti mitradvayaṃ jane prasiddham | anyadā subuddhirdeśāntaraṃ yayau | kubuddhistu mitrastriyaṃ ramate | subuddhiśca dhanamarjayitvā deśāntarātsamāgataḥ | tataḥ kubuddhiḥ subuddheḥ kapaṭasnehaṃ darśayati | subuddhināpi saṃmānitaḥ kubuddhistaṃ pratyāha | bhavatā kvāpi kiṃcitkautukaṃ dṛṣṭam | tenoktam | sarasvatīnadītīre kūpamadhye taramāṇamakālajamāmraphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ manoramanāmni grāme | kubuddhirāha | mithyedam | subuddhirāha | satyametat | tenoktam | yadi satyaṃ bhavati tadā yadasmadgṛhe dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahītuṃ śakyate tattvayā grāhyam | alīke tvadīyagṛhādahaṃ gṛhṇāmi | iti paṇabandhaṃ kṛtvā kubuddhī rātrau kūpāttatphalaṃ jagrāha | phalābhāve tu subuddhinā hāritam | atha sa tadbhāryāṃ grahītukāmaḥ paṇabandhaṃ yācate | tadatra subuddhir nijabhāryārakṣaṇe kamupāyaṃ karotviti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ śuka āha | subuddhistaṃ duṣṭāśayaṃ jñātvā nijagṛhavastujātaṃ nijakalatraṃ ca prāsādopari kṣiptvā ārohaṇikāṃ pātayāmāsa | kubuddhiḥ samāyātaḥ | subuddhir āha | evaṃ yadrocate tadasmadgṛhādgṛhyatām | sa ca kalatrāharaṇāya niḥśreṇikāṃ dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ jagrāha | tadā subuddhinoktam | mayaivaṃ pūrvaṃ gaditaṃ ca | yaddvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahīṣyase tava tadeva nānyat | tataḥ kubuddhirvilakṣo bhūtvā bahiryayau janaiśca ninditaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau catvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

(p.121, l.12)vaidyairasādhyetyuktvā parityaktā | tato rājñā ḍiṇḍimāghoṣaṇaṃ
(p.122, l.1)kāritaṃ yathā yaḥ ko 'pi matsutāṃ gatarogāṃ karoti tamahaṃ dāridryarahitaṃ
(p.122, l.2)karomīti śrutvāparagrāmādāgatayā kayāciddvijabhāryayā ḍiṇḍimaḥ
(p.122, l.3)spṛṣṭaḥ | tasmin spṛṣṭe tayoktam | yanmama patirmāntrikaḥ | sa rājasutāṃ
(p.122, l.4)praguṇāṃ vidhāsyati | tato rājapuruṣaiḥ samānītaḥ | tasya ca
(p.122, l.5)nīyamānasya bhāryā jagāda | nātha gaccha nagaram | rājasutāyāṃ praguṇīkṛtāyāṃ
(p.122, l.6)tava bahu phalaṃ bhāvi | sa ca maṇḍalopaviṣṭo mantrādikam
(p.122, l.7)ajānan kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa māntrika
(p.122, l.8)ācāryavistāraṃ kṛtvā mantramityuccārayāmāsa |

prabhāvatī prāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra śatrumardano nāma rājā | tatsutāyā madanarekhāyā gale granthirbabhūva | vaidyairasādhyetyuktvā parityaktā | tato rājñā ḍiṇḍimāghoṣaṇaṃ kāritaṃ yathā yaḥ ko 'pi matsutāṃ gatarogāṃ karoti tamahaṃ dāridryarahitaṃ karomīti śrutvāparagrāmādāgatayā kayāciddvijabhāryayā ḍiṇḍimaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tasmin spṛṣṭe tayoktam | yanmama patirmāntrikaḥ | sa rājasutāṃ praguṇāṃ vidhāsyati | tato rājapuruṣaiḥ samānītaḥ | tasya ca nīyamānasya bhāryā jagāda | nātha gaccha nagaram | rājasutāyāṃ praguṇīkṛtāyāṃ tava bahu phalaṃ bhāvi | sa ca maṇḍalopaviṣṭo mantrādikam ajānan kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa māntrika ācāryavistāraṃ kṛtvā mantramityuccārayāmāsa |

  • taṃ dṛṣṭvā kānane vyāghraṃ naṣṭaṃ jātaṃ bhayākulam | (p.128, l.12)mṛgadhūrto hasannāha vyāghro naṣṭaḥ kuto bhayāt || 43.3 (= 214) ||

śukaḥ |

taṃ dṛṣṭvā kānane vyāghraṃ naṣṭaṃ jātaṃ bhayākulam | mṛgadhūrto hasannāha vyāghro naṣṭaḥ kuto bhayāt || 43.3 (= 214) ||

p.129, l.1

(p.129, l.1)vyāghraḥ | gaccha gaccha jambuka tvamapi kiṃcidgūḍhapradeśam | yato vyāghramārīti
(p.129, l.2)yā śāstre śrūyate tayāhaṃ hantumārabdhaḥ paraṃ gṛhītakarajīvito
(p.129, l.3)naṣṭaḥ śīghraṃ tadagrataḥ | mṛgadhūrtaḥ | vyāghra tvayā mahatkautukamāveditaṃ
(p.129, l.4)yanmāṃsapiṇḍānmānuṣādapi bibheṣi | vyāghraḥ | pratyakṣameva mayā sātmaputrāv
(p.129, l.5)ekaikaśo māmantuṃ kalahāyamānau capeṭayā ghnantī dṛṣṭā | jambukaḥ |
(p.129, l.6)svāminyatrāste sā dhūrtā tatra gamyatām | yadi vyāghra tava tatra gatasya
(p.129, l.7)sā saṃmukhamapīkṣate tadā mama tvadīyā velā smaraṇīyā | vyāghraḥ |
(p.129, l.8)śṛgāla yadi tvaṃ māṃ muktvā yāsi tadā velāpyavelā syāt | jambukaḥ |
(p.129, l.9)yadyevaṃ tarhi māṃ nijagale baddhvā cala śīghram | sa vyāghrastathā kṛtvā
(p.129, l.10)kānanaṃ yayau | vyāghramāryapi prāptā putrasahitā tena jambukakṛtotsāhād
(p.129, l.11)vyāghrātsā kathaṃ mucyatām | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tayā vyāghramāryā
(p.129, l.12)tadā cintitaṃ yadayaṃ mṛgadhūrtenānītastasmādamumeva jambukamākṣipanty
(p.129, l.13)aṅgulyā tarjayantyuvāca |

vyāghraḥ | gaccha gaccha jambuka tvamapi kiṃcidgūḍhapradeśam | yato vyāghramārīti yā śāstre śrūyate tayāhaṃ hantumārabdhaḥ paraṃ gṛhītakarajīvito naṣṭaḥ śīghraṃ tadagrataḥ | mṛgadhūrtaḥ | vyāghra tvayā mahatkautukamāveditaṃ yanmāṃsapiṇḍānmānuṣādapi bibheṣi | vyāghraḥ | pratyakṣameva mayā sātmaputrāv ekaikaśo māmantuṃ kalahāyamānau capeṭayā ghnantī dṛṣṭā | jambukaḥ | svāminyatrāste sā dhūrtā tatra gamyatām | yadi vyāghra tava tatra gatasya sā saṃmukhamapīkṣate tadā mama tvadīyā velā smaraṇīyā | vyāghraḥ | śṛgāla yadi tvaṃ māṃ muktvā yāsi tadā velāpyavelā syāt | jambukaḥ | yadyevaṃ tarhi māṃ nijagale baddhvā cala śīghram | sa vyāghrastathā kṛtvā kānanaṃ yayau | vyāghramāryapi prāptā putrasahitā tena jambukakṛtotsāhād vyāghrātsā kathaṃ mucyatām | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tayā vyāghramāryā tadā cintitaṃ yadayaṃ mṛgadhūrtenānītastasmādamumeva jambukamākṣipanty aṅgulyā tarjayantyuvāca |

p.129, l.14

  • (p.129, l.14)re re dhūrta tvayā dattaṃ mahyaṃ vyāghratrayaṃ purā | (p.129, l.15)viśvasyādyaikamānīya kathaṃ yāsi vadādhunā || 43.4 (= 215) ||
  • (p.130, l.1)ityuktvā dhāvitā tūrṇaṃ vyāghramārī bhayaṃkarā | (p.130, l.2)vyāghro 'pi sahasā naṣṭo galabaddhaśṛgālakaḥ || 43.5 (= 216) ||
  • (p.130, l.3)nijabuddhyā punarmuktā vyāghrajāddevi sā bhayāt | (p.130, l.4)buddhirbalavatī tanvi sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā || 43.6 (= 217) ||
re re dhūrta tvayā dattaṃ mahyaṃ vyāghratrayaṃ purā | viśvasyādyaikamānīya kathaṃ yāsi vadādhunā || 43.4 (= 215) ||
ityuktvā dhāvitā tūrṇaṃ vyāghramārī bhayaṃkarā | vyāghro 'pi sahasā naṣṭo galabaddhaśṛgālakaḥ || 43.5 (= 216) ||
nijabuddhyā punarmuktā vyāghrajāddevi sā bhayāt | buddhirbalavatī tanvi sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā || 43.6 (= 217) ||

p.130, l.8

p.130, l.10

(p.130, l.10)sa ca jambuko galabaddho nighṛṣṭapṛṣṭhacaraṇo galadrudhirapravāho mumūrṣuriva
(p.130, l.11)deśāntaraṃ gantumicchatā vyāghramārībhayādvyāghreṇa nīyate | tato mahato
(p.130, l.12)'pāyāt śṛgālaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ prāha śukaḥ |
(p.130, l.13)tatastaṃ vyāghraṃ bahunadīkānanaviṣamasamapradeśaparvatānullaṅghayantaṃ satvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā
(p.131, l.1)ātmānaṃ mocayitukāmaḥ śṛgālo bhṛśaṃ jahāsa pīḍito 'pi san |
(p.131, l.2)vyāghreṇoktam | kathaṃ hasitam | sa āha | deva sā mayā vyāghramārīti
(p.131, l.3)dhūrtikā jñātā | tvatprasādācca dūradeśamāgato 'haṃ jīvitaḥ |
(p.131, l.4)paraṃ yadi sāsmadraktasrāvasaṃlagnā pāpinī pṛṣṭhataḥ sameti tadā kathaṃ
(p.131, l.5)jīvitavyam | ato 'haṃ hasitaḥ | vyāghrasvāmin sthirībhūya vicāraya |
(p.131, l.6)atha tuṣṭo vyāghrastena vākyena tathetyuktvā jambukaṃ muktvā sahasā naṣṭaḥ |
(p.131, l.7)śṛgālo 'pi sukhaṃ tasthau |

sa ca jambuko galabaddho nighṛṣṭapṛṣṭhacaraṇo galadrudhirapravāho mumūrṣuriva deśāntaraṃ gantumicchatā vyāghramārībhayādvyāghreṇa nīyate | tato mahato 'pāyāt śṛgālaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ prāha śukaḥ | tatastaṃ vyāghraṃ bahunadīkānanaviṣamasamapradeśaparvatānullaṅghayantaṃ satvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ mocayitukāmaḥ śṛgālo bhṛśaṃ jahāsa pīḍito 'pi san | vyāghreṇoktam | kathaṃ hasitam | sa āha | deva sā mayā vyāghramārīti dhūrtikā jñātā | tvatprasādācca dūradeśamāgato 'haṃ jīvitaḥ | paraṃ yadi sāsmadraktasrāvasaṃlagnā pāpinī pṛṣṭhataḥ sameti tadā kathaṃ jīvitavyam | ato 'haṃ hasitaḥ | vyāghrasvāmin sthirībhūya vicāraya | atha tuṣṭo vyāghrastena vākyena tathetyuktvā jambukaṃ muktvā sahasā naṣṭaḥ | śṛgālo 'pi sukhaṃ tasthau |

  • (p.131, l.10)balaṃ prajñāvihīnasya parakāryāya kevalam | (p.131, l.11)girikūṭopamāṅgasya kuñjarasyeva dṛśyate || 44.3 (= 220) ||

p.132, l.1

  • (p.132, l.1)samayo 'yaṃ priyaṃ bhoktuṃ tava bhāmini saṃprati | (p.132, l.2)vañcitā vetsi cetkartuṃ kiṃcidviṣṇuḥ purā yathā || 45.1 (= 219bis) ||
samayo 'yaṃ priyaṃ bhoktuṃ tava bhāmini saṃprati | vañcitā vetsi cetkartuṃ kiṃcidviṣṇuḥ purā yathā || 45.1 (= 219bis) ||

p.132, l.3

(p.132, l.3)prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śuka āha | asti vilāsapuraṃ nāma nagaram |
(p.132, l.4)tatra ariṃdamo nāma rājā | tatra ca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo
(p.132, l.5)ratilolupaḥ kuṭumbavarjito ratikarmaṇi sarvanārīduḥsaha iti nagare
(p.132, l.6)prasiddho babhūva | veśyābhirapi na śakyate jetuṃ kiṃ punaḥ kulāṅganābhiḥ |
(p.132, l.7)tatra ratipriyā nāma gaṇikā | (yato gaṇikādīnāṃ bahavo bhedāḥ
(p.132, l.8)paraṃ pañca prasiddhāḥ | teṣu saṃlīnāḥ sarve 'pi bhavanti | te ceme pañca
(p.132, l.9)gaṇikā vilāsinī rūpājīvā arthavṛttikā dārikā ceti | eteṣāṃ
(p.132, l.10)bhedānāṃ sā sarvottamā gaṇikā |) atha sā ṣoḍaśa drammāngṛhītvā
(p.132, l.11)tamājuhāva | tamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā cāṭūktibhiḥ paricaryāṃ cakāra | so
(p.132, l.12)'pi cānyakāryanivṛttastasminneva ratikarmaṇi dattamanāstāṃ rantuṃ jetumārebhe |
(p.133, l.1)tayā ca sa ratilolupaḥ dravyārthaṃ vā parājayārthaṃ vā praharadvayaṃ yāvat
(p.133, l.2)soḍhaḥ | niśīthe cādhobhūmikāmāgatya kuṭṭinyagrato niveditaṃ yadduḥsaho
(p.133, l.3)'yaṃ dvijaḥ | paṇabandhaṃ samarpayitvā tamutkālaya | mayi jīvantyāṃ
(p.133, l.4)prāgeva bāhulyaṃ bhaviṣyati | kuṭṭinyāha | asmadgṛhe na ko 'pi kāmuko
(p.133, l.5)gaṇikāṃ jitvā paṇabandhaṃ jagrāha | tato 'hamenaṃ yāvatprapañcena niḥsārayāmi
(p.133, l.6)tāvatsoḍhavya iti | yadā cāhaṃ pippalamāruhya sūrpadvayena pakṣaśabdaṃ
(p.133, l.7)kurvāṇā kukkuṭadhvaniṃ vidadhāmi tadā vibhātamiti kṛtvā niḥsāraṇīyaḥ |
(p.133, l.8)ityuktvā preṣitoparibhūmau gaṇikā | yathoktaṃ ca kuṭṭinyā
(p.133, l.9)tāvatkṛtam | tasmin kṛte vibhātamiti kṛtvā niḥsārito dvijaḥ | yāvad
(p.133, l.10)gṛhadvārastho vyomamālokayate tadopari niśītho vartate | tadā sa
(p.133, l.11)vipraḥ kuṭṭinīparājito janamadhye parājayaṃ kathaṃ vahatu | iti praśnaḥ |
(p.133, l.12)śukaḥ | yadi vipraḥ kukkuṭadhvanisthānamavalokayati tāvatsūrpadvayayutāṃ
(p.133, l.13)kuṭṭinīṃ dadarśa | tena ca sā loṣṭenāhatya bhūmau pātitā pramadājanaiśca
(p.134, l.1)dhikkṛtā | sa ca brāhmaṇo grahaṇakaṃ dviguṇaṃ gṛhītvā puramadhye gaṇikāṃ
(p.134, l.2)viḍambya svagṛhaṃ yayau | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.134, l.3)iti śukasaptatau pañcacatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śuka āha | asti vilāsapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra ariṃdamo nāma rājā | tatra ca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo ratilolupaḥ kuṭumbavarjito ratikarmaṇi sarvanārīduḥsaha iti nagare prasiddho babhūva | veśyābhirapi na śakyate jetuṃ kiṃ punaḥ kulāṅganābhiḥ | tatra ratipriyā nāma gaṇikā | (yato gaṇikādīnāṃ bahavo bhedāḥ paraṃ pañca prasiddhāḥ | teṣu saṃlīnāḥ sarve 'pi bhavanti | te ceme pañca gaṇikā vilāsinī rūpājīvā arthavṛttikā dārikā ceti | eteṣāṃ bhedānāṃ sā sarvottamā gaṇikā |) atha sā ṣoḍaśa drammāngṛhītvā tamājuhāva | tamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā cāṭūktibhiḥ paricaryāṃ cakāra | so 'pi cānyakāryanivṛttastasminneva ratikarmaṇi dattamanāstāṃ rantuṃ jetumārebhe | tayā ca sa ratilolupaḥ dravyārthaṃ vā parājayārthaṃ vā praharadvayaṃ yāvat soḍhaḥ | niśīthe cādhobhūmikāmāgatya kuṭṭinyagrato niveditaṃ yadduḥsaho 'yaṃ dvijaḥ | paṇabandhaṃ samarpayitvā tamutkālaya | mayi jīvantyāṃ prāgeva bāhulyaṃ bhaviṣyati | kuṭṭinyāha | asmadgṛhe na ko 'pi kāmuko gaṇikāṃ jitvā paṇabandhaṃ jagrāha | tato 'hamenaṃ yāvatprapañcena niḥsārayāmi tāvatsoḍhavya iti | yadā cāhaṃ pippalamāruhya sūrpadvayena pakṣaśabdaṃ kurvāṇā kukkuṭadhvaniṃ vidadhāmi tadā vibhātamiti kṛtvā niḥsāraṇīyaḥ | ityuktvā preṣitoparibhūmau gaṇikā | yathoktaṃ ca kuṭṭinyā tāvatkṛtam | tasmin kṛte vibhātamiti kṛtvā niḥsārito dvijaḥ | yāvad gṛhadvārastho vyomamālokayate tadopari niśītho vartate | tadā sa vipraḥ kuṭṭinīparājito janamadhye parājayaṃ kathaṃ vahatu | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | yadi vipraḥ kukkuṭadhvanisthānamavalokayati tāvatsūrpadvayayutāṃ kuṭṭinīṃ dadarśa | tena ca sā loṣṭenāhatya bhūmau pātitā pramadājanaiśca dhikkṛtā | sa ca brāhmaṇo grahaṇakaṃ dviguṇaṃ gṛhītvā puramadhye gaṇikāṃ viḍambya svagṛhaṃ yayau | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcacatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.134, l.5

  • (p.134, l.5)yāhi devi gṛhaṃ muktvā yadi vetsi tvamuttaram | (p.134, l.6)yathā karagarānāthaḥ kṛtavānbhūtanigrahe || 46.1 (= 220bis) ||

p.134, l.7

(p.134, l.7)asti devi vatsomaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vidvāndaridro brāhmaṇaḥ |
(p.134, l.8)tasya priyā ca karagarābhidhānā yathārthanāmnī sarvajantūdvegakāriṇī yattaddvāradeśavṛkṣasthito
(p.134, l.9)bhūtastasyāḥ karagarāyā bhayātpalāyyāṭavyāṃ gataḥ |
(p.134, l.10)brāhmaṇo 'pi tasyā udvegāddeśāntarābhimukho 'bhūt | so 'pi ca tena
(p.135, l.1)bhūtena dṛṣṭo jalpitaśca | mārgaśrāntastvam | tena tvayādya mamātithinā
(p.135, l.2)bhāvyam | vipreṇa bhīruṇoktam | yadātithyaṃ karoṣi tadvidhehi śīghram |
(p.135, l.3)bhūtenoktam | na tvayā bhetavyam | tvaṃ mama svāmī yato 'haṃ tvadgṛhadvāravṛkṣastho
(p.135, l.4)bhūtaḥ karagarābhayenehāgataḥ | tatastava nijasvāmino guṇavad
(p.135, l.5)upakartavyameva | tasmāttvaṃ dvija mṛgāvatīṃ rājadhānīṃ madanabhūpatisanāthāṃ
(p.135, l.6)gaccha | tatra cāhaṃ tatputrīṃ mṛgalocanāṃ grahīṣye | sā cānyairmantrikairnīrujā
(p.135, l.7)na bhaviṣyati | tattvayi samāgate tava darśanādevāhaṃ tyakṣyāmi |
(p.135, l.8)tataḥ paraṃ tu mantravādo na vidheyaḥ | iti bhaṇitvā so 'pi bhūto
(p.135, l.9)gatvā tāṃ rājaputrīṃ jagrāha | vipro 'pi tatra yayau | tena ca ḍiṇḍimaḥ
(p.135, l.10)spṛṣṭaḥ | tato rājakulaṃ gato vipra ācāryavistaraṃ vidadhe | bhūta
(p.135, l.11)ācāryavistare yāvanna muñcati tāvatkiṃ karotviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ |
(p.135, l.12)bhūtagrahe 'nivartite vipreṇoktam |

asti devi vatsomaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vidvāndaridro brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya priyā ca karagarābhidhānā yathārthanāmnī sarvajantūdvegakāriṇī yattaddvāradeśavṛkṣasthito bhūtastasyāḥ karagarāyā bhayātpalāyyāṭavyāṃ gataḥ | brāhmaṇo 'pi tasyā udvegāddeśāntarābhimukho 'bhūt | so 'pi ca tena bhūtena dṛṣṭo jalpitaśca | mārgaśrāntastvam | tena tvayādya mamātithinā bhāvyam | vipreṇa bhīruṇoktam | yadātithyaṃ karoṣi tadvidhehi śīghram | bhūtenoktam | na tvayā bhetavyam | tvaṃ mama svāmī yato 'haṃ tvadgṛhadvāravṛkṣastho bhūtaḥ karagarābhayenehāgataḥ | tatastava nijasvāmino guṇavad upakartavyameva | tasmāttvaṃ dvija mṛgāvatīṃ rājadhānīṃ madanabhūpatisanāthāṃ gaccha | tatra cāhaṃ tatputrīṃ mṛgalocanāṃ grahīṣye | sā cānyairmantrikairnīrujā na bhaviṣyati | tattvayi samāgate tava darśanādevāhaṃ tyakṣyāmi | tataḥ paraṃ tu mantravādo na vidheyaḥ | iti bhaṇitvā so 'pi bhūto gatvā tāṃ rājaputrīṃ jagrāha | vipro 'pi tatra yayau | tena ca ḍiṇḍimaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tato rājakulaṃ gato vipra ācāryavistaraṃ vidadhe | bhūta ācāryavistare yāvanna muñcati tāvatkiṃ karotviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | bhūtagrahe 'nivartite vipreṇoktam |

p.136, l.1

  • (p.136, l.1)karagaraṇāhau āiau bhūa eu vīsasiu ṭhiu dhutta | (p.136, l.2)āpaṇi boliu saṃbhari re kūḍauṃ kiṃ maiṃ deva jutta || 46.2 (= 221) || (•)
  • (p.136, l.3)uktaṃ ca |
  • manuṣyāḥ sukulotpannā api ca brahmacāriṇaḥ | (p.136, l.4)na bhavanti mṛṣāvācaḥ kiṃ punardevayonayaḥ || 46.3 (= 222) ||
karagaraṇāhau āiau bhūa eu vīsasiu ṭhiu dhutta | āpaṇi boliu saṃbhari re kūḍauṃ kiṃ maiṃ deva jutta || 46.2 (= 221) || (•)

uktaṃ ca |

manuṣyāḥ sukulotpannā api ca brahmacāriṇaḥ | na bhavanti mṛṣāvācaḥ kiṃ punardevayonayaḥ || 46.3 (= 222) ||

p.136, l.5

(p.136, l.5)tato bhūtaḥ tyaktvā jagāma | iyaṃ muktetyuktvā brāhmaṇāya rājñā sutā
(p.136, l.6)rājyārdhaṃ ca pradattam | vipro 'pi pūrṇamanoratho jagāma | iti kathāṃ
(p.136, l.7)śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.136, l.8)iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

tato bhūtaḥ tyaktvā jagāma | iyaṃ muktetyuktvā brāhmaṇāya rājñā sutā rājyārdhaṃ ca pradattam | vipro 'pi pūrṇamanoratho jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.137, l.4

(p.137, l.4)sa karagarāpatiḥ rājakanyayā saha rājalakṣmīṃ bhuṅkte | atrāntare sa
(p.137, l.5)bhūtaḥ karṇāvatīṃ gatvā rājño bhāryāṃ sulocanāṃ jagrāha | sā madanasya
(p.137, l.6)pitṛṣvasā | sā cātyarthaṃ pīḍitā jīvitaśeṣābhūt | sāpi śatrughnanarapater
(p.137, l.7)bhāryā mātṛrājye keśavamāntrikamākārayāmāsa | sa ca nijadūtān
(p.137, l.8)preṣayitvā keśavo 'pi rājñā priyavākyaiḥ prahito 'pyagantukāmukaḥ |
(p.137, l.9)tadā sa karagarāpatirbhāryānurodhato jagāma | tatra gataḥ sanmānito
(p.137, l.10)mahībhujā śatrughnena gataḥ sulocanāveśmani | sa ca bhūtastamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā
(p.137, l.11)paruṣairvākyaistarjayannityāha | mayā pratipannamekadeśe kṛtam | adhunā tu
(p.137, l.12)vipra tvayā ātmā rakṣaṇīyaḥ | sa ca dvijo na mantraṃ na tantraṃ vijānāti |
(p.137, l.13)kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tadā taṃ bhūtaṃ jñātvā kālavedī
(p.137, l.14)kṛtāñjalirbhūtvā tatkarṇamāśrityeti jagāda dvijaḥ |

sa karagarāpatiḥ rājakanyayā saha rājalakṣmīṃ bhuṅkte | atrāntare sa bhūtaḥ karṇāvatīṃ gatvā rājño bhāryāṃ sulocanāṃ jagrāha | sā madanasya pitṛṣvasā | sā cātyarthaṃ pīḍitā jīvitaśeṣābhūt | sāpi śatrughnanarapater bhāryā mātṛrājye keśavamāntrikamākārayāmāsa | sa ca nijadūtān preṣayitvā keśavo 'pi rājñā priyavākyaiḥ prahito 'pyagantukāmukaḥ | tadā sa karagarāpatirbhāryānurodhato jagāma | tatra gataḥ sanmānito mahībhujā śatrughnena gataḥ sulocanāveśmani | sa ca bhūtastamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā paruṣairvākyaistarjayannityāha | mayā pratipannamekadeśe kṛtam | adhunā tu vipra tvayā ātmā rakṣaṇīyaḥ | sa ca dvijo na mantraṃ na tantraṃ vijānāti | kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tadā taṃ bhūtaṃ jñātvā kālavedī kṛtāñjalirbhūtvā tatkarṇamāśrityeti jagāda dvijaḥ |

(p.139, l.8)'pi nandarājye ghoṭikānirṇayaṃ kartuṃ na kṣamastadā nandarājā vyacintayat |
(p.139, l.9)śakaṭālaṃ vināhaṃ paribhavāspadaṃ jātaḥ |

sa ca rājā dharmanāśakaṃ kurvannirdravyāṃ ca medinīṃ vidadhāno niṣiddho mantriṇā | tatastenāpi mūrkheṇa rājñā sacivo 'vaṭe nikṣiptaḥ | sa ca saputrastatra ciraṃ tasthau | tataḥ śakaṭāle mahāmātye tatrasthe sarvatra mṛto mṛta iti vārttābhūt | tato vaṅgālanāthena tatparīkṣārthaṃ ātmīyapuruṣā ghoṭikādvayaṃ samarpya nandapārśve preṣitāḥ | yadetayormadhyātkā mātā kā ca putrī iti jñātvā samāgantavyam | sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇe sadṛśe ghoṭike tāni ca lakṣaṇāni śālihotrajñātavyāni | yadā ca ko 'pi nandarājye ghoṭikānirṇayaṃ kartuṃ na kṣamastadā nandarājā vyacintayat | śakaṭālaṃ vināhaṃ paribhavāspadaṃ jātaḥ |

(p.141, l.8)yathā pūrvaṃ tathaiva vaṅgālanātho yaṣṭikāṃ suvṛttāṃ dhvajācchidriṇīmayīṃ

(p.142, l.3)ādyantavibhāgaṃ na ko 'pi jānāti | tatastvayā nirṇayo vidheya eva |

p.143, l.4

(p.143, l.4)kathametat | śukaḥ | asti devi dharāpṛṣṭhe jāṅgalābhidho grāmaḥ | tatra
(p.143, l.5)mitradvayaṃ vartate dharmabuddhirduṣṭabuddhiśceti | anyadā tau dvāvapi dhanāśayā
(p.143, l.6)deśāntaraṃ gatau | kiyadbhirdinaiḥ pracuraṃ dhanamarjayitvā svagrāmāgatau
(p.143, l.7)parasparaṃ mantraṃ cakrāte | yatpippalādho dhanaṃ kiṃcitkṣiptvānyadgṛhe nīyate |
(p.143, l.8)paścātkrameṇa vibhajyate lagnam | iti kṛtvā tau nijagṛhaṃ jagmatur
(p.143, l.9)hṛṣṭatuṣṭau sukhāsvādatatparau sthitau | atrāntare yatkṛtaṃ duṣṭabuddhinā
(p.143, l.10)tanniśamyatām | na ca yujyate vaktum |

kathametat | śukaḥ | asti devi dharāpṛṣṭhe jāṅgalābhidho grāmaḥ | tatra mitradvayaṃ vartate dharmabuddhirduṣṭabuddhiśceti | anyadā tau dvāvapi dhanāśayā deśāntaraṃ gatau | kiyadbhirdinaiḥ pracuraṃ dhanamarjayitvā svagrāmāgatau parasparaṃ mantraṃ cakrāte | yatpippalādho dhanaṃ kiṃcitkṣiptvānyadgṛhe nīyate | paścātkrameṇa vibhajyate lagnam | iti kṛtvā tau nijagṛhaṃ jagmatur hṛṣṭatuṣṭau sukhāsvādatatparau sthitau | atrāntare yatkṛtaṃ duṣṭabuddhinā tanniśamyatām | na ca yujyate vaktum |

p.143, l.11

  • (p.143, l.11)yataḥ |
  • na vaktavyaṃ dhruvaṃ devi pāpaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā | (p.143, l.12)kathāpi khalu pāpānāmalamaśreyase yataḥ || 50.2 (= 237) ||

yataḥ |

na vaktavyaṃ dhruvaṃ devi pāpaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ mayā | kathāpi khalu pāpānāmalamaśreyase yataḥ || 50.2 (= 237) ||

p.143, l.13

(p.143, l.13)tena ca duṣṭabuddhinā taddravyamutpāṭya gṛhītvā nijagṛhamānītam | kālakrameṇa
(p.144, l.1)ca saṃmīlitau pippalādhaḥsthitaṃ dravyaṃ grahītuṃ gatau yāvadālokayataḥ
(p.144, l.2)tāvaddravyaṃ nāsti | dharmabuddhistato gatvā mantriṇo 'gre ācakhyau
(p.144, l.3)dhanavṛttāntaṃ hṛtaṃ cāpi kubuddhinā | kubuddhināhṛtena uttaraṃ kṛtam |
(p.144, l.4)sahasrasya paṇo muktaḥ | etadarthe śapathaṃ dāpayiṣyāmi | mantriṇoktamevam
(p.144, l.5)evāstu | dvitīyenāpi pratipannaṃ yadā tadā mantriṇā pratibhuvau gṛhītvā
(p.144, l.6)muktau gatau gehaṃ pṛthakpṛthak | tato duṣṭabuddhirnijaṃ pitaraṃ viditārthaṃ
(p.144, l.7)kṛtvā vṛkṣakoṭare cikṣepa | prabhāte sacivastau ca vādinau kautukī
(p.144, l.8)lokaśca taṃ pippalaṃ yayuḥ | duṣṭabuddhiḥ snātaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ satyaṃ
(p.144, l.9)kṛtvā jagāda | idaṃ satyaṃ brūhi nagottama | yadi mayā dravyamapahṛtaṃ
(p.144, l.10)tadānena hṛtamiti vācyam | yadi na hṛtaṃ tadānena na hṛtamiti
(p.144, l.11)vācyam | iti śrutvā tatpitrā nahīti jalpitaṃ sarvalokapratyakṣam |
(p.145, l.1)tato dharmabuddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavatu | iti praśnaḥ | tatsaṃdiṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha |
(p.145, l.2)dharmabuddhistaṃ śabdaṃ tatpiturjñātvā koṭare vahniṃ jajvāla | taṃ pitaraṃ koṭarāt
(p.145, l.3)pūtkurvantamardhajvalitaṃ ca patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā duṣṭabuddhernigrahaṃ vidhāya mantrī
(p.145, l.4)dharmabuddhimānandayāmāsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.145, l.5)iti śukasaptatau pañcāśattamī kathā ||

tena ca duṣṭabuddhinā taddravyamutpāṭya gṛhītvā nijagṛhamānītam | kālakrameṇa ca saṃmīlitau pippalādhaḥsthitaṃ dravyaṃ grahītuṃ gatau yāvadālokayataḥ tāvaddravyaṃ nāsti | dharmabuddhistato gatvā mantriṇo 'gre ācakhyau dhanavṛttāntaṃ hṛtaṃ cāpi kubuddhinā | kubuddhināhṛtena uttaraṃ kṛtam | sahasrasya paṇo muktaḥ | etadarthe śapathaṃ dāpayiṣyāmi | mantriṇoktamevam evāstu | dvitīyenāpi pratipannaṃ yadā tadā mantriṇā pratibhuvau gṛhītvā muktau gatau gehaṃ pṛthakpṛthak | tato duṣṭabuddhirnijaṃ pitaraṃ viditārthaṃ kṛtvā vṛkṣakoṭare cikṣepa | prabhāte sacivastau ca vādinau kautukī lokaśca taṃ pippalaṃ yayuḥ | duṣṭabuddhiḥ snātaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ satyaṃ kṛtvā jagāda | idaṃ satyaṃ brūhi nagottama | yadi mayā dravyamapahṛtaṃ tadānena hṛtamiti vācyam | yadi na hṛtaṃ tadānena na hṛtamiti vācyam | iti śrutvā tatpitrā nahīti jalpitaṃ sarvalokapratyakṣam | tato dharmabuddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavatu | iti praśnaḥ | tatsaṃdiṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | dharmabuddhistaṃ śabdaṃ tatpiturjñātvā koṭare vahniṃ jajvāla | taṃ pitaraṃ koṭarāt pūtkurvantamardhajvalitaṃ ca patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā duṣṭabuddhernigrahaṃ vidhāya mantrī dharmabuddhimānandayāmāsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcāśattamī kathā ||

p.148, l.3

(p.148, l.3)tato duṣṭena tena lobhābhibhūtena tadratnacatuṣṭayaṃ jaṅghāntare kṣiptvā sīvitam |
(p.148, l.4)ekadā anyadā ca mārge phūtkṛtaṃ paścāddūrasthitena vaṇijā
(p.148, l.5)muṣito 'smīti vadanaiḥ | tairuktam | kena hetunā | sā āha | mama
(p.148, l.6)mūtrotsargārthaṃ paścātsthitasya caureṇa mātrāpahṛtā viśvāpi | evaṃ ca
(p.148, l.7)nivedite tairjñātaṃ paśya dhūrto 'yam | nūnamanena vaṇijā kimapi kūṭaṃ
(p.148, l.8)kṛtaṃ bhaviṣyatīti manyamānā vivadantaḥ airāvatīṃ purīṃ yayuḥ | tatra ca
(p.148, l.9)nītisāra ityākhyāto bhūpatiḥ | tasya ca mantrī buddhisāro nāma
(p.148, l.10)jagadvikhyātaḥ | tasyaivaṃ prasiddhirdeśe deśāntare ca yadvivādināṃ vacanamuktamātraṃ
(p.148, l.11)jānāti | tataste rājaputrādyāstasmai mantriṇe ācakhyuḥ nijaṃ ratnagamanavṛttāntaṃ
(p.149, l.1)yathā jātam | tathaiva nirīkṣyāsmākaṃ madhye ratnajātaṃ vadhabandhaṃ
(p.149, l.2)vinā pṛthakpṛthak ekaikaṃ samarpaya | yadi ca nārpayasi tāni
(p.149, l.3)jñātvā tadā prasiddhirbhuvi te vyarthatāṃ yāti | buddhisāra iti śrutvā
(p.149, l.4)cintāvaṣṭabdhaḥ sthitaḥ | sa ca rājā nītisāraḥ kathaṃ syāditi praśnaḥ |
(p.149, l.5)śukaḥ prāha | yadā sa mantrī ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ tanmadhye sthitaṃ na janāti
(p.149, l.6)tadā viṣaṇṇo gṛhamāyayau | atrāntare mantriputrī prāptanavayauvanā pārvatīṃ
(p.149, l.7)natvā piturnamaskāraṇāya gatā jayaśrīnāmadheyā | pitaraṃ tādṛśaṃ sacintaṃ
(p.149, l.8)dṛṣṭvā viṣādakāraṇaṃ pṛcchati sma | tato mantrī yathāsthitamācaṣṭe |
(p.149, l.9)sutā prāha | tāta mā viṣīda | teṣāṃ nirṇayamahaṃ kariṣye | te vivādinaḥ
(p.149, l.10)pumāṃso yadā kāraṇāyāgacchanti tadā gṛhe preṣaṇīyāḥ yathāhaṃ
(p.149, l.11)tanmadhyādratnajātahartāraṃ samarpayāmi | sā āha | putri yanmayā na jñātaṃ
(p.149, l.12)tattvaṃ kathaṃ jñāsyasi | sā āha |

tato duṣṭena tena lobhābhibhūtena tadratnacatuṣṭayaṃ jaṅghāntare kṣiptvā sīvitam | ekadā anyadā ca mārge phūtkṛtaṃ paścāddūrasthitena vaṇijā muṣito 'smīti vadanaiḥ | tairuktam | kena hetunā | sā āha | mama mūtrotsargārthaṃ paścātsthitasya caureṇa mātrāpahṛtā viśvāpi | evaṃ ca nivedite tairjñātaṃ paśya dhūrto 'yam | nūnamanena vaṇijā kimapi kūṭaṃ kṛtaṃ bhaviṣyatīti manyamānā vivadantaḥ airāvatīṃ purīṃ yayuḥ | tatra ca nītisāra ityākhyāto bhūpatiḥ | tasya ca mantrī buddhisāro nāma jagadvikhyātaḥ | tasyaivaṃ prasiddhirdeśe deśāntare ca yadvivādināṃ vacanamuktamātraṃ jānāti | tataste rājaputrādyāstasmai mantriṇe ācakhyuḥ nijaṃ ratnagamanavṛttāntaṃ yathā jātam | tathaiva nirīkṣyāsmākaṃ madhye ratnajātaṃ vadhabandhaṃ vinā pṛthakpṛthak ekaikaṃ samarpaya | yadi ca nārpayasi tāni jñātvā tadā prasiddhirbhuvi te vyarthatāṃ yāti | buddhisāra iti śrutvā cintāvaṣṭabdhaḥ sthitaḥ | sa ca rājā nītisāraḥ kathaṃ syāditi praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā sa mantrī ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ tanmadhye sthitaṃ na janāti tadā viṣaṇṇo gṛhamāyayau | atrāntare mantriputrī prāptanavayauvanā pārvatīṃ natvā piturnamaskāraṇāya gatā jayaśrīnāmadheyā | pitaraṃ tādṛśaṃ sacintaṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣādakāraṇaṃ pṛcchati sma | tato mantrī yathāsthitamācaṣṭe | sutā prāha | tāta mā viṣīda | teṣāṃ nirṇayamahaṃ kariṣye | te vivādinaḥ pumāṃso yadā kāraṇāyāgacchanti tadā gṛhe preṣaṇīyāḥ yathāhaṃ tanmadhyādratnajātahartāraṃ samarpayāmi | sā āha | putri yanmayā na jñātaṃ tattvaṃ kathaṃ jñāsyasi | sā āha |

(p.150, l.6)tasmāttāta nātra kāpi cintā kāryā | prasthāpyāste 'nyadeśinaḥ yathā
(p.150, l.7)tān prabodhayāmi | prasthāpitāste mantriṇā tayāpi snāpitā bhojitāśca

(p.150, l.10)dattvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tenoktam | ahaṃ tava dravyaṃ rājyaṃ copārjya dāsyāmi |
(p.150, l.11)paramadhunā na kiṃcana vidyate | iti taṃ nirdravyaṃ jñātvā brāhmaṇaṃ
(p.150, l.12)gatā | brāhmaṇamapi pūrvoktamevoktavatī | brāhmaṇo jagāda | yadas matpituḥ
(p.150, l.13)pārśve dravyaṃ śāsanabaddhā bhūmirapi tatsarvaṃ tubhyaṃ dāsye | tamapi nirdhanaṃ
(p.150, l.14)jñātvā parityajya sūtradhāraṃ yayau | āha ca saḥ | sāṃprataṃ mama pārśve
(p.150, l.15)kiṃcinna vidyate paraṃ paścāllākṣaṃ dāsyāmi | tamapi nirdravyaṃ parityajya
(p.151, l.1)vaṇiksutaṃ yayau | tathaiva gaditavatī | sa āha | svāmini ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ
(p.151, l.2)gṛhītvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tato jaṅghāyāḥ samākṛṣya ratnajātaṃ samarpayām
(p.151, l.3)āsa | tataḥ sā savyājamutthāya śīlarakṣāṃ kurvāṇā jayaśrīrgṛhamāyayau |
(p.151, l.4)ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ piturarpayāmāsa | mantryapi tānākārya nijaṃ nijaṃ
(p.151, l.5)ratnaṃ samarpayāmāsa | te 'pi svaratnalābhātkṛtakṛtyā nijaṃ nijaṃ gṛhaṃ
(p.151, l.6)yayuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.151, l.7)iti śukasaptatī dvipañcāśattamī kathā ||

tasmāttāta nātra kāpi cintā kāryā | prasthāpyāste 'nyadeśinaḥ yathā tān prabodhayāmi | prasthāpitāste mantriṇā tayāpi snāpitā bhojitāśca pṛthakpṛthakśāyitāḥ | tataḥ sā śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya pradhānaṃ rājaputraṃ prāha | ahaṃ ratyarthinī tava pārśvaṃ samāgatā | tvaṃ ca mahyaṃ kāñcanaśataṃ dattvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tenoktam | ahaṃ tava dravyaṃ rājyaṃ copārjya dāsyāmi | paramadhunā na kiṃcana vidyate | iti taṃ nirdravyaṃ jñātvā brāhmaṇaṃ gatā | brāhmaṇamapi pūrvoktamevoktavatī | brāhmaṇo jagāda | yadas matpituḥ pārśve dravyaṃ śāsanabaddhā bhūmirapi tatsarvaṃ tubhyaṃ dāsye | tamapi nirdhanaṃ jñātvā parityajya sūtradhāraṃ yayau | āha ca saḥ | sāṃprataṃ mama pārśve kiṃcinna vidyate paraṃ paścāllākṣaṃ dāsyāmi | tamapi nirdravyaṃ parityajya vaṇiksutaṃ yayau | tathaiva gaditavatī | sa āha | svāmini ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ gṛhītvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tato jaṅghāyāḥ samākṛṣya ratnajātaṃ samarpayām āsa | tataḥ sā savyājamutthāya śīlarakṣāṃ kurvāṇā jayaśrīrgṛhamāyayau | ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ piturarpayāmāsa | mantryapi tānākārya nijaṃ nijaṃ ratnaṃ samarpayāmāsa | te 'pi svaratnalābhātkṛtakṛtyā nijaṃ nijaṃ gṛhaṃ yayuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatī dvipañcāśattamī kathā ||

(p.151, l.13)bhāryā paraṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tataḥ sa carmakāraścarmaṇāṃ krayaṇāya yadā
(p.152, l.1)bahirnirgataḥ tadā tayā upapatiḥ samānītaḥ | tayoścāntaḥ suratasevinoḥ
(p.152, l.2)patiścarmasamāyukto bahirāgataḥ | tataḥ sa upapatiḥ sā ca kathaṃ
(p.152, l.3)bhavetām | iti praśnaḥ | tatpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā patir

p.153, l.4

(p.153, l.4)prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti śakrāvatī nāma purī |
(p.153, l.5)tasyāṃ dharmadatto nāma rājā dharmādiguṇopetaḥ | tasyāmātyaḥ suśīlo
(p.153, l.6)nāma | tasya ca suto viṣṇunāmā saṃdhivigrahikaḥ pūrvamāsīt | tasmāt
(p.153, l.7)padādyadā bhraṣṭo dravyahīnaḥ kulāmātyo 'hamityahaṃkṛtaḥ karkaśaśca | tato
(p.153, l.8)rājā na kiṃcidvadati | mantrī ca kadācinnṛpamāha | devāsya viṣṇor
(p.153, l.9)upari kimiti ko 'pi prasādo na vidhīyate | rājā ca tasyopari
(p.153, l.10)vimukhastato na kiṃcidvadati | punarapyuktaṃ mantriṇā | svāminnayaṃ viṣṇur
(p.153, l.11)bhakto raktaḥ pravīṇo dūtakarmaṇi | taddevapādaiḥ kvāpi preṣayitvā
(p.154, l.1)parīkṣaṇīyaḥ | tato rājā tadvākyaṃ śrutvā tatpratikūlaḥ sanbhasmaprābhṛtaṃ
(p.154, l.2)mudrayā mudritaṃ samarpya śatrudamananṛpapārśve vidiśāyāṃ nagaryāṃ taṃ preṣayām
(p.154, l.3)āsa | so 'pi ca tatra gatastatprābhṛtaṃ bhasmamayamajānanmudritaṃ rājñaḥ
(p.154, l.4)puro muktavān | tasmiṃścāmaṅgalakāriṇi prābhṛte rājño 'gre mukte rājā
(p.154, l.5)kopāṭopasahito babhūva | tataḥ sa dūtastasmin prābhṛte samānīte kathaṃ
(p.154, l.6)kṣemamavāpnotu | iti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa viṣṇustaṃ kruddhaṃ
(p.154, l.7)dṛṣṭvā buddhimānidamuvāca | svāminmadīyena nāthenāśvamedho yajñaḥ kṛtaḥ |
(p.154, l.8)tasya kuṇḍasya tretāgnisaṃbhavaṃ pavitraṃ śreyaskaramaghāpahaṃ bhasma vandanāya
(p.154, l.9)samarpitavān |

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti śakrāvatī nāma purī | tasyāṃ dharmadatto nāma rājā dharmādiguṇopetaḥ | tasyāmātyaḥ suśīlo nāma | tasya ca suto viṣṇunāmā saṃdhivigrahikaḥ pūrvamāsīt | tasmāt padādyadā bhraṣṭo dravyahīnaḥ kulāmātyo 'hamityahaṃkṛtaḥ karkaśaśca | tato rājā na kiṃcidvadati | mantrī ca kadācinnṛpamāha | devāsya viṣṇor upari kimiti ko 'pi prasādo na vidhīyate | rājā ca tasyopari vimukhastato na kiṃcidvadati | punarapyuktaṃ mantriṇā | svāminnayaṃ viṣṇur bhakto raktaḥ pravīṇo dūtakarmaṇi | taddevapādaiḥ kvāpi preṣayitvā parīkṣaṇīyaḥ | tato rājā tadvākyaṃ śrutvā tatpratikūlaḥ sanbhasmaprābhṛtaṃ mudrayā mudritaṃ samarpya śatrudamananṛpapārśve vidiśāyāṃ nagaryāṃ taṃ preṣayām āsa | so 'pi ca tatra gatastatprābhṛtaṃ bhasmamayamajānanmudritaṃ rājñaḥ puro muktavān | tasmiṃścāmaṅgalakāriṇi prābhṛte rājño 'gre mukte rājā kopāṭopasahito babhūva | tataḥ sa dūtastasmin prābhṛte samānīte kathaṃ kṣemamavāpnotu | iti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa viṣṇustaṃ kruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā buddhimānidamuvāca | svāminmadīyena nāthenāśvamedho yajñaḥ kṛtaḥ | tasya kuṇḍasya tretāgnisaṃbhavaṃ pavitraṃ śreyaskaramaghāpahaṃ bhasma vandanāya samarpitavān |

p.156, l.1

(p.156, l.1)prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śuko brūte | carmakūṭe grāme dvijaḥ śrīdharo
(p.156, l.2)nāma | tatraiva candanākhyaścarmakāraḥ | tatpārśvāt śrīdhareṇopānahayugalaṃ
(p.156, l.3)kāritam | carmakāro 'pi nityameva dravyaṃ yācate | vipro 'pi vadati |
(p.156, l.4)tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣye | evaṃ sumahān kālo yayau | sa vipro
(p.156, l.5)'nyadā carmakāreṇa vidhṛtaḥ | dhanaṃ vinā sa vipraḥ kathaṃ mucyate | tatkathayeti
(p.156, l.6)praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ prāha | etasminnantare grāmapālasya gṛhe
(p.156, l.7)suto jātaḥ | tato dvijaḥ prāha chalānveṣī san | carmakṛnmayā pūrvam
(p.156, l.8)uktam | tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣyāmi | tadasmin sute jāte tvaṃ hṛṣṭacitto
(p.156, l.9)na veti | yadi sa brūte nāhaṃ hṛṣṭacitta iti tadā rājñā grāhyaḥ
(p.156, l.10)syāt | anyathā ca dravyaṃ yāti | tatastenoktam | hṛṣṭacitto 'haṃ jātaḥ |
(p.157, l.1)tato dvijaśchalenātmānaṃ vimucya gataḥ | tato bhāmini yadyevamuttaraṃ
(p.157, l.2)jānāsi tadā gaccha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.157, l.3)iti śukasaptatau pañcapañcāśattamī kathā ||

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śuko brūte | carmakūṭe grāme dvijaḥ śrīdharo nāma | tatraiva candanākhyaścarmakāraḥ | tatpārśvāt śrīdhareṇopānahayugalaṃ kāritam | carmakāro 'pi nityameva dravyaṃ yācate | vipro 'pi vadati | tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣye | evaṃ sumahān kālo yayau | sa vipro 'nyadā carmakāreṇa vidhṛtaḥ | dhanaṃ vinā sa vipraḥ kathaṃ mucyate | tatkathayeti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ prāha | etasminnantare grāmapālasya gṛhe suto jātaḥ | tato dvijaḥ prāha chalānveṣī san | carmakṛnmayā pūrvam uktam | tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣyāmi | tadasmin sute jāte tvaṃ hṛṣṭacitto na veti | yadi sa brūte nāhaṃ hṛṣṭacitta iti tadā rājñā grāhyaḥ syāt | anyathā ca dravyaṃ yāti | tatastenoktam | hṛṣṭacitto 'haṃ jātaḥ | tato dvijaśchalenātmānaṃ vimucya gataḥ | tato bhāmini yadyevamuttaraṃ jānāsi tadā gaccha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcapañcāśattamī kathā ||

(p.158, l.1)galagrahanāmno yakṣasya samīpavartino 'ntikaṃ yayau | tasyāgrataśca
(p.158, l.2)dravyaṃ muktvā haste ca khaṭikāmādāya yakṣādhīśamidamabravīt |

astyatra tripatho nāma grāmaḥ | tatra sāntako nāma vaṇik mahādhanī kṛpaṇo duṣṭaśīlo grāmāntarapriyaśca | tataśca grāmāntarādudgrāhaṇikāṃ kṛtvā āgacchan pathi caurairdhṛtaḥ sa bhāmini kathaṃ caurabhayānmucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | sa vaṇikputra ātmānaṃ caurairdhṛtaṃ jñātvā galagrahanāmno yakṣasya samīpavartino 'ntikaṃ yayau | tasyāgrataśca dravyaṃ muktvā haste ca khaṭikāmādāya yakṣādhīśamidamabravīt |

p.158, l.5

p.158, l.9

  • (p.158, l.9)pradoṣe 'nyatra sā bālā punaḥ prāha vihaṅgamam | (p.158, l.10)sukhaṃ bhoktuṃ vrajāmyadya narāntararatodbhavam || 57.1 (= 253) ||

p.165, l.10

(p.165, l.10)paṇḍito 'pi rājñaḥ prasādātsukhaṃ bhuṅkte tayā samam | yadyevaṃ prabhāvati

(p.165, l.12)iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.165, l.13)iti śukasaptatau saptapañcāśattamī kathā ||

paṇḍito 'pi rājñaḥ prasādātsukhaṃ bhuṅkte tayā samam | yadyevaṃ prabhāvati tvamapi samaye vaktuṃ jānāsi tadā gamyatām | anyathā sthīyatām | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptapañcāśattamī kathā ||

§ 58

p.166, l.1

(p.166, l.1)anyadā pradoṣe calitā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

anyadā pradoṣe calitā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.166, l.2

  • (p.166, l.2)ratyarthini vrajādya tvaṃ rantuṃ cetsamayocitam | (p.166, l.3)duḥśīlāpativadvetsi kartuṃ gaṇapateḥ puraḥ || 58.1 (= 276) ||

p.166, l.4

(p.166, l.4)prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti lohapurī nāma nagaram |
(p.166, l.5)tasmiṃśca rājaḍo nāma pāmaraḥ | tasyāpi patnī parapuruṣalampaṭā duḥśīlety
(p.166, l.6)āhvayā | sā ca sūtravikrayārthaṃ sakhībhiḥ sametya padmāvatīṃ purīṃ
(p.166, l.7)prayāti | tataśca grāmasamīpasthasya gaṇapatestābhiḥ pṛthakpṛthak upayācitam
(p.166, l.8)uktam | tayā tu cumbanamupayācitamuktaṃ madanākrāntadehayā | sa
(p.166, l.9)ca tāsāṃ prabhūtaṃ lābhaṃ cakre | tataḥ sarvābhiranyābhirātmīyātmīyamupayācitaṃ
(p.166, l.10)tasmai gaṇeśāya pradattam | tayā ca nagnībhūya cumbanaṃ kṛtam |
(p.166, l.11)tataḥ kelipriyeṇa tena sā adhare dhṛtā | tasmiṃśca dhṛte sā kukkuṭīva
(p.166, l.12)tatra sthitā | taṃ ca vṛttāntaṃ tanmokṣaṇāya tadbhartuḥ sakhyo 'pahasamānā nivedayām
(p.167, l.1)āsuḥ | so 'pi tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tatrāgamat | tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ
(p.167, l.2)dṛṣṭvā sa vyacintayat | kathamiyaṃ mucyata iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tāṃ
(p.167, l.3)tathāsthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ sanrāsabhaṃ rantumārebhe | tataśca sa gaṇapatis
(p.167, l.4)tathāvidhaṃ kautukaṃ dṛṣṭvā jahāsa | hasatastasya oṣṭhau śithilau jātau |
(p.167, l.5)tataḥ sā muktā satī praṇamya nijaṃ nāthaṃ tarjayantī gṛhaṃ yayau |

prabhāvatyāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti lohapurī nāma nagaram | tasmiṃśca rājaḍo nāma pāmaraḥ | tasyāpi patnī parapuruṣalampaṭā duḥśīlety āhvayā | sā ca sūtravikrayārthaṃ sakhībhiḥ sametya padmāvatīṃ purīṃ prayāti | tataśca grāmasamīpasthasya gaṇapatestābhiḥ pṛthakpṛthak upayācitam uktam | tayā tu cumbanamupayācitamuktaṃ madanākrāntadehayā | sa ca tāsāṃ prabhūtaṃ lābhaṃ cakre | tataḥ sarvābhiranyābhirātmīyātmīyamupayācitaṃ tasmai gaṇeśāya pradattam | tayā ca nagnībhūya cumbanaṃ kṛtam | tataḥ kelipriyeṇa tena sā adhare dhṛtā | tasmiṃśca dhṛte sā kukkuṭīva tatra sthitā | taṃ ca vṛttāntaṃ tanmokṣaṇāya tadbhartuḥ sakhyo 'pahasamānā nivedayām āsuḥ | so 'pi tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tatrāgamat | tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa vyacintayat | kathamiyaṃ mucyata iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tāṃ tathāsthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ sanrāsabhaṃ rantumārebhe | tataśca sa gaṇapatis tathāvidhaṃ kautukaṃ dṛṣṭvā jahāsa | hasatastasya oṣṭhau śithilau jātau | tataḥ sā muktā satī praṇamya nijaṃ nāthaṃ tarjayantī gṛhaṃ yayau |

p.167, l.6

  • (p.167, l.6)kṛtaṃ tena rataṃ devi samayocitamīdṛśam | (p.167, l.7)svakārye mocitā sāpi duḥśīlā vighnanāyakāt || 58.2 (= 277) ||
  • (p.167, l.8)samayocitamārambhaṃ kurute yastu kṛtyavit | (p.167, l.9)sarvadā tu phalaṃ tasya samayajño hi śiṣyate || 58.3 (= 278) ||
kṛtaṃ tena rataṃ devi samayocitamīdṛśam | svakārye mocitā sāpi duḥśīlā vighnanāyakāt || 58.2 (= 277) ||
samayocitamārambhaṃ kurute yastu kṛtyavit | sarvadā tu phalaṃ tasya samayajño hi śiṣyate || 58.3 (= 278) ||

p.167, l.10

(p.169, l.1)tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ vikṛtāṃ jñātvā ca rāhaḍo gṛhamagamat | dhikkṛtya paruṣākṣarair

(p.169, l.3)jīvitaṃ yauvanaṃ ca tadā saphalaṃ yadā etasya pratyakṣaṃ narāntaramupabhokṣye |
(p.169, l.4)pratijñātaṃ ca manasā dṛḍham | tata ātmīyapratijñāṃ kathaṃ nirvāhayatviti
(p.169, l.5)praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā kadācittaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ naraṃ gṛhapārśve gacchantaṃ
(p.169, l.6)dṛṣṭvā taṃ pratyāha | adya rātrau tvayāsmadgṛhāṅgaṇasthaciñciṇīmūle nijakāyākāragartāyām
(p.169, l.7)ūrdhvaliṅginā śayanaṃ vidheyamiti | sa tatheti pratijñāya
(p.169, l.8)rātrau tathā bhūtvā sthitaḥ | sā ca kāmārtā sarvakaraṇacaturā
(p.169, l.9)tatra yayau | agārabhūmimuddiśya bhartāramāhvayati sma | sā
(p.170, l.1)ciñciṇīcchāyāyāṃ gatvā tasya liṅgasyopari upaviśya satūṇadhanuṣaṃ
(p.170, l.2)tamabravīt |

tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ vikṛtāṃ jñātvā ca rāhaḍo gṛhamagamat | dhikkṛtya paruṣākṣarair gṛhāntare yantritāṃ dhārayāmāsa | sā ca cintayati | mama janma jīvitaṃ yauvanaṃ ca tadā saphalaṃ yadā etasya pratyakṣaṃ narāntaramupabhokṣye | pratijñātaṃ ca manasā dṛḍham | tata ātmīyapratijñāṃ kathaṃ nirvāhayatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā kadācittaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ naraṃ gṛhapārśve gacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ pratyāha | adya rātrau tvayāsmadgṛhāṅgaṇasthaciñciṇīmūle nijakāyākāragartāyām ūrdhvaliṅginā śayanaṃ vidheyamiti | sa tatheti pratijñāya rātrau tathā bhūtvā sthitaḥ | sā ca kāmārtā sarvakaraṇacaturā tatra yayau | agārabhūmimuddiśya bhartāramāhvayati sma | sā ciñciṇīcchāyāyāṃ gatvā tasya liṅgasyopari upaviśya satūṇadhanuṣaṃ tamabravīt |

p.175, l.5

  • (p.175, l.5)yataḥ |

  • (p.175, l.7)uktaṃ ca |
  • gṛhe 'raṇye tathā deve havye tīrthe jalāśaye | (p.175, l.8)vivāhe cotsave nityaṃ mālinīnilaye tathā || 61.3 (= 307) ||
  • (p.175, l.9)yātrāyāṃ strīsamūhe ca nirjane janasaṃkule | (p.175, l.10)pattane ca tathā grāme svacchandā dvāravartinī || 61.4 (= 308) ||
  • (p.176, l.1)khale kṣetre pravāse ca mārge veśmani catvare | (p.176, l.2)praveśe nirgame rājñāṃ sadā yā kautukapriyā || 61.5 (= 309) ||
  • (p.176, l.3)prativeśmagṛhe śūnye rajakīsūcikīgṛhe | (p.176, l.4)divārātrau ca saṃdhyāyāṃ durdine rājacatvare | (p.176, l.5)śoke ca vyasane bhartuḥ svacchandā strī vinaśyati || 61.6 (= 310) ||

yataḥ |

vivāhe devayātrāyāṃ rājaveśmani saṃkaṭe | paragehe vivāde ca devi nārī vinaśyati || 61.2 (= 306) ||

uktaṃ ca |

gṛhe 'raṇye tathā deve havye tīrthe jalāśaye | vivāhe cotsave nityaṃ mālinīnilaye tathā || 61.3 (= 307) ||
yātrāyāṃ strīsamūhe ca nirjane janasaṃkule | pattane ca tathā grāme svacchandā dvāravartinī || 61.4 (= 308) ||
khale kṣetre pravāse ca mārge veśmani catvare | praveśe nirgame rājñāṃ sadā yā kautukapriyā || 61.5 (= 309) ||

p.176, l.6

(p.176, l.6)tejukā ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhrūsaṃjñayā āhūyedamabravīt | ahaṃ tavāsaktā paraṃ
(p.176, l.7)madīyo bhartā duḥsaho niṣṭhuraśca gṛhādbahirnirgantuṃ notsahe | ato yasmiṃs
(p.176, l.8)tasmindivase 'smadgṛhadvāri ghaṭe kṣiptvā vṛściko moktavyaḥ | tadāhaṃ
(p.176, l.9)vṛścikadaṣṭā bhaviṣyāmi | tvayāsmadgṛhadvāri vaidyena bhāvyam | iti saṃketaṃ
(p.176, l.10)vidhāya svagṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tenāpi tathā kṛtam | sāpi ghaṭaṃ khaṭvocchīrṣake
(p.176, l.11)kṣiptvā iti jagāda | ahamanena vṛścikena ghaṭasthena daṣṭā |
(p.177, l.1)iti rāraṭīti | so 'pi ca puruṣastadā vaidyo bhūtvā tadgṛhadvāri
(p.177, l.2)tasthau | tāḍaṃ bandhau poṭṭaṃ malau sūlaṃ pheḍau visaṃ harau iti jalpati |
(p.177, l.3)tadā ca sā bhartāraṃ jagāda |

tejukā ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhrūsaṃjñayā āhūyedamabravīt | ahaṃ tavāsaktā paraṃ madīyo bhartā duḥsaho niṣṭhuraśca gṛhādbahirnirgantuṃ notsahe | ato yasmiṃs tasmindivase 'smadgṛhadvāri ghaṭe kṣiptvā vṛściko moktavyaḥ | tadāhaṃ vṛścikadaṣṭā bhaviṣyāmi | tvayāsmadgṛhadvāri vaidyena bhāvyam | iti saṃketaṃ vidhāya svagṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tenāpi tathā kṛtam | sāpi ghaṭaṃ khaṭvocchīrṣake kṣiptvā iti jagāda | ahamanena vṛścikena ghaṭasthena daṣṭā | iti rāraṭīti | so 'pi ca puruṣastadā vaidyo bhūtvā tadgṛhadvāri tasthau | tāḍaṃ bandhau poṭṭaṃ malau sūlaṃ pheḍau visaṃ harau iti jalpati | tadā ca sā bhartāraṃ jagāda |

p.177, l.4

  • (p.177, l.4)dehi kāṣṭhāni me nātha mariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ | (p.177, l.5)āhūya māntrikānvaidyāngatārtiṃ vā kuruṣva mām || 61.7 (= 311) ||
dehi kāṣṭhāni me nātha mariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ | āhūya māntrikānvaidyāngatārtiṃ vā kuruṣva mām || 61.7 (= 311) ||

p.177, l.6

(p.177, l.6)tatastadbhartā gṛhādbahiḥ sthitaṃ tamākārayāmāsa | vaidyo 'pi tāṃ dṛṣṭvā
(p.177, l.7)tatpatiṃ jagāda | yadyeṣā kāladaṣṭā jīvati tatastvaṃ bhāgyavānahamapi
(p.177, l.8)yaśaḥpātraṃ bhavāmi | vaṇigāha | vaidya prasādaṃ vidhāya enāṃ viṣarahitāṃ
(p.177, l.9)kuru | tataḥ sa vaidyaḥ kenāpi kaṭukabhaiṣajyena vanitauṣṭhamālipya tatpatim
(p.178, l.1)āha | aho vaṇiksarveṣāmapi viṣāṇāṃ samadhikaṃ mānuṣaviṣameva |
(p.178, l.2)tato viṣasya viṣamauṣadhamiti kṛtvā tvamasyā oṣṭhaṃ dhāva | tato
(p.178, l.3)vaṇiktathā kartumārebhe | kṣaṇamātreṇa tasya vaṇijaḥ kaṭukauṣadhamiśrauṣṭhāsvādena
(p.178, l.4)mukhaṃ kaṭukaṃ saṃjātam | tato vaṇigāha | tvamevauṣṭhaṃ dhāvetyuktvā
(p.178, l.5)vaṇiksthitaḥ | vaṇijo 'pi viṣaśaṅkārūḍhā | tato bahirgate vaṇiji
(p.178, l.6)vaidyena sā kāmārtā yathecchaṃ bhojitā | tadanantaraṃ sā māyinī svasthābhūt |
(p.178, l.7)vaṇigapi kṣaṇena svastho babhūva | upakṛtaśca vaidyastena caraṇaiḥ
(p.178, l.8)spṛṣṭvā tvadīyo 'smīti | tataḥ sa vaidyacchadmanā gṛhamāyāti satataṃ
(p.179, l.1)vaṇiji bahirgate bhuṅkte ca tāṃ nityam | tato bhāmini evaṃ kartuṃ vaktuṃ
(p.179, l.2)ca yadi jānāsi tato yāhi |

tatastadbhartā gṛhādbahiḥ sthitaṃ tamākārayāmāsa | vaidyo 'pi tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tatpatiṃ jagāda | yadyeṣā kāladaṣṭā jīvati tatastvaṃ bhāgyavānahamapi yaśaḥpātraṃ bhavāmi | vaṇigāha | vaidya prasādaṃ vidhāya enāṃ viṣarahitāṃ kuru | tataḥ sa vaidyaḥ kenāpi kaṭukabhaiṣajyena vanitauṣṭhamālipya tatpatim āha | aho vaṇiksarveṣāmapi viṣāṇāṃ samadhikaṃ mānuṣaviṣameva | tato viṣasya viṣamauṣadhamiti kṛtvā tvamasyā oṣṭhaṃ dhāva | tato vaṇiktathā kartumārebhe | kṣaṇamātreṇa tasya vaṇijaḥ kaṭukauṣadhamiśrauṣṭhāsvādena mukhaṃ kaṭukaṃ saṃjātam | tato vaṇigāha | tvamevauṣṭhaṃ dhāvetyuktvā vaṇiksthitaḥ | vaṇijo 'pi viṣaśaṅkārūḍhā | tato bahirgate vaṇiji vaidyena sā kāmārtā yathecchaṃ bhojitā | tadanantaraṃ sā māyinī svasthābhūt | vaṇigapi kṣaṇena svastho babhūva | upakṛtaśca vaidyastena caraṇaiḥ spṛṣṭvā tvadīyo 'smīti | tataḥ sa vaidyacchadmanā gṛhamāyāti satataṃ vaṇiji bahirgate bhuṅkte ca tāṃ nityam | tato bhāmini evaṃ kartuṃ vaktuṃ ca yadi jānāsi tato yāhi |

p.179, l.3

  • (p.179, l.3)evaṃ kartuṃ ca vaktuṃ ca yo jānāti chalapriyaḥ | (p.179, l.4)sa karotu sa yātvevaṃ kartuṃ bhoktuṃ nijaṃ hitam || 61.8 (= 312) ||
evaṃ kartuṃ ca vaktuṃ ca yo jānāti chalapriyaḥ | sa karotu sa yātvevaṃ kartuṃ bhoktuṃ nijaṃ hitam || 61.8 (= 312) ||

p.180, l.1

(p.180, l.1)asti gambhīrākhyo grāmaḥ | tatra kuhano nāma rājaputra īrṣyāluḥ śūro
(p.180, l.2)jaḍaḥ strīpriyo durdharaśca | tasyābhūtāṃ dve kalatre śobhikātejikākhye
(p.180, l.3)ratalolupe parapuruṣalampaṭe surūpe | tadbhartā tadrakṣaṇāya grāmādbahirnadītīre
(p.180, l.4)gṛhaṃ cakre | dvārasthaste rakṣayati | anyadā sa tābhyāmuktaḥ | yadā
(p.180, l.5)kaścinnāpitaḥ samabhyeti tadā bhavyaṃ bhavati | tatastenāpi bhrāmako nāpitaḥ
(p.180, l.6)preṣitaḥ pratisīrāntaraistayornakhakalpanāya | tataśca tayoścaraṇān
(p.180, l.7)tiras kariṇībahiḥsthānnāpitaḥ prakṣālayati | patiścādūre pathi niviṣṭaḥ |
(p.180, l.8)tābhyāṃ ca sa nāpitaḥ suvarṇakaṭakamarpayitvā pracchannamevamuktaḥ | etaddravyaṃ
(p.180, l.9)gṛhītvā āvayoḥ kenāpi sārdhaṃ saṃyogaṃ vidhehi | divākīrtirapi
(p.180, l.10)tatheti pratijñāya rājaputramāpṛcchya jagāma | anyadātmamitraṃ navayauvanaṃ
(p.181, l.1)kalāpātramanudgataśmaśruṃ strīveṣaṃ kārayitvā tayoḥ patyuḥ pārśve tena saha
(p.181, l.2)samāgatya nāpita idamāha | mameyaṃ vallabhā | ahaṃ ca grāmāntaraṃ jigamiṣur
(p.181, l.3)yuṣmadgṛhaṃ vinānyatra moktuṃ na śaknomi | yato bhavatāṃ gṛhe strīyantraṇā
(p.181, l.4)bhavyā | ityukte tena pratipannaṃ muñceti | tataścaṇḍālo 'pi taṃ
(p.181, l.5)muktvā tayoḥ pārśve gato jagāda yadiyaṃ yuṣmābhirātmīyā karaṇīyā |
(p.181, l.6)tataste taṃ caṇḍālānītaṃ jñātvā bahu menāte | sa ca divā strīrūpī
(p.181, l.7)rātrau ca kāmukaḥ rājaputrakalatre prativāraṃ bhuṅkte | sa ca rājaputraḥ
(p.181, l.8)strīlolupastatsaṅgamāya spṛhayati | yayāce ca tāṃ nityam | sā tu
(p.181, l.9)kapaṭastrī neti jagāda | tato rājaputrasya strītve bhrāntirutpannā | tadbhrāntim
(p.181, l.10)apanetuṃ nijakalatre jagāda | devyādeśānmayā prātarmahotsavo vidheyaḥ |
(p.182, l.1)tatra bhavatībhirvivastrābhistisṛbhirapi nartitavyam | tataḥ sa strīcchadmā
(p.182, l.2)kathaṃ nṛtyatu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | tantryā liṅgāgraṃ niyamya
(p.182, l.3)gudamadhyagamānamya sphuṭāṃ bhagākṛtiṃ kṛtvā patyau samāgate sahastatālaṃ
(p.182, l.4)sarvā evaṃ vadantyo nanṛtuḥ |

asti gambhīrākhyo grāmaḥ | tatra kuhano nāma rājaputra īrṣyāluḥ śūro jaḍaḥ strīpriyo durdharaśca | tasyābhūtāṃ dve kalatre śobhikātejikākhye ratalolupe parapuruṣalampaṭe surūpe | tadbhartā tadrakṣaṇāya grāmādbahirnadītīre gṛhaṃ cakre | dvārasthaste rakṣayati | anyadā sa tābhyāmuktaḥ | yadā kaścinnāpitaḥ samabhyeti tadā bhavyaṃ bhavati | tatastenāpi bhrāmako nāpitaḥ preṣitaḥ pratisīrāntaraistayornakhakalpanāya | tataśca tayoścaraṇān tiras kariṇībahiḥsthānnāpitaḥ prakṣālayati | patiścādūre pathi niviṣṭaḥ | tābhyāṃ ca sa nāpitaḥ suvarṇakaṭakamarpayitvā pracchannamevamuktaḥ | etaddravyaṃ gṛhītvā āvayoḥ kenāpi sārdhaṃ saṃyogaṃ vidhehi | divākīrtirapi tatheti pratijñāya rājaputramāpṛcchya jagāma | anyadātmamitraṃ navayauvanaṃ kalāpātramanudgataśmaśruṃ strīveṣaṃ kārayitvā tayoḥ patyuḥ pārśve tena saha samāgatya nāpita idamāha | mameyaṃ vallabhā | ahaṃ ca grāmāntaraṃ jigamiṣur yuṣmadgṛhaṃ vinānyatra moktuṃ na śaknomi | yato bhavatāṃ gṛhe strīyantraṇā bhavyā | ityukte tena pratipannaṃ muñceti | tataścaṇḍālo 'pi taṃ muktvā tayoḥ pārśve gato jagāda yadiyaṃ yuṣmābhirātmīyā karaṇīyā | tataste taṃ caṇḍālānītaṃ jñātvā bahu menāte | sa ca divā strīrūpī rātrau ca kāmukaḥ rājaputrakalatre prativāraṃ bhuṅkte | sa ca rājaputraḥ strīlolupastatsaṅgamāya spṛhayati | yayāce ca tāṃ nityam | sā tu kapaṭastrī neti jagāda | tato rājaputrasya strītve bhrāntirutpannā | tadbhrāntim apanetuṃ nijakalatre jagāda | devyādeśānmayā prātarmahotsavo vidheyaḥ | tatra bhavatībhirvivastrābhistisṛbhirapi nartitavyam | tataḥ sa strīcchadmā kathaṃ nṛtyatu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | tantryā liṅgāgraṃ niyamya gudamadhyagamānamya sphuṭāṃ bhagākṛtiṃ kṛtvā patyau samāgate sahastatālaṃ sarvā evaṃ vadantyo nanṛtuḥ |

(p.184, l.10)prabhāvatī prāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti kūṭapurābhidho grāmaḥ |
(p.185, l.1)tatra rājaputraḥ somarājaḥ | tasya maṇḍukā nāma patnī priyadarśanā
(p.185, l.2)narāntaralolupā | tāṃ caiko naraḥ kṛtasaṃketaḥ saghaṇṭako rātrau gṛhāṅgaṇe
(p.185, l.3)bhuṅkte | tatpatirghaṇṭāśabdaṃ śṛṇvannekadā laguḍamādāya pradhāvitaḥ ṣaṇḍaśaṅkayā |

(p.185, l.6)dṛṣṭvā jārasya naśyato ghaṇṭālālāṃ haste dhṛtvā taṃ prati jagāda | bhāvuka
(p.185, l.7)kāṃdiśīko vṛṣo naṣṭaḥ | tataḥ sa vyāvṛtya nijapauruṣaṃ patnyai kathayām
(p.185, l.8)āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.185, l.9)iti śukasaptatau catuḥṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

prabhāvatī prāha | kathametat | śukaḥ | asti kūṭapurābhidho grāmaḥ | tatra rājaputraḥ somarājaḥ | tasya maṇḍukā nāma patnī priyadarśanā narāntaralolupā | tāṃ caiko naraḥ kṛtasaṃketaḥ saghaṇṭako rātrau gṛhāṅgaṇe bhuṅkte | tatpatirghaṇṭāśabdaṃ śṛṇvannekadā laguḍamādāya pradhāvitaḥ ṣaṇḍaśaṅkayā | tataḥ ṣaṇḍaveṣadhārī upapatiḥ kathaṃ bhavitviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | devikā nāma sakhī maṇḍukāyāḥ patiṃ ghaṇṭāśabdānusāriṇamāgacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā jārasya naśyato ghaṇṭālālāṃ haste dhṛtvā taṃ prati jagāda | bhāvuka kāṃdiśīko vṛṣo naṣṭaḥ | tataḥ sa vyāvṛtya nijapauruṣaṃ patnyai kathayām āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau catuḥṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

p.186, l.4

(p.186, l.4)asti devi janasthānaṃ nāma pattanam | tatra nandano nāma rājā
(p.186, l.5)yathārthaḥ | tatpattane śrīvatso nāma śrāvakaḥ paraṃ maheśvararataḥ | tena
(p.186, l.6)anyadā vārāṇasīṃ nagarīṃ prati prasthitena saśiṣyena pathi gacchatā ekaḥ
(p.186, l.7)śiṣyaḥ māṃsaharaṇāya sthāpitaḥ | anyaśrāvakairdṛṣṭaḥ sa kathaṃ bhavatviti
(p.186, l.8)praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yathā sarvaśrāvakā āgatyopaviṣṭāḥ tadāṭṭahāsaṃ
(p.186, l.9)jahasuḥ | pṛṣṭaḥ sarvairjagāda | īdṛśo 'yaṃ śiṣyaḥ | mayoktaṃ māṃ saṃvartata
(p.186, l.10)abuddhyā anena māṃsasya ● ● ● ● | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.186, l.11)iti śukasaptatau pañcaṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

asti devi janasthānaṃ nāma pattanam | tatra nandano nāma rājā yathārthaḥ | tatpattane śrīvatso nāma śrāvakaḥ paraṃ maheśvararataḥ | tena anyadā vārāṇasīṃ nagarīṃ prati prasthitena saśiṣyena pathi gacchatā ekaḥ śiṣyaḥ māṃsaharaṇāya sthāpitaḥ | anyaśrāvakairdṛṣṭaḥ sa kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yathā sarvaśrāvakā āgatyopaviṣṭāḥ tadāṭṭahāsaṃ jahasuḥ | pṛṣṭaḥ sarvairjagāda | īdṛśo 'yaṃ śiṣyaḥ | mayoktaṃ māṃ saṃvartata abuddhyā anena māṃsasya ● ● ● ● | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcaṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

(p.189, l.10)iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

(p.197, l.1)tato 'rdhasnātaṃ patiṃ muktvā tathā sthitā kimuttaraṃ karotviti praśnaḥ |
(p.197, l.2)uttaram | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā jāreṇa bhuktā svapativañcanaṃ vicintyātmānaṃ
(p.197, l.3)kūpe cikṣepa | tataḥ kolāhalaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | kūpe kāpi varākī patitāstīti
(p.197, l.4)pravādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | tena tatpatistadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyacintayat | nūnaṃ
(p.197, l.5)sā matpatnī kūpe patitā bhaviṣyati | iti drutaṃ gatvāvalokayāmāsa |
(p.197, l.6)tatastāṃ kūpādākṛṣyānīyāmānayat | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā |
(p.197, l.7)iti śukasaptatau ekonasaptatitamī kathā ||

asti sthānaṃ kalāsthānaṃ nāma | tatraiko vaṇiksutaḥ | tasya bhāryā ca vejikā nāmātivallabhā | anyadā ca taṃ bhartāraṃ snāpayantī upapatiṃ pūrvakṛtasaṃketaṃ pathi gacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā nātra pānīyaṃ pracuramiti miṣāntaraṃ kṛtvā pānīyānayanavyājādgṛhānnirgatā jāreṇa sākaṃ bahukālaṃ ca sthitā | tato 'rdhasnātaṃ patiṃ muktvā tathā sthitā kimuttaraṃ karotviti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā jāreṇa bhuktā svapativañcanaṃ vicintyātmānaṃ kūpe cikṣepa | tataḥ kolāhalaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | kūpe kāpi varākī patitāstīti pravādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | tena tatpatistadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyacintayat | nūnaṃ sā matpatnī kūpe patitā bhaviṣyati | iti drutaṃ gatvāvalokayāmāsa | tatastāṃ kūpādākṛṣyānīyāmānayat | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekonasaptatitamī kathā ||

(p.197, l.8)etāvatīnāṃ kathānāṃ paryante tadbhartā madano deśāntarādāgataḥ | tasmiṃś

p.198, l.2

(p.198, l.2)paraṃ madano na śṛṇoti | upahāsya tadā caivaṃ vadati | yaḥ kaściddhitaṃ

(p.198, l.4)muhuḥ paṭhitaṃ madanaḥ śrutvā pṛcchati | tataḥ sā svayameva śaṅkitā
(p.198, l.5)kathayati |

(p.200, l.11)hatā | anena śukena tu vacanaprapañcena saptati dināni sthāpitāham |

(p.201, l.2)pṛcchati | sa āha |
