p.202, l.7

(p.202, l.7)śukaḥ kathāṃ madanāgre kathayāmāsa | asti jagatītale malayo nāma
(p.202, l.8)parvataḥ | tasya śṛṅge manoharaṃ nāma gandharvapuram | tatra madano nāma
(p.202, l.9)gandharvaḥ | tasya bhāryā ratnāvalī | tayoḥ sutā madanamañjarī | tasyā
(p.202, l.10)rūpasaṃpadaṃ dṛṣṭvā devo vā dānavo vādhomukho muhyati | na ko 'pi
(p.203, l.1)tadanurūpo varo labhyate yasya sā dīyate | athānyadā nāradaḥ samāyātaḥ |
(p.203, l.2)so 'pyasyā rūpamavalokya mūrcchitaḥ sakāmo 'bhūt | paścāllabdhasaṃjñena
(p.203, l.3)ṛṣiṇā sā śaptā |

śukaḥ kathāṃ madanāgre kathayāmāsa | asti jagatītale malayo nāma parvataḥ | tasya śṛṅge manoharaṃ nāma gandharvapuram | tatra madano nāma gandharvaḥ | tasya bhāryā ratnāvalī | tayoḥ sutā madanamañjarī | tasyā rūpasaṃpadaṃ dṛṣṭvā devo vā dānavo vādhomukho muhyati | na ko 'pi tadanurūpo varo labhyate yasya sā dīyate | athānyadā nāradaḥ samāyātaḥ | so 'pyasyā rūpamavalokya mūrcchitaḥ sakāmo 'bhūt | paścāllabdhasaṃjñena ṛṣiṇā sā śaptā |

p.203, l.4

  • (p.203, l.4)uktaṃ ca |
  • taruṇī ramaṇī ratiramyatarā pramadā sukhadā ca sadā samadā | (p.203, l.5)yadi sā subhagā hṛdaye nihitā kva jayaḥ kva ● ● ● ● ● || 70.17 (= 348) ||

uktaṃ ca |

taruṇī ramaṇī ratiramyatarā pramadā sukhadā ca sadā samadā | yadi sā subhagā hṛdaye nihitā kva jayaḥ kva ● ● ● ● ● || 70.17 (= 348) ||

p.203, l.6

(p.203, l.6)yadetasyā rūpe dṛṣṭe me smarajvaro jātaḥ tadiyaṃ śīlaviḍambanāṃ prāpsyate |
(p.203, l.7)tato rājā praṇamya prāha | svāmin prasanno bhūtvā prasādaṃ kuru |
(p.203, l.8)nārada āha | nāsyāḥ śīlakhaṇḍane doṣo bhaviṣyati na ca pativirahaḥ |
(p.203, l.9)meruparvate vipulāpurīnivāsī kanakaprabho nāma gandharvaḥ | sa
(p.203, l.10)tava putryā varo bhaviṣyati | ityuktvā nārado yayau | tato munivacanena
(p.204, l.1)tena gandharveṇa sodvāhitā | so 'nyadā tāṃ muktvā kailāsaṃ yayau |
(p.204, l.2)sāpi tadviyogārtā śilāpaṭṭe luṭhantī vastrādirahitā kenacidvidyādhareṇa
(p.204, l.3)rūpātiśayamavalokya saṃyogārthaṃ prārthitā | sā taṃ na vāñchati |
(p.204, l.4)tatastena tadbharturgandharvarūpaṃ kṛtvā sā bhuktā | tataḥ kālakrameṇa tasyā
(p.204, l.5)bhartā gṛhamāgataḥ | tāṃ suratasukhasaṃtuṣṭāmapaśyat | paropabhuktadeheyam
(p.204, l.6)iti tāṃ duṣṭāṃ matvā sāvaśyaṃ vadhyeti niścitya caṇḍikālayaṃ yayau |
(p.204, l.7)yāvattadagrato mārayati tāvadanayā phūtkṛtam | svāmini mama tvayā
(p.204, l.8)varo datto yattava gandharvacakravartī putro bhaviṣyati | tatkathaṃ putramukham
(p.204, l.9)adṛṣṭvā vipatsye | evaṃ vilapantyāstasyāḥ puratastāṃ prati devī prāha |
(p.204, l.10)he gandharvavīra nāsyāḥ ko 'pi doṣaḥ | kiṃ tu vidyādhareṇeyaṃ tvadīyarūpam
(p.204, l.11)ayena māyayā bhuktā | tato 'jānantyā asyā na doṣaḥ | anyacca
(p.204, l.12)muniśāpo vidyate | tata idaṃ saṃjātam | śāpavṛttāntaśca niveditaḥ |
(p.205, l.1)tato munivacanādiyaṃ nirdoṣā tvayā grāhyā | iti gaurīvacanaṃ śrutvā
(p.205, l.2)sa niḥśaṅkaṃ tayā saha svasthānaṃ gatastathaiva sukhito 'bhūt | tato vaṇikputra
(p.205, l.3)yadi madvacaḥ pramāṇaṃ tadaināmaduṣṭāṃ prati prasādaṃ kartumarhasi |
(p.205, l.4)iti kīravacanānmadanenānugṛhītā | tato haridatto 'pi putrāgamanatuṣṭo
(p.205, l.5)mahotsavaṃ cakāra | tasminmahotsave divyamālā patitā | taddarśane
(p.205, l.6)śukasārikātrivikramāṇāṃ śāpamokṣātsvargagamanaṃ babhūva | madano 'pi
(p.205, l.7)priyayā prabhāvatyā saha sukhāni bhuṅkte |
(p.205, l.8)iti śukasaptatiḥ samāptā ||

yadetasyā rūpe dṛṣṭe me smarajvaro jātaḥ tadiyaṃ śīlaviḍambanāṃ prāpsyate | tato rājā praṇamya prāha | svāmin prasanno bhūtvā prasādaṃ kuru | nārada āha | nāsyāḥ śīlakhaṇḍane doṣo bhaviṣyati na ca pativirahaḥ | meruparvate vipulāpurīnivāsī kanakaprabho nāma gandharvaḥ | sa tava putryā varo bhaviṣyati | ityuktvā nārado yayau | tato munivacanena tena gandharveṇa sodvāhitā | so 'nyadā tāṃ muktvā kailāsaṃ yayau | sāpi tadviyogārtā śilāpaṭṭe luṭhantī vastrādirahitā kenacidvidyādhareṇa rūpātiśayamavalokya saṃyogārthaṃ prārthitā | sā taṃ na vāñchati | tatastena tadbharturgandharvarūpaṃ kṛtvā sā bhuktā | tataḥ kālakrameṇa tasyā bhartā gṛhamāgataḥ | tāṃ suratasukhasaṃtuṣṭāmapaśyat | paropabhuktadeheyam iti tāṃ duṣṭāṃ matvā sāvaśyaṃ vadhyeti niścitya caṇḍikālayaṃ yayau | yāvattadagrato mārayati tāvadanayā phūtkṛtam | svāmini mama tvayā varo datto yattava gandharvacakravartī putro bhaviṣyati | tatkathaṃ putramukham adṛṣṭvā vipatsye | evaṃ vilapantyāstasyāḥ puratastāṃ prati devī prāha | he gandharvavīra nāsyāḥ ko 'pi doṣaḥ | kiṃ tu vidyādhareṇeyaṃ tvadīyarūpam ayena māyayā bhuktā | tato 'jānantyā asyā na doṣaḥ | anyacca muniśāpo vidyate | tata idaṃ saṃjātam | śāpavṛttāntaśca niveditaḥ | tato munivacanādiyaṃ nirdoṣā tvayā grāhyā | iti gaurīvacanaṃ śrutvā sa niḥśaṅkaṃ tayā saha svasthānaṃ gatastathaiva sukhito 'bhūt | tato vaṇikputra yadi madvacaḥ pramāṇaṃ tadaināmaduṣṭāṃ prati prasādaṃ kartumarhasi | iti kīravacanānmadanenānugṛhītā | tato haridatto 'pi putrāgamanatuṣṭo mahotsavaṃ cakāra | tasminmahotsave divyamālā patitā | taddarśane śukasārikātrivikramāṇāṃ śāpamokṣātsvargagamanaṃ babhūva | madano 'pi priyayā prabhāvatyā saha sukhāni bhuṅkte | iti śukasaptatiḥ samāptā ||
